## How to Record Personal Intros | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/10033937-how-to-record-personal-intros

How to Record Personal Intros 

How to Record Personal Intros 

Easy steps to record a 60-second intro video in one minute! 

Updated over a week ago 

Table of contents 

Step 1 

Browse Your Video Library : Log in to your Roomvu dashboard or check your content calendar . Select the video you want to enhance with a personal intro. 

Step 2 

Now click "Add Face Message" 

Step 3 

Click "Record 60 Seconds Intro" 

Step 4 

Review the Script : A relevant script will appear on your screen. You can read it as is or use it as inspiration for your own message. 

Step 6 

Hit the "Start Recording" Button : A countdown will appear. When it reaches zero, you have 60 seconds to record your message. 

Step 7 

Deliver Your Message : Share the script or speak from the heart. It's your moment to shine! 

Step 8 

Review Your Recording : 

If you're happy with it, click "Save" to add it to the beginning of your real estate video. 

Step 9 

If not, click "Retake" to record again. You can do this as many times as you need. 

How to Record a “Video Face Message” 

The “Video Face Message” . This feature allows you to add a live video overlay to your marketing videos, offering a new level of personalization and engagement. 

Follow these simple steps to create your own “Video Face Message”: 

Step 1 

Pick the Video : Choose the video you want to comment on. 

Step 2 

Click “More” : Access the advanced editing options. 

Step 3 

Click “Record Personal Intro” : Select this option to start the process. 

Step 4 

Edit the Script : Use the “Review Your Script” option to adjust the provided stats or add notes for your video. 

Step 5 

Record Your Face Message : Hit “Record Face Message” and start narrating. 

Step 6 

Save Your Recording : Once done, click “Save” to finalize your video. 

Step 7 

Retake if Necessary : Not happy with the result? Click “Retake” and record again.​ 

Setting a Default 60-Second Intro 

If you want a consistent introduction across all your videos, you can record a default 60 second intro that will automatically apply to every video you create. However, since this intro will remain the same, we recommend updating it periodically to keep your content fresh and engaging. 

To set up your default intro: 

Step 1 

On your Dashboard main page, click the gear icon in the top-right corner. 

Step 2 

From the left menu, select “Video Intro & Outro.” 

Step 3 

Click “Record Personal Intro.” 

Step 4 

Ensure your camera is working, control the video inout. 

Step 5 

You can apply effects like background blur or change the theme. 

Step 6 

A sample text will appear above the video—feel free to use it or personalize your message. 

This feature offers a quick and efficient way to brand your videos, but for maximum engagement, remember to update your intro occasionally! 

​ 

Why You Should Use Personalized Intro Videos 

Humanize Your Content : In an age where authenticity reigns supreme, showing your face adds a personal touch that static graphics can't match. Your audience will feel a genuine connection when they see and hear from you directly. 

Boost Engagement : Our data shows that agents who use the intro video feature experience a 10x increase in audience engagement . Viewers are likelier to stop scrolling and watch your content when it starts with a friendly face. 

Stand Out from the Crowd : With so much automated content out there, a personal intro sets you apart. It shows you're not just another agent—you're someone who goes the extra mile to connect. 

Time-Efficient : We know your schedule is tight. That's why we've made it possible to add a personal intro in less than a minute . Even if you post daily, that's just one minute of your time for a massive return on engagement. 

It's Incredibly Easy to Use 

We've streamlined the process so that adding a personal touch to your content is both quick and effortless. Plus, we provide a relevant script on your screen, so you don't have to think about what to say. Of course, if you prefer, you can ignore the script and share your own thoughts—the choice is entirely yours!

## Resolving Issues for Your Pending Facebook Ad | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/10201229-resolving-issues-for-your-pending-facebook-ad

Resolving Issues for Your Pending Facebook Ad 

Resolving Issues for Your Pending Facebook Ad 

Resolve connection and compliance issues to ensure your Facebook ads run smoothly with roomvu's platform. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

If your Facebook ad is currently pending, follow this guide to quickly resolve the issues and ensure your ad goes live seamlessly. 

Step 1: Connect Your Facebook Page to Roomvu 

To run ads on Facebook via Roomvu, your Facebook Page must be connected to our platform. Here's how: 

Log in to your Roomvu dashboard by clicking here . 

Click the Settings (Gear Icon) in the top-right corner. 

Navigate to the Content Calendar tab. 

Click the Connect button next to the Facebook icon. 

Follow the prompts and accept all permissions to complete the process. 

Step 2: Accept Facebook’s Terms of Service 

Before your ad can go live, Facebook requires you to accept their Terms of Service. Here’s what to do: 

Click here to access the Facebook Terms of Service. 

Use the drop-down menu in the top-left corner to select the Facebook Business Page connected to Roomvu. 

Click Accept to confirm. 

Manual Page Assignment (If Your Ad Remains Pending) 

If your Smart Ad is still pending, it may be because the Facebook Page was connected to Roomvu with a user who does not have an “Owner” or “Administrator” role. Someone with an Owner/Admin role on the page should follow these steps to fix this. After completing them, please inform Roomvu support. 

Approving Through the Facebook Page 

Visit your Facebook Page and make sure you are selecting the correct profile from the top-right corner. 

Go to Settings & Privacy > Settings . 

In the left-hand menu, select Page Setup and then Page Access . 

Scroll to the bottom of the page and accept the partner’s access request from Content Media RV . 

Shorter Way 

If you’ve selected the correct profile, click here to directly approve the partner access request. 

Alternative Method (If the Above Did Not Work) 

If the direct link doesn’t work, try this instead: 

Have the agent log in to their Facebook account and visit this URL to approve the request we sent. 

What Happens If the Issues Are Not Resolved? 

If the issues are not resolved within two weeks, Roomvu will take action to ensure your ad runs without interruption. Your ad will be moved to another account named "Real Estate Trends," maintaining your branding and campaign details.

## How to Connect Your Google My Business Account to roomvu | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/10214711-how-to-connect-your-google-my-business-account-to-roomvu

How to Connect Your Google My Business Account to roomvu | Roomvu Help Center

How to Connect Your Google My Business Account to roomvu 

How to Connect Your Google My Business Account to roomvu 

Updated over a week ago 

Table of contents 

Your Google My Business (GMB) page is one of the first places potential clients check when researching a real estate agent or mortgage broker. Keeping it active with relevant, local content showcases your expertise and builds credibility. With roomvu, connecting your GMB account is a simple process that ensures your page stays up-to-date with scheduled posts, saving you time and enhancing your professional presence. 

What Is Google My Business? 

Google My Business (GMB) is a free tool provided by Google that helps businesses manage their online presence across Google Search and Maps. It serves as a virtual storefront where businesses can showcase essential details like their address, hours of operation, contact information, and customer reviews. Additionally, businesses can share updates, photos, videos, and other relevant content to engage with potential customers. 

Why Real Estate Agents Should Use Google My Business 

GMB is an invaluable platform for real estate agents to build a strong local presence. Here's why: 

Increase Visibility : A well-maintained GMB profile ensures that your business appears in local search results when clients search for real estate agents in your area. 

Showcase Expertise : By posting regular updates, including market insights, open house announcements, or success stories, you can demonstrate your expertise and attract potential clients. 

Boost Credibility : Reviews and fresh content on your GMB page reflect professionalism and help establish client trust. 

Stay Top of Mind : Sharing relevant and engaging content frequently keeps your business visible and positions you as an active, knowledgeable agent. 

What Content Can You Share on GMB? 

Google My Business allows businesses to post a variety of content types, including: 

Updates : Share market trends, community events, or real estate tips. 

Photos and Videos : Showcase properties, virtual tours, or highlights from open houses. 

Special Announcements : Promote special deals, new services, or milestones. 

Q&A : Provide answers to common questions clients might have about your services. 

For real estate agents, sharing local and industry-relevant content on GMB is a great way to highlight your knowledge and stay engaged with your audience. 

How to Connect Your Google My Business Account to roomvu 

Here’s how you can connect your Google My Business account to roomvu in just a few steps: 

Log In to your roomvu Account 

Start by logging into your roomvu account with your credentials. 

2. Navigate to "Connect Social Media" 

On your dashboard's bottom left side, click " Connect Social Media => More." 

3. Find and Select Google My Business 

Scroll to the bottom of the menu and locate "Google My Business." Click on "Connect." 

4. Sign In to Your Google Account 

5. A new window will open. Enter the username and password for your business account on Google. 

6. If you’re already logged in to Google, select the account you want to connect. 

7. You’re All Set! 

Your Google My Business account is now connected to roomvu. roomvu will automatically schedule and post content on your behalf, ensuring your page stays active and relevant. 

Why Keeping Your GMB Page Active Matters 

First Impressions Count : Clients often start their search on GMB to verify your credibility. An empty page can raise doubts. 

Demonstrate Expertise : Sharing local, insightful content showcases your knowledge and informs your audience. 

Build Trust : Regular updates help establish you as an active and reliable professional in your industry. 

Integrating your Google My Business account with roomvu saves time and ensures your online presence remains polished and professional. Today, connect your account and start reaping the benefits of automated, consistent posts! 

Stay active. Stay credible with roomvu .

## How to Set up and Optimize Google My Business | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/10222279-how-to-set-up-and-optimize-google-my-business

How to Set up and Optimize Google My Business | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content

How to Set up and Optimize Google My Business 

How to Set up and Optimize Google My Business 

Learn how to create a Google My Business Account for Your Real Estate Business 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Google My Business makes your business appear in the upper right-hand corner for searches relevant to your business. Moreover, it is free and offers you more exposure. Having Google My Business for your business as an agent will help you be discovered by leads easily. Furthermore, it is more than just an entry in a listing of businesses. It provides a convenient way to interact with potential clients and prospects on Google and Google Maps. 

​ 

In this article, we will examine Google My Business, its features, and the benefits it provides. We will then discuss how to create a profile or claim an existing one, and finally, we will go through the steps to optimize it for your business. 

How to Set up a Google My Business 

Setting up your profile on Google My Business is pretty simple. It will take only a few minutes. 

​ 

To get started, you need a Google account. You might be tempted to use your own personal Google account, but we recommend that you use another email address. One that you don’t mind sharing with clients and employees. Once created, sign in to that account and: 

​ 

Step 1: Visit Google My Business 

Go to google.com/business and click " Manage now " in the top right corner. 

Step 2: Enter the name for your business. 

On the next page, enter a name for your business. 

​ 

Step 3: Choose your business category. 

Be sure to select all that are relevant to your business. “Real estate agents” and “Real estate consultant” apply to all agents. 

Step 4: Add a location for your business. 

If you do not have a business office and would rather have a home address, select no in the next step. This will make the verification process much easier. 

Step 5: Add your working address 

In the next step, add one or more addresses where you usually work and meet clients. 

Step 6: Provide contact information. 

Provide your phone number and select the option you would like to be contacted by. 

Step 7: Add your mailing address 

Step 8: Choose a way to verify Your business. 

To fully manage and represent this business on Google, you must confirm it's yours. Google will send a postcard with a unique verification code to the address within a few days. You will need this code to verify that the business is yours. Some other businesses can verify through text, call, email, or Google Search Console. Click on later. However, if you did not add a physical address in the first few steps, you can easily verify by phone. 

Simply enter the code that is sent to your phone to verify. 

Step 9: Add your services. 

Continuing with your profile setup, add the services you offer. 

Step 10: Add your business hours. 

According to Google, "96% of customers are more likely to visit a business that has hours of operation on a Google Search/Maps results page." 

Step 11: Add a business description. 

Let customers find out more about your business. Make sure you describe your business well and state: 

Who you serve; 

What you offer; 

And what clients will get out of doing business with you. 

You can also define how long you have been in this business on this page. 

Step 12: Add photos of your business. 

Ensure the images you choose are high-quality and demonstrate the purpose of your business. 

Step 13: Manage your business in your dashboard. 

Now, you can head to your dashboard and manage your business. The dashboard also has many other features, like insights, that will greatly help your business by showing you who is getting connected to you. Some of these features cannot be unlocked unless your business is verified, but others, like your free website, can be set up easily. 

What is Google My Business 

Google My Business is a popular service that is shown in Google's search results, including Google Maps. When you search for a name on Google or Google Maps, if they have set up their Google My Business, it will show up in search results. Once set up and used correctly, it is a powerful way for REALTORS® to increase their visibility in Google searches and offer accurate information to anyone looking for you. 

It is the equivalent of the yellow pages from the past. In "the old days," whenever someone needed a service, they would go through the yellow pages to find the professional they needed. 

In modern times, services are found on platforms. Google My Business is one of the most practical and popular ones. It is just waiting for you to use it for your business. 

Google My Business: 

Costs $0 

Delivers a high ROI. 

Takes a short time to set up. 

Has great potential for turning your business into a successful one. 

How Google My Business Works 

When anyone searches for your name on Google, Google will show your listing in a special box on the right side of the results: 

On a mobile device, it will appear on top of the results: 

Similarly, when someone searches for something like "real estate agent Manhattan" or "top REALTORS® in Houston", Google My Business may show the result on Google Maps, marking the local businesses in the area or city you have searched for, which can be clicked on to see separate business profiles. 

Why Real Estate Agents Should Set up Their Profile on Google My Business 

There are many reasons why real estate agents should be on Google My Business. If you have not done it yet, read the following: 

It is a Business Profile 

Google My Business is your own professional space on Google where you can showcase photos of your work and other offers. It can convince your prospects to trust your business and engage. 

It Makes You Easier to Reach 

What is the ultimate goal behind any business? Do more business, right? Well, Google My Business makes your business easier to reach and connect. Your profile will offer your contact information, address, website, social media profile, etc. So, your prospects can contact you easily right from the search results screen, either through calls or messages. No hassle. 

It Provides Social Proof 

One of the best ways any business can attract more customers and clients is social proof. This is where others who have used your business leave reviews and thoughts on how they liked using your products and services. When people search for a keyword for which your name comes up, they can read the reviews others have left you. From there, they can decide if you are a good fit for their needs. If you have received enough good reviews, your business will be helped dramatically. After all, people trust others more than they trust you and what you say about your business. 

It Shows How Many People Are Connecting with You on Google 

Google My Business for REALTORS® lets you see clicks, calls, bookings, follows, etc., with your business profile. With this, you can analyze engagement. Also, you can see who is connecting with your business. 

Can All Real Estate Agents Have Their Own Profile on Google My Business 

All REALTORS® who own their business can have their profile on Google My Business even if their brokerage already has one. However, you are not eligible to create a profile for apartments you have to rent. You can have a look at Google's guidelines . 

How to Optimize Your Google My Business for REALTORS® Profile 

Once you have created a Google My Business profile for your real estate business now its time to optimize and provide as much information as possible to tell Google everything it needs about your business so that when people search for your name or other relevant keywords that apply to your business, Google can show maximum info about you. 

Ask Your Clients to Leave Reviews and Reply to Them 

If you have some very happy clients among others, you can ask them to leave reviews for you. Look on your dashboard for “Get more reviews” and share the link it provides with past clients. These reviews will be shown to others who see your profile once searching on Google. This kind of social proof works very well for those who do not know you or are unsure if you fit their needs and business well. 

Tip: Do not try to get a lot of reviews in a short time as that will come across as spam to Google. Make sure you get a steady flow of natural reviews. If your profile is new ask for reviews gradually. It is best if you get reviews as you go along by gradually asking your past clients to leave reviews. Keep it fair and natural and avoid trying too hard to make things happened quickly. 

If you are claiming an existing profile, you may have received some reviews already. One of the greatest ways to show others that your business is an active and real one is to reply to these reviews. Bear in mind that you are not just replying to the clients who have used your services before. These reviews and your replies will be shown to your prospects too who are evaluating your worth by reading through the lines to find clues if you are the one or not. 

Add Photos and Videos Related to Your Business 

According to Google , businesses with photos receive 42% more requests for directions and 35% more clicks through their website. Make sure you add photos and videos that: 

Represent your business. For example photos and videos of you working with clients. 

Show your For Sale, Sold, Open House signs 

Are taken recently. 

Are high-quality. 

Keep it Up to Date! 

The most important thing we think you should get from this article is the fact that with Google My Business you can't just create it and forget it. A lot of other agents are using it for their business and in order to stand out and appear in search results first, you need to keep it up to date with images and videos and make sure you get a steady flow of reviews. Bad reviews are not going to help your business. Consistent management of your profile will result in ranking higher on SERP and ultimately more free traffic without spending a dollar. 

Google My Business for REALTORS®: Final Words 

Google My Business matters a lot for REALTORS® for many reasons. First off, it is free, and you don’t need to spend even a dollar to get it running. Also, it takes no time to set up and will only take a few minutes of your daily time to monitor and add to it. However, the most important thing about it is that it focuses on local searches and can be a great tool for introducing you to local prospects looking for your business. Just make sure you get great reviews and keep it updated every week.

How to Create a TikTok Account for Real Estate 

How to Connect Your Google My Business Account to roomvu 

How to Get More Google Reviews for Your Business 

How to Find and Share Your Google Business Review Link 

How to Add Your Social Media Links to Google My Business and Facebook

## roomvu’s Integration with Constant Contact Email Marketing | Roomvu Help Center

roomvu’s Integration with Constant Contact Email Marketing 

roomvu’s Integration with Constant Contact Email Marketing 

Discover how Roomvu's Constant Contact integration enhances email deliverability for Platinum and Diamond users, saving time and money. 

Updated over a week ago 

Table of contents 

Overview of the Integration 

Roomvu is excited to announce the integration of Constant Contact into our platform! Constant Contact, a trusted leader in email marketing for over a decade, ensures that emails sent via Roomvu are delivered directly to recipients' inboxes—not their spam folders. This feature is now available to all users on the Platinum (Brand Builder) and Diamond packages, with Roomvu covering the costs of a Constant Contact plan worth $80 ($CAD 110). 

Why This Integration Matters 

Sending emails has become increasingly complex, with strict rules to avoid spam filters. With Constant Contact, Roomvu users can: 

Improve Deliverability : Avoid spam traps and ensure emails land in the intended inboxes. 

Eliminate Warm-Up Hassles : There is no need to send emails to “warm up” recipients gradually. 

Simplify Email Management : Roomvu handles everything from email delivery to tracking open rates and engagement. 

$80 Value 

By integrating Constant Contact into Roomvu, agents on the Platinum and Diamond packages receive a $80 ($CAD 110) plan at no additional cost. This means Roomvu is improving your email marketing performance and saving you the expense of purchasing this service independently. Over a year, this adds up to nearly $960 in savings —an incredible value that allows you to focus on growing your business without worrying about extra costs. 

Key Benefits for Roomvu Users 

Fully Managed Email Delivery : Roomvu manages everything related to Constant Contact, so users don’t need to worry about setup or maintenance. 

Generous Contact Limit : Roomvu provides a Constant Contact plan that allows users to send emails to up to 3,000 contacts . 

For users with more than 3,000 contacts, Roomvu supports the first 3,000 via Constant Contact, and the rest through Roomvu’s email engine. 

Enhanced Performance : Constant Contact ensures higher open rates and better inbox placement. 

Cost Savings : Roomvu covers the cost of the Constant Contact plan for Platinum and Diamond users. 

Seamless Integration : No separate Constant Contact account is required; everything is managed through Roomvu. 

What You Get with This Feature 

A fully paid Constant Contact plan for eligible Roomvu users. 

The ability to send professional emails to up to 3,000 contacts . 

Improved email deliverability and engagement metrics. 

Comprehensive email performance tracking, including open rates and click-through statistics. 

How It Works 

For New Roomvu Users : 

The Constant Contact integration is automatically activated for Platinum and Diamond package users. 

There is no setup required; Roomvu handles everything. 

For Existing Constant Contact Users : 

If you already have a Constant Contact account, Roomvu can integrate it with our platform. 

You can export your existing contacts, import them into Roomvu, and cancel your standalone Constant Contact subscription. 

Email Delivery and Management : 

Roomvu takes care of managing contacts, crafting engaging content, and tracking performance. 

Constant Contact’s role is solely to deliver the emails reliably. 

Why Roomvu + Constant Contact is a Perfect Match 

This integration combines Roomvu’s expertise in creating engaging content with Constant Contact’s industry-leading email deliverability. Together, we ensure your email marketing campaigns are: 

Visually stunning and highly engaging. 

Delivered straight to your recipients’ inboxes. 

Easy to track, manage, and optimize. 

Frequently Asked Questions (FAQ) 

1. Who is eligible for the Constant Contact integration? This feature is available to all Roomvu users on the Platinum (Brand Builder) and Diamond packages. 

2. Do I need to set up a Constant Contact account? No. Roomvu manages everything related to Constant Contact. You do not need a separate account. 

3. What if I already have a Constant Contact account? If you already have a Constant Contact account, contact Roomvu support to integrate it. Once your contacts are imported into Roomvu, you can cancel your standalone Constant Contact subscription. 

4. How many contacts can I send emails to? The Constant Contact plan provided by Roomvu allows you to send emails to up to 3,000 contacts . 

5. Will Constant Contact show me who opened my emails? Yes! Roomvu provides detailed analytics, including open rates, click-through rates, and more. 

6. What happens if I exceed the 3,000-contact limit? roomvu only sends emails to the first 300 contacts. 

7. Do I need to warm up my recipients with Constant Contact? No. Constant Contact eliminates the need for gradual email sending, ensuring your emails avoid spam filters from the start. 

8. What does Roomvu manage, and what does Constant Contact manage? Roomvu handles everything except email delivery, which Constant Contact manages. This includes creating content, tracking email performance, and managing your contacts. 

9. Does this integration cost extra? No. Roomvu covers the full cost of the Constant Contact plan for Platinum and Diamond users. 

10. Can I track email engagement metrics? Absolutely! Roomvu provides comprehensive insights, including who opened your emails, clicked links, and more. 

For additional questions or assistance, please contact Roomvu Support.

## How to Resolve Copyright Issues on Social Media Content | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/10305651-how-to-resolve-copyright-issues-on-social-media-content

How to Resolve Copyright Issues on Social Media Content | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English

All Collections 

Social media 

How to Resolve Copyright Issues on Social Media Content 

How to Resolve Copyright Issues on Social Media Content 

A step-by-step guide to resolving copyright claims on Instagram and YouTube 

December 23, 2024 

Table of contents 

If you encounter copyright claims on the content we share for you on Instagram or YouTube, follow the steps below to resolve them quickly. 

Resolving Copyright Claims on Instagram 

When Instagram blocks your video due to a copyright issue, you can appeal the claim to have the content restored. Follow these steps: 

Check Notifications : Open your Instagram app and navigate to your notifications. 

Find the Blocked Video Notification : Look for the notification indicating that your video has been blocked. 

Click on Appeal : Scroll down within the notification and tap the "Appeal" option. 

Agree to Terms : Check the box labeled "I Agree." 

Enter Your Name : Input your name as your signature to confirm the appeal. 

Submit Appeal : Tap the "Appeal" button. 

Your video will typically be restored within a few hours. 

​ 

Resolving Copyright Claims on YouTube 

If you receive a copyright claim on YouTube, here’s how you can dispute it: 

Visit YouTube Studio : Go to YouTube Studio and access the Content tab. 

Find the Affected Video : Use the "Copyright Claims" filter to locate the video. 

See the Claim Details : Hover over the claimed video and click on "See Details." 

Dispute the Claim : Click on "Actions" and select "Dispute." 

Select the Reason for Dispute : 

Check the box labeled "My dispute isn’t based on any of the reasons above. I would still like to dispute this Content ID claim." 

Click "Continue" and select "License" as the reason. 

Provide the License : In the Review Requirements section: 

Copy and paste the details from your license certificate. 

Check all the required boxes and submit. 

The claim should be resolved shortly after submission. 

Resolving Copyright Claims on Facebook 

Steps to Dispute a Facebook Copyright Claim: 

Visit Your Facebook Profile 

Open Facebook on your phone and tap your profile photo. 

Find the Support Inbox 

Scroll down on your profile to find Help & Support at the bottom. 

Tap Support Inbox to open it. 

Locate the Video in Question 

In your Support Inbox messages, find the copyright claim notification. 

Tap Continue at the bottom to proceed. 

Submit Dispute 

You will see a list of options for how to handle the claim. 

Select Submit Dispute and then tap Continue . 

Select the Reason 

If you have explicit permission or a license, choose Licensed Content . 

Otherwise, choose Other if you believe you’re allowed to use the content under fair use or a similar reason. 

Tap Submit to confirm. 

Add Additional Details 

Provide a clear explanation (20+ characters) about why you’re disputing. 

For example, state that the platform you sourced the content from (e.g., Pixabay) permits its use under their licensing terms. 

Tap Submit once you’ve added your details. 

By following these steps, you can effectively address copyright issues and ensure your content remains visible on social media platforms. For further assistance, feel free to reach out to our support team.

## roomvu Smart Ads | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/10421260-roomvu-smart-ads

roomvu Smart Ads | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Features 

roomvu Smart Ads 

roomvu Smart Ads 

What is roomvu Smart Ads and how you can use them. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Real estate ads are used to spread the word about REALTORS and the service they provide. On the other hand, they can be used to promote homes they are trying to sell. According to HubSpot effective ads should: 

Be targeted to a specific audience 

Audience quality is far more important than size because when running ads on Facebook your goal is engagement or conversion. Casting a wide net to a target audience that is not interested in your service will ruin your chances of getting results or insights. Luckily Facebook offers a wide range of targeting criteria including demographics, interests, location, and even behavior. 

Be relevant 

You are practically waiting for money when showing ads that are not relevant to your target audience. The more your ad content, copy, and landing page are relevant the more Facebook will favor your ads and the better results await you. 

Be visual 

Facebook algorithms favor visual content for a reason. They are more likely to gain attention, be remembered, or get shared. Videos are even better in terms of engagement and conversion. However, make sure the content you use is appealing and resonates to the need of your target audience. 

Have a clear call to action. 

The CTA you use in your ads is one of the most important steps in your ad campaign. Do it wrong and your ads will fail regardless of how carefully other parts are done. Add some sense of urgency to your viewer as it should encourage people to click on your ad NOW. 

That is why we in roomvu offer smart ads for real estate that primarily focus on relevant videos that include a value proposition to encourage action through a clear CTA. Optimized ads like roomvu Smart Ads for Real Estate can help you spend your PPC budget wisely and see a positive return on your investment . 

With roomvu Smart Ads for Real Estate, you can reach leads you otherwise would never have had the opportunity to meet. According to inman: 

“(Roomvu Smart Ads) capabilities include video landing pages with call-to-action forms that users can link to the associated ads to capture personal information from renters, buyers, and sellers.” 

Multi-Language Support on roomvu Smart Ads 

What’s better than talking to your audience in English? Talking to them in their native language! We know some of your audience may not be native speakers of English. Talking to them in their native language will build trust and gain their attention! 

How to Create and Manage Facebook & Instagram Ads in Roomvu 

Follow these steps to easily create and manage your Facebook and Instagram ads using Roomvu: 

Step 1: Navigate to FB & IG Ads 

On the left-hand menu, click FB & IG Ads . 

Step 2: Choose Your Ad Type 

Select the type of ad you want to create from the available options (e.g., Buyer Ads, Seller Ads) and Click Preview & Run. 

Step 3: Review and Edit Ad Details 

In the opened window, review the provided information. You can change the language or the style of the ad too. Ensure your personal details are up-to-date. 

Step 4: Set Your Ad’s Reach 

Choose the distance radius to define the geographical area your ad will target. 

Step 5: Confirm and Pay 

When everything is set, click Proceed to Payment. 

Select or add your credit card. 

Click Confirm Purchase. 

Additional Tips 

If you’re unsure about any settings, you can always go with the default values. 

For further assistance, feel free to contact our support team.

## How to Use The Video Face Message Feature | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/10449507-how-to-use-the-video-face-message-feature

How to Use The Video Face Message Feature | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles...

Features 

How to Use The Video Face Message Feature 

How to Use The Video Face Message Feature 

How to narrate over a video and add your comments to it. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Engage Like Never Before with Personalized Video Face Messages 

We’re excited to announce a game-changing feature for real estate agents and mortgage brokers: the "Video Face Message" . This feature allows you to add a live video overlay to your marketing videos, offering a new level of personalization and engagement. 

Previously, with our "Personalized Intro Video" feature, you could add a short introductory video at the beginning of your content, offering a personal touch and narrative. Now, with the "Video Face Message" feature, you can go beyond intros by adding a circle overlay video that appears throughout your shared video. This opens up a world of possibilities for agents and brokers to share insights, narrate content, and provide deeper commentary. 

How Does the "Video Face Message" Work? 

This feature allows you to overlay a small, circular video of yourself onto the main video, making it more interactive and engaging. Here’s what makes it unique: 

Full-Length Commentary : Unlike the short intros of the "Personalized Intro Video," the "Video Face Message" covers the entire video duration, letting you narrate and add insights. 

Dynamic Personalization : You can share market stats, property highlights, or expert commentary while your audience views the main video. 

Customizable Placement : Move the video overlay to different positions on the screen to suit your content. 

Things to Keep in Mind 

To make the most of this feature, here’s what you need to know: 

Prepare for a Longer Narrative : You must speak for the entire video. Prepare your talking points in advance. 

No Full Scripts Provided : While we’ll offer key stats and guidelines, you must craft your narrative to suit the video. 

Engagement Requires Effort : Unlike shorter intros, this feature requires more planning to create a professional and compelling message. 

How to Record a "Video Face Message" 

On your content calendar , click the video you would like to add a face message to and then click "Add Face Message" 

Edit the Script : Use the "Review Your Script" option to adjust the provided stats or add notes for your video. 

You will have two options. On the Record Face Message option, click "Record" 

Start recording, read the script. 

​ 

Save Your Recording : Once done, click "Save" to finalize your video. 

Retake if Necessary : Not happy with the result? Click "Retake" and record again. 

Why Use the "Video Face Message" Feature? 

Adding your commentary directly to your videos enhances their engagement and credibility. Your face on the video builds trust, while your voiceover connects with the audience personally. By preparing a longer, insightful message, you can increase viewer retention and position yourself as an expert in your field. 

Ready to Get Started? 

Transform your marketing with "Video Face Messages." Prepare your script, position your overlay, and start recording to deliver professional and engaging videos today!

How to Log Out of Your roomvu Account 

Learn how you can log out of your roomvu account from the settings. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Logging out of your roomvu account is simple and can be done in just a few steps. Follow the guide below: 

Access the Settings: 

On the main dashboard of your Roomvu account, locate the Settings option (represented by a gear icon) in the top-right corner of the page. 

Click on the gear icon to open the Settings menu . 

Navigate to "Log Out": 

On the new page, look at the menu on the left-hand side. 

Scroll down the menu until you see the "Log Out" option.

Once you click "Log Out," you will be logged out of your account.

How to Connect Your LinkedIn Account to Roomvu 

How to Connect Your LinkedIn Account to Roomvu 

Learn how to connect your LinkedIn personal or business account to roomvu 

Updated over a week ago 

Follow these simple steps to connect your LinkedIn account to Roomvu and start automating your social media content: 

Step 1: Log In to Your Roomvu Account 

• Visit roomvu.com and log in to your account. 

Step 2: Locate LinkedIn in the Dashboard 

• On the main page of your dashboard , find the LinkedIn option at the bottom-left corner. Alternatively, go the to social media connection page . 

• Click the toggle switch next to LinkedIn. 

Step 3: Sign In to LinkedIn 

• You will be redirected to LinkedIn. 

• If you are not already signed in to LinkedIn, the login page will appear. 

• Enter your LinkedIn username and password to continue. 

Step 4: Select Your LinkedIn Account 

• Once logged in, you will see a page to choose the LinkedIn account you want to connect. 

• If you manage a business or company page on LinkedIn, you can select it here. 

Important: You must be a Super Admin or Content Admin on LinkedIn to connect your account to Roomvu. 

Step 5: Save the Connection 

• After selecting your account, click Save . 

• Your LinkedIn account is now connected to Roomvu! 

You’re all set! Roomvu will now help you create and share engaging real estate content seamlessly on LinkedIn.

How to Connect YouTube to roomvu 

Connect your YouTube account to roomvu using your Google account 

Updated over a week ago 

Table of contents 

Follow these simple steps to connect your YouTube account to roomvu and start sharing your content seamlessly. 

Step 1: Prepare Your Google Account 

Since your YouTube account is tied to your Google account, we recommend using Google Chrome and logging in to the Google account associated with the YouTube account you want to connect. 

Step 2: Log in to Your Roomvu Account 

1. Log in to your roomvu account. 

2. On your dashboard, locate the “More” button at the lower-left corner of the screen to open the social media connection page . 

3. Click on “More” and a new menu will appear. 

Step 3: Connect YouTube 

1. In the opened menu, find the “YouTube” option. 

2. Click on “Connect.” 

Step 4: Log in to Your Google Account 

• A Google login page will appear. 

• Select the Google account you want to connect to roomvu. 

Note: If you’re not using Google Chrome or are not logged in to your Google account, you will be prompted to enter your Google account email and password manually. 

Step 5: Complete the Connection 

After selecting or logging into your Google account, your YouTube account will be successfully connected to roomvu. 

You’re all set! You can now share videos directly from roomvu to your YouTube channel effortlessly.

roomvu Referral Program: Empower Your Network and Reap Rewards 

roomvu Referral Program: Empower Your Network and Reap Rewards 

Learn how the roomvu Referral Program works, how to refer friends, and earn rewards while helping fellow real estate professionals. 

March 8, 2026 

Table of contents 

Are you a satisfied roomvu subscriber looking to share the platform with your network and earn rewards? Our Referral Program allows you to introduce fellow real estate professionals to roomvu while earning a reward when they join. 

By referring colleagues, you help them improve their marketing while also benefiting financially. It is a simple way to support your peers while growing your own network. 

Why Participate? 

By participating in the roomvu Referral Program, you are not only earning rewards. You are helping grow a community of successful real estate professionals using better marketing tools. 

Support Your Peers 

Help fellow realtors and mortgage brokers discover roomvu and improve their marketing strategies with automated, hyper-local content. 

Strengthen Professional Relationships 

Sharing valuable tools with colleagues can deepen your professional connections and open doors for future collaboration. 

Enjoy Mutual Benefits 

Your referrals gain access to powerful marketing tools while you receive a financial reward for introducing them. 

How the Referral Program Works 

Earn 10% Cash Reward 

When you refer a friend to roomvu, you receive 10% of their first one-time purchase . 

Example 

If your referral purchases the Brand Builder plan for $1,800 per year , you receive $180 . 

Give Your Friends a Discount 

Your referrals may receive 10% off their purchase , making it easier for them to get started with roomvu. 

Unlock More Rewards 

If you refer more than 10 friends within a year , roomvu can create a personalized referral link for you. This link helps simplify sharing roomvu and makes tracking your referrals easier. 

Important Referral Rules 

To ensure fairness and proper tracking, the following conditions apply: 

• Referral rewards apply only to the first one-time purchase made by the referred user. 

• Referral rewards are void if any discount is applied during the purchase . 

• Referral rewards cannot be combined with other promotions, discounts, or coupons . 

• If either party uses a discount , the referral reward will not apply . 

• The referred user must be new to roomvu . 

• You must notify roomvu before the referral completes their purchase . 

• The program is available only to existing subscribers with paid individual accounts . Enterprise accounts are excluded. 

How to Submit a Referral 

Before your referral completes their purchase, please notify our team. 

Send an email to info@roomvu.com with: 

• Your name 

• Your referral’s name 

• Your referral’s contact information 

Once the purchase is confirmed and meets the referral program requirements, your 10% cash reward will be processed . 

Success Story 

One roomvu user in Toronto referred several colleagues to the platform. After those colleagues subscribed, the agent earned approximately $300 in referral rewards , while their referrals gained access to roomvu’s automated marketing tools. 

It is a simple example of how the program benefits everyone involved. 

Tips for Successful Referrals 

Share Your Experience 

Tell colleagues how roomvu has improved your marketing, visibility, or client engagement. 

Use Social Media 

Share your experience with roomvu on LinkedIn, Facebook, or Instagram to reach a wider audience. 

Demonstrate the Platform 

Hosting a casual meetup or short webinar can help colleagues see how roomvu works in practice. 

Offer Guidance 

Helping someone through the sign-up process can make them more confident about joining. 

The Benefits of roomvu 

roomvu helps real estate professionals grow their online presence through: 

• Automated social media posting 

• Hyper-local real estate video content 

• Custom branding and marketing tools 

• Consistent content that keeps you visible to your audience 

• An easy-to-use platform designed for busy professionals 

Questions? 

If you have questions about the Referral Program, contact us at:

How to Enroll in roomvu’s New Agent Program and Get 50% Off 

Learn how new real estate agents can enroll in roomvu’s New Agent Program and get 50% off their first year of marketing services. 

February 24, 2025 

Overview 

Starting a real estate career can be both exciting and challenging, especially in the first year. To help new agents establish their brand and grow their business, roomvu has launched the New Agent Program , offering 50% off on our Social Starter and Omni Presence packages. This guide will walk you through eligibility, enrollment, and how to take full advantage of this offer. 

What is roomvu’s New Agent Program? 

Roomvu’s New Agent Program is designed to help new Realtors build a strong online presence and generate leads effectively. With a 50% discount , you get access to powerful marketing tools at a significantly reduced cost, making it easier to market yourself and your listings. 

Who is Eligible? 

To qualify for this program, you must meet the following criteria: 

✅ You are a newly licensed real estate agent. 

✅ You are purchasing roomvu services for the first time. 

✅ You can provide proof of entry into the real estate industry (e.g., real estate license or certification). 

How to Enroll 

Follow these simple steps to take advantage of this offer: 

1️⃣ Provide Proof of Entry 

Submit a valid real estate license, certification, or any official document proving your recent entry into the industry. 

2️⃣ Book a Demo with Our Team 

Schedule a session where our experts will walk you through the Social Starter and Omni Presence packages, demonstrating how they can benefit your business. 

3️⃣ Get Compliance Approval 

Our team will verify your credentials, and once approved, you will receive a one-time 50% discount on your selected package. 

Why Choose roomvu? 

🚀 Boost Your Online Presence – Stand out in a crowded market with automated marketing tools. 

🎯 Generate Quality Leads – Connect with potential clients effortlessly through targeted content. 

💡 Save Time & Resources – Let us handle your marketing while you focus on closing deals. 

📈 Stay Ahead of the Competition – Access cutting-edge marketing strategies tailored for real estate professionals. 

Terms and Conditions 

• The 50% discount applies only to the Social Starter and Omni Presence Yearly packages. 

• This is a one-time discount valid for the first year. 

• Cannot be combined with other promotions or retroactively applied to past purchases. 

• Proof of entry into the real estate industry is required. 

Ready to Get Started? 

💬 Contact Us Today to send your credentials and schedule a demo. 

📅 Secure Your Spot – Take advantage of this limited-time offer and jumpstart your real estate career! 

👉 Book a Demo Now

## How Can I Nurture and Follow Up with My Real Estate Leads Automatically? | Roomvu Help Center

How Can I Nurture and Follow Up with My Real Estate Leads Automatically? 

How Can I Nurture and Follow Up with My Real Estate Leads Automatically? 

Learn how Roomvu Engage in the Agency Package (Diamond) automates lead follow-ups, nurtures prospects, and books appointments for agents. 

March 12, 2025 

Table of contents 

Never Let a Lead Go Cold Again with Roomvu Engage 

As a real estate professional, keeping up with leads can be overwhelming. Manually calling, emailing, and following up takes time—time that could be better spent closing deals. If you’ve ever wondered how to nurture your leads automatically and increase your appointment bookings , Roomvu Engage , available in our Agency Package (Diamond) , is the solution. 

What is Roomvu Engage? 

Roomvu Engage is an AI-powered lead engagement system designed to follow up with, nurture, and convert your leads— without you lifting a finger . It instantly connects with new leads, provides consistent follow-ups, and even schedules appointments for you. 

​ 

How Can I Automatically Follow Up with My Leads? 

Roomvu Engage takes care of the follow-up process from start to finish. Here’s how it works: 

✅ Instant Lead Calls – Every new lead gets an immediate call to establish a connection before they lose interest. 

​ 

​ 

✅ AI-Powered SMS & Email Updates – Leads receive automated messages with property insights, market updates, and personalized videos to keep them engaged. 

​ 

​ 

✅ Persistent Follow-Ups – The system ensures leads don’t slip away by making multiple follow-up attempts. 

✅ Human Scheduler for Hot Leads – Once a lead is engaged, a human scheduler books the appointment for you. 

✅ Done-For-You Appointment Scheduling – You only step in when the lead is ready to buy or sell. 

Note: roomvu will follow up with leads generated through roomvu tools and landing pages. However, if you’ve uploaded leads from an external source to your roomvu dashboard, we may not have their consent for follow-ups via calls. 

Why is Automated Lead Follow-Up Important? 

🏡 Faster Response Times – Leads expect quick responses, and Roomvu Engage ensures you never miss an opportunity. 

📈 Higher Conversion Rates – Consistent, automated follow-ups keep leads engaged and move them closer to a decision. 

⏳ More Time for Selling – No more spending hours chasing leads—focus on closing deals instead. 

📅 More Appointments, Less Effort – Only speak with high-quality, ready-to-convert leads. 

Who Can Benefit from Roomvu Engage? 

✔ Real estate agents who want to automate their follow-ups and increase sales. 

✔ Brokerages looking to boost lead conversion rates and streamline agent workflows. 

✔ Busy professionals who don’t have time for manual lead tracking and follow-ups. 

Where Can I Get Roomvu Engage? 

Roomvu Engage is exclusively available in our Agency Package (Diamond) . If you’re looking for a complete lead engagement and marketing solution , this package provides the most advanced automation tools to grow your real estate business. 

How Do I Get Started? 

1️⃣ Sign up for Roomvu’s Agency Package (Diamond) . 

2️⃣ Connect your lead sources (website, CRM, social media, etc.). 

3️⃣ Let Roomvu Engage handle the follow-ups. 

4️⃣ Step in only when it’s time to close the deal! 

Ready to Automate Your Lead Nurturing? 

Stop letting valuable leads go cold. Upgrade to the Agency Package (Diamond) today and start converting more leads into real estate deals—effortlessly.

How to Co-Brand Listings with Real Estate Agents as a Loan Officer 

How to Co-Brand Listings with Real Estate Agents as a Loan Officer 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Roomvu now offers a seamless and fully automated co-branding solution for loan officers and mortgage brokers . For the first time, mortgage professionals can legally partner with real estate agents to co-brand property listings , expanding their visibility and enhancing lead generation. 

This article explains how the co-branding process works , who can participate, and why it is a valuable marketing opportunity. 

How It Works 

In order to get this feature: 

1. Get Agent Consent 

All real estate agents need to do is have a free account with roomvu and opt in and provide consent to have their listings co-branded with a loan officer’s information. This ensures compliance and a mutually beneficial partnership. 

2. Mortgage Broker Joins Roomvu 

To participate, loan officers and mortgage brokers must have a paid Roomvu account . This unlocks exclusive marketing tools that allow for seamless cross-promotion with real estate agents. 

3. Automated Co-Branded Promotions 

Once an agent has opted in, Roomvu automatically co-brands the listing with the loan officer’s details. The listings are then published across social media and digital platforms , maximizing exposure for both the real estate agent and the loan officer. 

​ 

Benefits of Co-Branding Listings 

Increased Exposure and Lead Generation 

Co-branded listings benefit from the combined reach of both the agent and the loan officer , ensuring greater visibility and more qualified leads . 

Effortless Automation 

Roomvu’s system handles the entire process —from creating the co-branded content to distributing it across digital platforms—eliminating the need for manual work. 

Regulatory Compliance 

Unlike traditional marketing methods, Roomvu’s co-branding feature is designed to meet compliance standards , allowing mortgage professionals to legally promote listings alongside real estate agents. 

Stronger Industry Presence 

By associating with top-performing real estate agents , loan officers can build credibility, increase brand recognition, and establish themselves as trusted mortgage experts . 

Who Can Benefit from Co-Branding? 

• Real estate agents looking for additional marketing support to increase listing visibility 

• Loan officers and mortgage brokers who want to engage more homebuyers and position themselves as industry leaders 

• Brokerages and real estate teams seeking an automated, compliant marketing solution 

How to Get Started 

1. Sign up for a Roomvu account if you are a loan officer or mortgage broker. 

2. Go to your listings menu 

3. Turn on Cobranded listings and let roomvu handle the automation , ensuring your branding appears on every co-branded listing. 

Start Co-Branding Today 

This exclusive feature allows loan officers and real estate agents to collaborate effortlessly, increase their marketing reach, and generate more leads . If you are a mortgage professional, sign up for Roomvu today and start co-branding with top real estate agents in your area.

## How to Merge Followers from Multiple Instagram Accounts to Grow Your Business Account Followers | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/10729701-how-to-merge-followers-from-multiple-instagram-accounts-to-grow-your-business-account-followers

All Collections

How to Merge Followers from Multiple Instagram Accounts to Grow Your Business Account Followers 

How to Merge Followers from Multiple Instagram Accounts to Grow Your Business Account Followers 

March 7, 2025 

Table of contents 

If you have multiple Instagram accounts—such as a personal account, an old account, or a second business profile—you can merge their followers into your main business account. The best way to do this is by sending follow requests to the followers of your other accounts. Here’s how: 

Steps to Merge Followers from Multiple Accounts 

1. Switch to Your Main Business Account: 

• Open the Instagram app. 

• Tap on your profile icon at the bottom right. 

• If you’re logged into a different account, tap your username at the top and select your main business account. 

2. Find Followers from Your Other Accounts: 

• Go to your other accounts (personal, old, or additional business accounts). 

• Open the “Followers” list for each account. 

3. Send Follow Requests to These Followers: 

• One by one, visit their profiles. 

• Tap the “Follow” button from your main business account. 

• Many will follow back, especially if they already know you from another account. 

4. Post a Story Announcing Your Main Account: 

• On your other accounts, post an Instagram Story telling your followers about your main business account. 

• Add a direct link to your profile and encourage them to follow. 

5. Update Your Bio on Other Accounts: 

• If you’re keeping multiple accounts active, update their bios with a message like: 

“Follow my main account @YourBusinessHandle for the latest updates!”

How to Add Contacts to Instagram to Increase Your Followers 

How to Add Contacts to Instagram to Increase Your Followers 

March 7, 2025 

Table of contents 

Instagram allows you to connect with people you already know by syncing your phone’s contact list. This is an easy way to increase your followers by inviting people who have your number saved. 

Steps to Add Your Contacts to Instagram 

1. Check If You’ve Given Instagram Access to Your Contacts: 

• Open the Instagram app. 

• Go to your profile by tapping the bottom-right icon. 

• Tap the three-line menu (☰) in the top-right corner and select “Settings and privacy.” 

• Scroll to “Account” and select “Contacts Syncing.” 

• If it’s off, turn on the toggle for “Connect Contacts.” 

2. Sync Your Contacts with Instagram: 

• Once enabled, Instagram will suggest people from your contact list to follow. 

• Go to the “Discover People” section in your profile: 

Tap the notification on your phone's home screen, then tap Follow . 

You can also tap the heart icon in the top right to view the notification, then tap Follow and follow those you recognize. 

Many of them will follow you back. 

3. Manually Invite People in Your Contacts to Follow You: 

If you have a list of real estate clients or business connections, send them a direct message or SMS. 

​ 

Example message: 

​ 

“Hey [Name], I just started sharing great real estate tips on Instagram! Follow me at @YourHandle for market updates and home-buying tips!” 

This method helps you reach people who are already familiar with you, increasing the chances of gaining loyal followers.

Steps to Promote Your Instagram on Other Platforms 

1. Add Your Instagram Handle to All Social Profiles 

• Update your bio on Facebook, Twitter, and LinkedIn with your Instagram link. 

• Example: “📸 Follow me on Instagram for daily real estate insights: @YourHandle.”

• Reply to comments, DMs, and mentions.

## Why Your Facebook Business Page Doesn’t Get Organic Engagement | Roomvu Help Center

Why Your Facebook Business Page Doesn’t Get Organic Engagement 

Why Your Facebook Business Page Doesn’t Get Organic Engagement 

March 7, 2025 

Table of contents 

1. Facebook Prioritizes Paid Content Over Organic Reach 

Facebook’s algorithm favors ads and personal interactions . Since Facebook Business Pages are designed for companies, their posts are often limited in reach unless boosted with paid ads. 

2. Facebook Wants Businesses to Pay for Visibility 

Unlike a few years ago, when organic reach was higher, Facebook now limits unpaid posts from Business Pages. Without advertising, your posts may only reach a tiny percentage of your followers. 

3. Facebook Business Pages Are Like Digital Storefronts 

A Facebook Business Page is no longer a place for organic engagement but rather a reference point for your business. It’s where people: 

• Look up your services 

• Read reviews 

• Find contact details 

The Solution: Use Your Personal Facebook Profile for Engagement 

Your Personal Facebook Profile gets up to 5X more engagement than a Business Page. This is because: 

✅ Personal profiles appear more often in people’s feeds. 

✅ Friends and family are more likely to interact with your content. 

✅ Facebook favors real people over businesses in its algorithm. 

What You Can Do: 

💡 Post real estate content on your Personal Facebook Profile in addition to your Business Page. 

💡 Engage with your audience personally by commenting, liking, and sharing posts. 

💡 Use your Business Page as a professional reference , but focus engagement efforts on your personal profile. 

How to Set Up & Connect Your Facebook Accounts to roomvu 

Option 1: Connect Your Personal Facebook Profile to roomvu 

Since personal profiles get better engagement, we strongly recommend connecting your Personal Facebook Profile to roomvu. This allows us to post real estate content directly to your profile, helping you reach more people organically. 

Steps to Connect Your Personal Profile: 

1️⃣ Log in to your roomvu account . 

2️⃣ Go to Account Settings > Social Media Connections . 

3️⃣ Click Connect Facebook and select your Personal Profile . 

4️⃣ Grant roomvu the necessary permissions. 

5️⃣ Done! roomvu will now post content to your profile for better reach. 

Option 2: Keep Your Facebook Business Page & Use It Strategically 

If you prefer to keep your Business Page connected , consider using it mainly as a digital presence while sharing roomvu content manually to your Personal Profile for better engagement. 

How to Share Business Page Content on Your Personal Profile 

🔹 Go to your Facebook Business Page. 

🔹 Find a post you want to share. 

🔹 Click Share , then select Share to Feed . 

🔹 Add a personal caption (optional) and post it. 

This will boost visibility and encourage engagement from your personal network. 

Final Thoughts: Maximize Your Facebook Strategy 

✅ Facebook Business Pages are no longer built for organic reach. 

✅ Personal Profiles get 5X more engagement and should be used to share real estate content. 

✅ Your Business Page is a digital storefront —use it as a reference for potential clients. 

✅ For the best results, connect your Personal Facebook Profile to roomvu for automated, high-engagement content. 

🚀 Start growing your reach today! Connect your Facebook Profile to roomvu and take your engagement to the next level.

## How to Sync Contacts on LinkedIn to Connect with People You Know | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/10730098-how-to-sync-contacts-on-linkedin-to-connect-with-people-you-know

How to Sync Contacts on LinkedIn to Connect with People You Know | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content

How to Sync Contacts on LinkedIn to Connect with People You Know 

How to Sync Contacts on LinkedIn to Connect with People You Know 

March 7, 2025 

Table of contents 

Syncing your contacts on LinkedIn allows you to connect with people directly from your address book . This makes it easier to grow your network by finding colleagues, clients, and business connections who are already on LinkedIn. 

Follow this guide to sync all your contacts via LinkedIn. 

How to Sync Your Contacts on LinkedIn 

Step 1: Access Account Settings 

1. Open LinkedIn and log in to your account. 

2. Click on your profile icon at the top right. 

3. Select Settings & Privacy from the dropdown menu. 

4. Go to Account Preferences . 

Step 2: Select the Syncing Options 

1. In Account Preferences , scroll down to find Syncing Options . 

2. Click Sync Contacts to begin the process. 

Step 3: Choose Where to Sync Contacts From 

You can choose to sync contacts from: 

✅ Phone Contacts – Syncs LinkedIn with your saved mobile contacts. 

✅ Gmail Account – Connects LinkedIn with your Google Contacts. 

✅ Outlook – Syncs contacts from your Microsoft account. 

💡 Recommendation: Selecting Phone Contacts ensures that anyone on LinkedIn with their current phone number will sync to your account. 

Step 4: Syncing with Gmail or Outlook 

• If you choose Gmail , LinkedIn will redirect you to log in. 

• Follow the on-screen instructions to allow LinkedIn to access your contacts. 

Step 5: Syncing with Mobile Contacts 

If you want to sync contacts directly from your mobile device , follow these steps: 

1. Open the LinkedIn mobile app . 

2. Tap your profile icon at the top left. 

3. Select Settings > Sync Contacts . 

4. Enable Contacts Syncing to allow LinkedIn to connect with people in your phone’s address book. 

Why Syncing Contacts Helps You on LinkedIn 

✔ Easier Networking – Connect with people you already know. 

✔ Find Business Opportunities – Reconnect with past colleagues and potential clients. 

✔ Expand Your Professional Network – Automatically discover people in your industry. 

By syncing your contacts, you can make the most out of LinkedIn and stay connected with valuable connections. 🚀

• Click on the My Network icon at the top of your LinkedIn homepage. 

• Review the list of suggested connections based on your profile and existing network.

## How to Manage Your LinkedIn Profile Photo Visibility | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/10730147-how-to-manage-your-linkedin-profile-photo-visibility

How to Manage Your LinkedIn Profile Photo Visibility | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Tutorials 

How to Manage Your LinkedIn Profile Photo Visibility 

How to Manage Your LinkedIn Profile Photo Visibility 

March 7, 2025 

Table of contents 

Your LinkedIn profile photo plays a crucial role in helping your connections and other professionals recognize you. While adding a profile photo is optional, it significantly boosts your visibility— profiles with a photo receive up to 2X more views and 3X more connection requests. 

You can control who can see your profile photo by adjusting your visibility settings. Follow the steps below to manage your profile photo visibility both within LinkedIn and on your public profile. 

How to Change Profile Photo Visibility on LinkedIn 

To modify the visibility of your profile photo for LinkedIn members: 

1️⃣ Click the Me icon at the top of your LinkedIn homepage. 

2️⃣ Click View Profile . 

3️⃣ Click on your profile photo to open the settings. 

4️⃣ Click the Visibility icon (on the left side of the pop-up window). 

5️⃣ Select who can see your profile photo from the following options: 

• 1st-degree connections only (People you’re directly connected with) 

• Your network (Connections + their connections) 

• All LinkedIn members (Anyone with a LinkedIn account) 

• Anyone (Completely public, even outside LinkedIn) 

6️⃣ Click Save to apply changes. 

How to Change Profile Photo Visibility on Your Public Profile 

Your public profile determines how your profile appears to people outside of LinkedIn , including search engines. If you want to adjust how your profile photo appears in Google or Bing searches: 

1️⃣ Click the Me icon at the top of your LinkedIn homepage. 

2️⃣ Click View Profile . 

3️⃣ Click Edit public profile & URL on the right-side panel. 

4️⃣ Under Edit Visibility , scroll down to the Profile Photo section. 

5️⃣ Select one of the following options: 

• Only 1st-degree connections (Only direct connections can see it) 

• Your network (Connections + their connections) 

• All LinkedIn members (Anyone on LinkedIn can see it) 

• Public (Anyone on the internet can see it) 

🔹 Changes are saved automatically. 

🚨 Important: These settings can only be updated on the LinkedIn desktop site and cannot be changed from the mobile app. 

Key Notes About Profile Photo Visibility 

✅ The default setting for profile photos is Anyone (Public). 

✅ If you adjust your profile photo visibility from your profile page , it also updates your public profile settings automatically. 

✅ You can set different visibility levels for your LinkedIn profile and your public profile (e.g., making your photo visible to all LinkedIn members but not to search engines). 

✅ If your public profile is disabled , you cannot set your profile photo visibility as Public . 

Final Thoughts 

Your LinkedIn profile photo helps establish credibility and build trust with potential connections, recruiters, and clients. If you want to maximize your professional presence, consider keeping your profile photo visible to a broader audience. 

🔹 Need help optimizing your LinkedIn presence? Check out more LinkedIn tips in our Help Center! 🚀

## How to Get More Google Reviews for Your Business | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/10730176-how-to-get-more-google-reviews-for-your-business

How to Get More Google Reviews for Your Business | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Tutorials 

How to Get More Google Reviews for Your Business 

How to Get More Google Reviews for Your Business 

March 7, 2025 

Table of contents 

Google reviews are essential for enhancing your online presence, building trust with potential clients, and improving your local search ranking. A robust collection of positive reviews can significantly influence a prospect’s decision to engage your services. Here’s a guide on how to effectively gather reviews for your Google My Business (GMB) profile: 

1. Claim and Verify Your Google My Business Profile 

Ensure you have claimed and verified your GMB profile to manage your business information and interact with reviewers. This process allows you to respond to reviews and make necessary updates to your business details. 

2. Create and Share a Direct Review Link 

Simplify the review process for your clients by providing them with a direct link to your GMB review page: 

• Generate the Link: Sign in to your GMB account, click on the “Home” tab, and find the “Get more reviews” card. Click “Share review form” to copy your unique review link. 

• Shorten the Link: Use a URL shortening service like Bitly to create a more manageable link, especially useful for printed materials or concise communications. 

• Share the Link: Incorporate this shortened link into your email signatures, thank-you emails, invoices, or directly send it via text messages to clients after a successful transaction. 

3. Request Reviews from Satisfied Clients 

Encourage your happy clients to share their experiences: 

• Timing: Ask for a review soon after a successful transaction when the experience is fresh in their minds. 

• Personalization: Tailor your request to each client, expressing genuine interest in their feedback. 

• Guidance: Provide clear instructions on how to leave a review, possibly including a step-by-step guide to assist them. 

4. Utilize Review Generation Tools 

Consider using automated tools to streamline the review collection process: 

• Automation: These tools can send timely review requests to clients, increasing the likelihood of receiving feedback. 

• Customization: Many platforms allow you to customize messages to align with your brand’s tone and style. 

5. Display Existing Reviews to Encourage More Feedback 

Showcasing current reviews can motivate other clients to share their experiences: 

• Website Integration: Feature positive reviews on your website to highlight client satisfaction. 

• Social Media Sharing: Share testimonials on your social media platforms to reach a broader audience. 

6. Respond to All Reviews 

Engage with clients by responding to their reviews: 

• Positive Reviews: Express gratitude and appreciation for their feedback. 

• Negative Reviews: Address concerns professionally and offer solutions to resolve any issues. 

This interaction demonstrates your commitment to client satisfaction and can encourage others to leave their feedback. 

7. Provide Exceptional Service 

Delivering outstanding service naturally leads to positive reviews: 

• Exceed Expectations: Go above and beyond in your client interactions to leave a lasting impression. 

• Follow-Up: Check in with clients after services are rendered to ensure their satisfaction and address any concerns promptly. 

By implementing these strategies, you can effectively gather more reviews on your Google My Business profile, enhancing your online reputation and attracting more potential clients. 

For a visual walkthrough on setting up Google reviews with Google My Business, you might find this video helpful:

## How to Export Contacts from Gmail and Yahoo | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/10742594-how-to-export-contacts-from-gmail-and-yahoo

How to Export Contacts from Gmail and Yahoo | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Tutorials 

How to Export Contacts from Gmail and Yahoo 

How to Export Contacts from Gmail and Yahoo 

March 10, 2025 

Table of contents 

Exporting your contacts from Gmail and Yahoo Mail allows you to back them up or transfer them to another service. Follow the steps below to export your contacts from each platform. 

Exporting Contacts from Gmail 

1. Access Google Contacts : 

• Log in to your Gmail account. 

• Click the Google Apps icon (a grid) in the top-right corner and select Contacts . 

2. Select Contacts to Export : 

• In Google Contacts, choose the contacts you wish to export by clicking the checkboxes next to their names. To select all contacts, click the checkbox at the top of the list. 

3. Initiate Export : 

• Click the More actions icon (three vertical dots) and select Export . 

4. Choose Export Settings : 

• In the pop-up window, select the contacts you want to export and choose the export format: 

• Google CSV : For importing into another Google account. 

• Outlook CSV : For importing into Microsoft Outlook. 

• vCard (VCF) : For importing into Apple Address Book or other applications. 

5. Complete Export : 

• Click Export and save the file to your computer. 

Exporting Contacts from Yahoo Mail 

1. Access Yahoo Contacts : 

• Log in to your Yahoo Mail account. 

• Click the Contacts icon in the top-right corner. 

2. Initiate Export : 

• Click the More options icon (three dots) and select Export (CSV) . 

3. Save the File : 

• Choose a location on your computer to save the exported contacts file. 

By following these steps, you can successfully export your contacts from both Gmail and Yahoo Mail for backup or transfer purposes.

## Exporting Contacts from DocuSign and Authentisign | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/10742628-exporting-contacts-from-docusign-and-authentisign

Exporting Contacts from DocuSign and Authentisign | Roomvu Help Center

Exporting Contacts from DocuSign and Authentisign 

Exporting Contacts from DocuSign and Authentisign 

March 10, 2025 

Table of contents 

Exporting your contacts from DocuSign and Authentisign enables you to back them up or import them into other applications. Follow the steps below to export your contacts from each platform. 

Exporting Contacts from DocuSign 

1. Log into Your DocuSign Account : 

• Access your DocuSign eSignature account using your credentials. 

2. Navigate to the Reports Section : 

• Click on the Reports tab located in the main navigation menu. 

3. Generate a Recipient Activity Report : 

• Select Recipient Activity from the list of available reports. 

• Set the desired date range for the report to include all relevant contacts. 

• Click Run Report to generate the data. 

4. Export the Report : 

• Once the report is generated, click the Download button to export it as a CSV file. 

• Save the CSV file to your computer for future use. 

Note : This method exports a list of recipients you have interacted with over the specified period. For more detailed instructions, refer to DocuSign’s support article: 

Exporting Contacts from Authentisign (TransactionDesk) 

1. Log into TransactionDesk : 

• Access your TransactionDesk account with your credentials. 

2. Access the Contacts Section : 

• Click on the Address Book icon located in the Tools tab. 

3. Select Contacts to Export : 

• Choose the contacts you wish to export by clicking the checkboxes next to their names. 

• To select all contacts, click the checkbox at the top of the list. 

4. Initiate Export : 

• Click the Export button. 

5. Save the Exported File : 

• Choose a location on your computer to save the exported CSV file. 

Note : The exported CSV file can be imported into other applications as needed. For a detailed guide, consult the following resource: 

By following these steps, you can successfully export your contacts from both DocuSign and Authentisign, ensuring you have backups or the ability to import them into other platforms.

At Roomvu, we offer Platinum Branding Design exclusively for our Platinum (or higher) subscribers . Our expert designers work closely with you to create a custom branding design that perfectly reflects your business. This branding will be applied to your videos, images, and other content shared on your social media platforms. 

Eligibility for Platinum Branding Design & Redesign 

• New Platinum Subscribers : If you have recently upgraded to a Platinum subscription, you are eligible to receive a custom branding design tailored to your business. 

• Redesign Requests : If 6 months have passed since your last branding design or redesign, you can request a new branding update . 

How to Request a Branding Redesign 

1. Check Your Eligibility 

• Ensure that you have a Platinum (or higher) subscription . 

• Make sure at least 6 months have passed since your last branding design or update. 

2. Submit Your Request 

• Head to " Branding Theme " section on your profile and click "Update Design". This will take you to our " Platinum Design Request Form " where you can pick from the options. 

3. Collaboration with Our Designers 

• Our team will review your request and work with you to create the best branding design for your business. 

• Once finalized, your new branding will be applied to all your Roomvu-generated content . 

Need Assistance? 

For any questions or concerns regarding branding design , feel free to reach out to us at info@roomvu.com .
