## How to Locate Your Zillow Profile | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/10908425-how-to-locate-your-zillow-profile

How to Locate Your Zillow Profile | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Tutorials 

How to Locate Your Zillow Profile 

How to Locate Your Zillow Profile 

Learn how to quickly find and share your Zillow profile link by searching your name through the Agent Finder on Zillow.com 

March 24, 2025 

Table of contents 

Your Zillow profile is a vital tool for showcasing your professional credentials, listings, and client reviews. To find and share your Zillow profile link, follow these steps: 

1. Visit Zillow’s Website: 

• Open your web browser and navigate to Zillow.com . 

2. Access the ‘Find an Agent’ Section: 

• At the top of Zillow’s homepage, click on the “Agent finder” tab. 

3. Search for Your Name: 

• In the search bar, enter your full name as it appears on your Zillow profile. 

• Optionally, input your location (city or ZIP code) to refine the search results. 

4. Locate and Select Your Profile: 

• Review the search results to find your profile. 

• Click on your name to access your public profile page. 

5. Copy Your Profile URL: 

• Once on your profile page, copy the URL from the browser’s address bar. This link directs others to your Zillow profile.

## Why Some Agents Hesitate to Use AI in Real Estate (And How to Move Past It) | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/11037024-why-some-agents-hesitate-to-use-ai-in-real-estate-and-how-to-move-past-it

Why Some Agents Hesitate to Use AI in Real Estate (And How to Move Past It) | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard

English 

Your Dashboard

English

Why Some Agents Hesitate to Use AI in Real Estate (And How to Move Past It) 

Why Some Agents Hesitate to Use AI in Real Estate (And How to Move Past It) 

April 4, 2025 

Table of contents 

Overview 

Many real estate professionals are still cautious about using AI tools for their marketing. At roomvu, we’ve heard common concerns about AI—from content quality to costs—and we’re here to help clarify what’s fact, what’s myth, and how our platform addresses these challenges. 

Common Concerns About Using AI (And How We Address Them) 

1. “AI content can be inaccurate.” 

While it’s true that AI tools can make occasional errors, roomvu’s engine pulls from only credible and verified sources , automatically filtering out irrelevant or unreliable data. This ensures that the content you post is grounded in real, local, and up-to-date information . 

2. “AI is still growing. It’s not there yet.” 

AI is evolving quickly, and professionals across industries are already using it for daily tasks. Waiting for it to “mature” could leave you behind your competition. Getting started early helps you build comfort and see results sooner. 

3. “AI content isn’t professional.” 

What feels professional is changing—especially for younger audiences who welcome tech-savvy agents. AI helps streamline your content, and with light customization, you can ensure your posts are both relevant and polished . 

4. “AI doesn’t have a human touch.” 

That’s why we encourage users to add personal intros, record quick video clips, and customize their branding. AI helps you with structure—but your personality is what makes the content truly connect . 

5. “AI content needs too much customization.” 

roomvu provides ready-to-use, hyperlocal content that doesn’t require heavy editing. You’re free to post it as-is, or tweak if you want to. Either way, it saves you hours each week. 

6. “If many agents use AI, won’t our content all look the same?” 

roomvu’s AI generates over 3,000 unique pieces of content for each market. Our system ensures that agents in the same area don’t get the same posts. Plus, 99% of your followers are unique to you , so even if content overlaps, your audience likely won’t notice. Want full customization? Our Platinum plan includes a custom visual theme made just for your brand. 

7. “Social media favors original, personal content.” 

That’s exactly why we recommend combining AI-generated posts with your face and voice . Add a video intro to your post and let AI write the script—it’s an ideal combo of efficiency and authenticity. 

8. “I’m not tech-savvy.” 

You don’t have to be! roomvu was built with agents in mind—no coding, no complex setup, just easy-to-use tools with drag-and-drop simplicity. Our support team is always here to help, too. 

9. “I barely use social media—I don’t know where to start.” 

AI can guide your posting strategy, write captions, suggest hashtags, and even schedule your posts. With just a few clicks, you’ll look like a seasoned marketer—even if you’re just getting started. 

10. “AI is expensive.” 

AI-powered marketing is more affordable than you think. Compared to hiring freelancers or spending hours creating content yourself, roomvu offers cost-effective plans that deliver value every week. 

Key Takeaway 

AI isn’t here to replace you—it’s here to help you do more, faster. By understanding the tools, customizing your content where it matters, and combining it with your own voice, you can use AI to boost your visibility and stay ahead in a competitive market. 

Still have questions? 

👉 Contact Support or check out our tutorials on Using roomvu AI for Social Media

## How to Optimize Your Instagram Profile for Real Estate | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/11321679-how-to-optimize-your-instagram-profile-for-real-estate

How to Optimize Your Instagram Profile for Real Estate | Roomvu Help Center

Your Dashboard

How to Optimize Your Instagram Profile for Real Estate 

How to Optimize Your Instagram Profile for Real Estate 

May 7, 2025 

Table of contents 

How to optimize your Instagram profile as a real estate agent or mortgage broker in the contemporary, digital-first era? That is a great question. After all, an optimized profile can significantly boost your online presence and credibility. With its visual appeal and vast user base, Instagram is a fantastic platform for showcasing property listings, client testimonials, and your brand. But to harness its full potential, it's crucial to ensure your profile is optimized. Let's delve into the intricate process of Instagram profile optimization. 

Understanding the Significance of a Complete Profile 

The first step in understanding how to optimize an Instagram profile is recognizing the significance of a complete profile. Your Instagram profile serves as a digital storefront for your brand. An incomplete profile can confuse visitors about your services and the areas you serve, undermining your professionalism. 

Remember, you only have a few seconds to make a great impression in the digital space. Hence, a comprehensive and engaging profile is paramount. It immediately communicates to visitors that you are serious about your work and adds credibility to your services. 

Mastering Instagram Profile Optimization 

Learning how to optimize your Instagram profile involves a series of steps to enhance your profile's aesthetic appeal, searchability, and informational value. Let's discuss each in detail: 

Username and Name Optimization 

Your username and name fields are the cornerstone of your Instagram presence. They should encompass your full name and relevant industry-specific keywords such as 'realtor', 'real estate agent', 'mortgage broker,' etc. By doing so, when people search for these terms, your profile is more likely to appear in their results, increasing your visibility. 

Indicate Your Operating Region 

Be clear about the city or region you cover. If you serve a broad area, list the major cities or regions you work in. This allows locals to identify you as a potential resource and helps those planning to move to your area. 

Define Your Unique Selling Proposition (USP) 

One essential aspect in your journey to understanding how to optimize your Instagram profile is identifying and articulating your USP. It could be your customer service excellence, comprehensive local real estate market knowledge, or track record securing fantastic deals. Mention these in your bio to set you apart from the competition. 

Showcase Your Achievements 

Your Instagram profile is the perfect place to highlight your professional accomplishments and recognition. Awards, notable sales, and positive client testimonials all help reinforce your expertise and commitment, providing further incentive for potential clients to choose you over others. 

Maintain Professionalism with Your Profile Picture 

Your profile picture is likely the first thing visitors notice, so it should be clear, professional, and appealing. Opt for a high-resolution headshot that's friendly yet professional. Avoid group photos, poorly lit images, or anything that could detract from your project image. 

I 

nclude Comprehensive Contact Information 

In learning how to optimize your Instagram profile, you mustn't overlook the importance of easily accessible contact information. Potential clients should have multiple ways to reach out to you, whether that's via email, phone, or direct messages. A business profile on Instagram allows you to include all these options. 

L 

ink to Your Website or Relevant Landing Pages 

Lastly, including a link to your website or relevant landing pages in your profile allows visitors to delve deeper into your services. Whether it's your latest listings, a blog on market trends, or an inquiry form, make it easy for potential clients to navigate to the information they need.

How to Optimize Your Instagram Profile to Convert More Visitors into Followers

## Are you compliant with CRTC, CTC, and other regulations regarding calling and SMS messaging to leads? | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/11654892-are-you-compliant-with-crtc-ctc-and-other-regulations-regarding-calling-and-sms-messaging-to-leads

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Features 

Are you compliant with CRTC, CTC, and other regulations regarding calling and SMS messaging to leads? 

Are you compliant with CRTC, CTC, and other regulations regarding calling and SMS messaging to leads? 

June 25, 2025 

Yes, we are fully compliant with the CRTC (Canadian Radio-television and Telecommunications Commission), CTC (Canadian Telecommunications Commission), and all applicable federal and provincial regulations governing telemarketing, SMS communication, and consumer privacy. 

When a lead submits their information through one of our landing pages—such as Facebook Lead Ads or other Roomvu-powered forms—they are presented with a clear and transparent consent statement. By submitting their information, they agree to our collection and use of their data, which includes permission to be contacted by phone and SMS. This process ensures that consent is both informed and documented, which is a requirement under Canada’s Anti-Spam Legislation (CASL) and other compliance frameworks. 

Additionally, every SMS we send includes a simple opt-out option. Leads can unsubscribe at any time by replying with the word “STOP,” and our system will immediately flag their number and halt future messaging. This ensures continued compliance and demonstrates our commitment to respectful communication practices. 

We take compliance seriously to protect not only our customers but also the reputation and integrity of the businesses we serve.

## Why can’t you call or text the leads I import into the system? | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/11654907-why-can-t-you-call-or-text-the-leads-i-import-into-the-system

Why can’t you call or text the leads I import into the system? | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Features 

Why can’t you call or text the leads I import into the system? 

Why can’t you call or text the leads I import into the system? 

June 25, 2025 

Leads that you manually import into our system—such as through CSV uploads or CRM integrations—have not provided consent through our standardized forms and processes. Because of this, we do not have documented proof that they agreed to receive phone calls or SMS messages from our platform or on your behalf. 

This is an important distinction when it comes to compliance. Regulations such as CASL and CRTC’s Unsolicited Telecommunications Rules require clear, affirmative consent for telemarketing and text messaging. Without that consent, initiating calls or SMS communications would be a violation of these laws. 

To protect your business from potential legal and financial risks, our platform is designed to only allow phone and SMS outreach to leads who have gone through our verified consent process. For imported leads, we limit communications to email—assuming you already have the appropriate email permissions from them. This approach ensures that we remain compliant while still giving you the tools to nurture and engage your contacts in a legally sound way. 

If you would like to start calling or texting a group of leads, we recommend directing them to one of our landing pages to re-capture the required consent in compliance with regulations.

How Can I Find My Subscription Details and Manage My Billing? 

March 30, 2026 

To easily view your subscription information and manage your billing options, follow these simple steps: 

Log into your account. 

Click the gear icon located at the top right corner to open your Settings . 

In the left-side menu, scroll down to the Other section. 

Click on Payment & Billing . 

Here, you will find important details about your subscription, including: 

Plan Fee 

Payment Amount 

Subscription Start Date 

Cancel On (Date) 

You will also have options to: 

Switch to Yearly billing 

Pause Your Billing 

Downgrade your plan 

Renew to Lock Prices 

Additionally, your Payment History is available, showing: 

Date 

Amount 

Transaction Type 

Details 

Reference Number 

If you have any questions or need further assistance, feel free to contact our support team.

## How to enable Facebook personal auto‑sharing? | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/11795169-how-to-enable-facebook-personal-auto-sharing

How to enable Facebook personal auto‑sharing? | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard

English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Tutorials 

How to enable Facebook personal auto‑sharing? 

How to enable Facebook personal auto‑sharing? 

Platinum+ lets you link one business Instagram for Roomvu publishing and one personal Instagram for cross‑posting to your Facebook profile. 

Updated over a week ago 

Table of contents 

Before you begin 

Plan level: You must be on a Platinum+ subscription. 

Accounts needed: 

Business Instagram – linked to a Facebook Page (for regular Roomvu posting). Connecting IG is more recommended for IG itself. 

Personal Instagram – linked to your Facebook profile (for auto‑sharing). 

Permissions: Have your Facebook login handy; Meta will ask you to grant access twice. 

1. Add your business Instagram (for publishing) 

Log in to Roomvu and click the Content Calendar from the left side menu. Then click " Connect More Socials ". 

Connect Instagram Business. 

Select your Business Instagram in the Meta pop‑up and allow all requested permissions. 

Back in roomvu, confirm it appears under Connected Accounts with the Publishing toggle ON . 

2. Add your personal Instagram (for Facebook profile sharing) 

Stay in the same menu and click Instagram . 

Choose your Personal Instagram in the Meta pop‑up. 

Grant the permissions. (Meta automatically detects its link to your Facebook profile via Accounts Center.) 

In Roomvu, turn the Publishing toggle OFF for this account (we won’t post to the personal IG feed). 

Make sure Share to Facebook Profile is ON . 

Got questions? Reach out via support@roomvu.com or live chat—we’re happy to help.

## How to Integrate BoldTrail (KVCore) and Zapier | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/11831433-how-to-integrate-boldtrail-kvcore-and-zapier

How to Integrate BoldTrail (KVCore) and Zapier | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Integration 

How to Integrate BoldTrail (KVCore) and Zapier 

How to Integrate BoldTrail (KVCore) and Zapier 

July 23, 2025 

Table of contents 

BoldTrail (Formerly kvCORE) has numerous options for funneling your generated leads. You can use Zapier to get leads from roomvu into BoldTrail automatically as a new lead and start getting all of your existing leads flowing in the system. If you have integrated roomvu into Zapier then you can use BoldTrail as well with a little help from this article! 

How to Integrate BoldTrail and Zapier 

1. On your BoldTrail dashboard, click on the ' Lead Engine ' tab from the left side bar. Then, click on the ' Lead Dropbox ' on the top right. 

2. Next copy your Zapier Key. 

Setting Up Zapier With Your BoldTrail Account 

Get the BoldTrail Zap Link 

Zapier Invite Link. 

Clicking on this link . This will prompt you to log into your existing Zapier account or create a new one. Since you are here, you already have a Zapier account. 

After logging in you’ll be asked to accept the invite and build a Zap! The next screen will look very similar to the previous one, but it will take you to your first Zap. 

Because the link is an invite, it assumes you want to create a Zap right away. You’re more than welcome to create a Zap later. 

Creating Zaps for New Leads 

The first page you land on after following the invite link and filling out your information has the steps for creating a new Zap. You’ll first want to select a trigger. 

However, before continuing you have to decide one of two things. 

· Am I sending leads FROM BoldTrail TO somewhere else ? 

· Am I sending leads TO BoldTrail FROM somewhere else ? 

Sending Leads FROM BoldTrail TO Another Platform: 

If you’d like to send your leads from BoldTrail to another system, you can proceed to the example Zap. The example Zap starts with the original page you land on after clicking the invite link at the beginning of this guide , and you don't need to change the trigger app. It's already set to BoldTrail. 

When starting with BoldTrail as the trigger app, your only option is to send a lead to another program from your BoldTrail CRM. 

Sending Leads TO BoldTrail FROM Another Platform: 

If you’d like to send leads from another system to BoldTrail, you need to change your trigger app. The trigger app is the first step of a Zap. Since the lead is coming from another program (not BoldTrail), we must start with that program as our trigger app. 

To change the trigger app: 

1. Click the ‘change’ button to change the trigger app from BoldTrail to a different starting program (the program where the leads are coming FROM.) 

2. Click on the search box to find the trigger you’d like to use. 

3. As soon as you select the one you want your trigger will change! 

From here you can proceed to the example zap below to follow along.

## Create Stand‑Out Videos in Seconds with roomvu’s AI Content Creation | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/11887174-create-stand-out-videos-in-seconds-with-roomvu-s-ai-content-creation

Create Stand‑Out Videos in Seconds with roomvu’s AI Content Creation 

Create Stand‑Out Videos in Seconds with roomvu’s AI Content Creation 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Introduction – Your New Content Superpower 

Online marketing success lives on social, and AI Content Creation lets you seize the moment without breaking stride. From your Roomvu dashboard you can dream up a hyper‑local topic, flip it into a polished video or slideshow, tack on a selfie intro for personality, and schedule it—all before your coffee cools. No editing software, no file juggling, just a seamless 10‑second workflow that turns ideas into lead‑magnet posts. 

1. Meet Your On‑Demand Studio 

Every market, every client base, every listing is unique—so why settle for one‑size‑fits‑all content? AI Content Creation places a virtual production crew at your fingertips: 

Cover any angle – Break down policy changes, showcase neighborhood coffee spots, or spotlight exclusive listings. 

Stay hyper‑local – Tailor clips to zip‑code‑level stats or school districts your followers care about. 

Mix formats – Quick slideshow carousels for swipe‑happy scroll‑ers, full videos for storytelling. 

Because you choose the topic and format, no two agents deliver the same feed. Your voice cuts through the noise—and your audience knows you “get” their market. 

2. Why It’s Revolutionary 

Speed – Idea‑to‑publish in 10 seconds keeps you topical. 

Ease – No technical hurdles; the AI writes, edits, and schedules. 

Brand control – Consistent colors, fonts, and logo placement keep every post on‑brand. 

Intros = impact – Agents who attach selfie intros via AI Content Creation enjoy up to 10× more engagement, quadruple watch‑time, and six‑times higher share rates. 

The result? A content engine that feels human, looks pro, and runs on autopilot. 

3. Step‑by‑Step: From Idea to Post 

Open your Content Calendar 

​ Navigate to your Roomvu dashboard and click “Content Calendar” on the left‑hand menu. 

​ 

Hit “Add Content” 

​ Find the blue “Add Content” button at the top‑right corner of the calendar view and click it. 

Choose “Create Your Own Content” 

​ In the pop‑up, pick the first option on the left labelled “Create Your Own Content.” 

Type Your Topic or Idea 

​ Enter anything—from “April condo prices in Kitsilano” to “5 staging tricks that cost under $100.” The AI can handle broad or niche prompts. 

Select Your Format 

​ Decide between Video (ideal for storytelling) or Slideshow Carousel (perfect for step‑by‑step tips). 

​ 

Create Content 

​ hit “Create My Video,” or “Create My Slideshow,”and pat yourself on the back—the post is queued and ready to roll. See the details of the slides or videos in the next step and once your are happy click "Generate video" or "Genrate Carousel" and done! 

4. Face‑Forward Intros: The Engagement Multiplier 

Algorithms crave authentic faces. A selfie intro delivered through AI Content Creation stops thumbs mid‑scroll, signals trust, and sets your clip apart from cookie‑cutter market updates. Our data shows: 

1,000 % engagement lift versus text‑only reels 

4× longer average watch‑time 

Increased inbound DMs as viewers feel they “know” you 

Keep the intro tight (under 10 seconds), smile, mention the value they’re about to get, and let roomvu’s engine handle the merge. 

5. Slide‑Show Carousels: Swipe‑Able Storytelling 

Sometimes video isn’t necessary—think before/after remodels, quick stat bursts, or multi‑step checklists. Choose Slideshow Carousel and AI Content Creation auto‑generates branded images, overlays concise captions, and schedules the post. Perfect for: 

Mini neighborhood tours (each slide = one hotspot) 

Cost breakdowns (slide per expense) 

“3 Mistakes Sellers Make” series 

Your feed stays varied and visually fresh without extra effort. 

6. Content Prompts to Try Tonight 

Breaking News : “Explain today’s Fed rate decision for first‑time buyers.” 

Hyper‑Local Stats : “3‑slide recap: median price change in River Oaks this month.” 

Lifestyle : “Top dog‑friendly patios in downtown Tampa.” 

Education : “Video: Adjustable vs. fixed mortgages simplified.” 

Seasonal : “Fall checklist for home‑sellers 2025.” 

Drop the prompt, select format, and AI Content Creation handles the rest—color‑grading, captions, and scheduling included. 

Final Words – Own Every Feed 

Consistency beats luck. With AI Content Creation baked into your Roomvu dashboard, your next viral post is always 10 seconds away. Pair smart topics with selfie intros, schedule a week’s content in one sitting, and turn your social presence into a round‑the‑clock lead engine—no technicians, no pricey editors, just you and your brand in every scroll.

## How to Grow Your Instagram Followers from 40 to 200 in 2 Months | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/12138574-how-to-grow-your-instagram-followers-from-40-to-200-in-2-months

How to Grow Your Instagram Followers from 40 to 200 in 2 Months 

How to Grow Your Instagram Followers from 40 to 200 in 2 Months 

September 5, 2025 

Table of contents 

If you’re starting out with only 40 followers, reaching 200 may feel challenging—but with the right daily actions, it’s achievable. By consistently spending just 15–20 minutes a day , you can expand your reach, build credibility, and grow your follower base to 200+ in about two months. Here’s how: 

1. Follow 10 People Daily 

Sync your phone contacts and connect with clients, colleagues, and friends already on Instagram. 

Search local businesses (cafés, gyms, shops) and follow their most active followers. 

How to: 

To access the "Upload contacts" feature on Instagram, follow these steps: 

​ 

Navigate to your Instagram profile and tap the three horizontal lines in the top right corner to open the Settings menu. 

From the menu, select "Settings and privacy." 

Tap on "Accounts Center." 

Within the Accounts Center, find and tap on "Your information and permissions." 

Finally, select "Upload contacts" to manage your contact syncing settings. 

​ 

While Instagram may suggest this feature to you, especially if you have a new or small account, it's helpful to know how to find it manually using the path above. 

Discovering People to Follow 

Stay consistent—10 a day adds up to 600+ new connections in two months. 

​ 

To grow your audience, staying consistent with who you follow is key. Aim for around 10 new connections a day, and you'll have over 600 in two months. 

While Instagram often suggests people for you to follow, you can also actively discover new connections. To do this, go to your Followers list. Scroll down to the bottom, and you'll find the Discover People option. Tapping on this will bring up a list of people Instagram recommends based on your interests and existing connections. 

​ 

2. Leave Thoughtful Comments 

Don’t just write “Nice post.” Instead, offer value: “Love how you staged this living room—it feels so inviting!” 

Engage with other realtors, local businesses, or community pages. 

Authentic comments spark curiosity and often lead to profile visits. 

3. Share Your Profile Link Everywhere 

Add your Instagram handle at the end of your email signature. 

Share it on WhatsApp, Facebook, or LinkedIn with friends, clients, and past contacts. 

The more entry points you create, the faster your audience grows. 

4. Collaborate with Friends and Colleagues 

Take photos or short videos together at events, showings, or community activities. 

Use Instagram’s collaborate feature to share the same post on both accounts. 

Collaborations double visibility and attract audiences from both sides. 

5. Use Location Tags 

Always tag your city, neighbourhood, or venue when posting. 

Posts with location tags can show up on the Instagram map, making you discoverable to people nearby. 

This works especially well for realtors aiming to reach local buyers and sellers. 

6. Boost with Local Ads or Sponsorships 

Run small ads targeting local audiences interested in real estate or community events. 

Partner with local businesses by sponsoring an event or cross-promoting content. 

Even a small budget can give you exposure to hundreds of new followers. 

The Bottom Line 

By following these steps consistently, you’ll not only reach 200 followers but also build a quality, local audience that engages with your content. The key is daily effort —just 15–20 minutes a day adds up to big results in two months. 

FAQs: 

How many followers can I realistically gain in 2 months? 

If you start with 40 and apply these tactics daily, reaching 200+ is achievable. 

What’s the fastest action I can take today? 

Follow 10 new local accounts and leave meaningful comments—that drives immediate profile visits. 

Do I need to run ads to hit 200? 

Not necessarily. Ads help speed things up, but organic engagement and collaborations can get you there too. 

How much time do I need to spend? 

Around 15–20 minutes a day is enough—consistency matters more than long sessions. 

Should I focus on quality or quantity of followers? 

Always quality. Local, engaged followers are more valuable than random numbers.

## How to Optimize Your Instagram Profile to Convert More Visitors into Followers | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/12139017-how-to-optimize-your-instagram-profile-to-convert-more-visitors-into-followers

How to Optimize Your Instagram Profile to Convert More Visitors into Followers | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Social media 

How to Optimize Your Instagram Profile to Convert More Visitors into Followers 

How to Optimize Your Instagram Profile to Convert More Visitors into Followers 

September 3, 2025 

Table of contents 

Your Instagram profile is your digital business card . When someone visits, you have only a few seconds to make them hit "Follow." By optimizing your profile photo, bio, highlights, pinned posts, and handle, you can turn casual visitors into engaged followers. 

1. Profile Photo: First Impressions Matter 

Use a high-quality headshot with good lighting. 

Look approachable: smile and face the camera directly. 

Avoid group shots or casual selfies—this should look professional. 

2. Bio: Who You Are & What You Do 

Start with your profession + location (e.g., “🏡 Realtor | Chicago Downtown” ). 

Add a short, clear value statement (e.g., “Helping families find their dream homes” ). 

Include a contact option (phone, email, or DM). 

If you have one, add your website link for leads. 

3. Highlights: Curate Your Brand Story 

Create 2–3 highlights with clean, branded covers. 

Good examples: 

About Me – introduce yourself. 

Clients – testimonials or success stories. 

Tips – quick real estate or market tips. 

Listings – feature your best properties. 

4. Pinned Posts: Showcase Your Best Content 

Pin 2–3 posts to the top of your profile. 

Best choices include: 

A short intro video to welcome visitors. 

A strong client testimonial . 

A market update to show authority. 

5. Instagram Page Name (Handle) 

Keep it simple and easy to spell . 

Ideally include your name, profession, or location . 

Short and memorable works best (avoid random numbers). 

FAQs: 

Do I need a professional photoshoot for my profile picture? 

Not always—just ensure it’s high-quality, well-lit, and professional-looking. 

How long should my bio be? 

Short and clear—1–2 lines that explain who you are and how you help. 

What if I don’t have many highlights yet? 

Start with just one (like About Me ) and add more as your content grows. 

How often should I update pinned posts? 

Every few months, or when you have new content that better represents your brand. 

Is it okay to change my handle later? 

Yes, but pick something simple early on to avoid confusion with followers.

## How to Reach Your First 50 LinkedIn Connections | Roomvu Help Center

How to Reach Your First 50 LinkedIn Connections 

How to Reach Your First 50 LinkedIn Connections 

September 5, 2025 

Table of contents 

Starting from zero on LinkedIn can feel intimidating, but reaching 50 connections is easier than you think. With a strong profile and consistent effort, you can quickly grow a valuable network that builds credibility and opens doors. 

1. Optimize Your Profile First 

Upload a professional headshot (no casual selfies). 

Write a clear headline that reflects your role and value. 

Complete your work history and education so people can instantly recognize your background. 

2. Sync & Upload Your Contacts 

Use LinkedIn’s "Sync Contacts" feature to instantly connect with people already in your phone or email, giving you an instant base of familiar connections. 

To find this feature: 

Tap your profile picture in the top-left corner of the LinkedIn app. 

Tap Settings 

Click Account Prefrences . 

Scroll down to the "Syncing options" section. 

Select Sync contacts to begin the process. 

​ 

​ 

3. Connect with Colleagues & Past Clients 

Search for coworkers, former colleagues, and clients you’ve worked with. 

Always include a personalized note with your connection request (e.g., “Great working with you at X — would love to stay connected here on LinkedIn!” ). 

4. Use LinkedIn Suggestions 

Visit the “My Network” tab and check “People you may know.” 

Send up to 10 requests per day —but focus on people who already know you or share common interests. 

5. Write Thoughtful Comments 

Engage with your connections’ posts regularly. 

Go beyond “Congrats” by adding meaningful insights or asking relevant questions. 

This builds visibility and encourages new connection requests. 

6. Add Your LinkedIn Link to Emails 

Place your LinkedIn profile link in your email signature . 

Every email becomes a chance for someone to connect with you. 

Quick FAQs 

How long will it take to reach 50 connections? 

With 5–10 connection requests daily, you can get there in 1–2 weeks. 

Should I connect with people I don’t know? 

Focus on those you know first—colleagues, classmates, clients. Later, expand to industry peers. 

What if someone ignores my request? 

Don’t worry. Keep engaging with their posts—sometimes they’ll connect later. 

Do I need to post content right away? 

Not required, but commenting on others’ posts is a great way to stay visible early on. 

Is it okay to connect with recruiters? 

Yes! Recruiters are always open to expanding their networks and can bring career opportunities.

How to Reach Your First 20 YouTube Subscribers 

September 3, 2025 

Table of contents 

Getting your first 20 subscribers is an important milestone. It shows people are interested in your content and gives your channel credibility. By using your personal network and simple promotion strategies, you can reach this goal quickly. 

1. Ask Friends, Family, and Colleagues 

Share your channel link directly with friends, family, and coworkers. 

Add a personal message : “I just launched my YouTube channel on local real estate tips—would love your support by subscribing!” 

2. Promote on Instagram Stories 

Post your new YouTube video link in your Instagram Stories . 

Use polls, stickers, or short teasers to encourage clicks. 

3. Share Short Local Clips

Post them on YouTube and promote with location tags and hashtags to make your videos discoverable. 

4. Use WhatsApp Status 

After uploading a video, add your channel link to your WhatsApp status . 

This way, friends and contacts see it passively without you needing to send direct messages every time. 

5. Host a Live Session on YouTube 

Run a short, simple live session (e.g., “5 Tips for First-Time Homebuyers”). 

Personally invite contacts via email and encourage them to subscribe while watching.

What type of videos work best early on?

Should I ask directly for subscriptions? 

Yes—always include a call-to-action like “Don’t forget to subscribe!” in your videos. 

Do I need professional equipment? 

No—your phone is enough as long as the video is clear and the sound is good.

## Import Google Contacts into roomvu | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/12599379-import-google-contacts-into-roomvu

Import Google Contacts into roomvu | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard

English

All Collections 

Tutorials 

Import Google Contacts into roomvu 

Import Google Contacts into roomvu 

A complete step-by-step guide to importing all your Google contacts, including hidden ones, into Roomvu for effortless email marketing. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

If you use Gmail or an Android phone, chances are you already have a full address book stored in Google Contacts —even if you’ve never added anyone manually. Google automatically keeps track of the people you email, call, or message, and stores them under your account. This includes: 

Contacts saved on your phone and synced to Google 

People you’ve emailed in Gmail (even if you never clicked “Save”) 

Contacts imported from apps like Calendar or Meet 

Before importing your Google contacts into roomvu , it’s important to make sure all of them; especially those under Other contacts are added to your main Contacts list. This ensures every person you communicate with appears in your roomvu dashboard for email marketing and automation. 

Follow the steps below to access, organize, and import your complete Google contact list into roomvu. 

What counts as “Google contacts” (and where they come from) 

Saved Contacts : people you explicitly saved in Google Contacts or your phone’s Contacts app (these sync to your Google Account). 

Other contacts : emails you’ve interacted with in Gmail that were auto-saved for convenience (they autocomplete in Gmail but aren’t in your main list until you add them). 

Device & SIM contacts you back up/sync to your Google Account also appear in Google Contacts. 

Open Google Contacts 

Search “Google Contacts” or go to contacts.google.com . 

If prompted, sign in to your Google Account. 

You’ll land on Contacts (your saved list). 

Reveal the hidden list: “Other contacts” 

In the left sidebar, click Other contacts . 

This shows addresses Gmail saved from your past emails that aren’t in your main list yet. (Note: “Other contacts” is only visible on desktop.) 

Select everything in “Other contacts” 

Hover your mouse over any contact’s avatar/photo to reveal a checkbox ; click to select it. 

A bar appears at the top (e.g., “1 selected” ). 

Click the down-arrow next to the selection count and choose All to select every entry in “Other contacts.” 

Add them to your main Contacts 

In the top-right toolbar, click the person + (Add to contacts) button. 

The selected entries move from Other contacts to Contacts and disappear from “Other contacts.” 

Why this step matters: roomvu (and most apps) pull from your Contacts list. Moving items over ensures you import everyone —not just the already-saved people. 

Connect Google to roomvu and import 

Open your roomvu dashboard. 

In the left sidebar, go to Email Newsletters . 

Under Contacts , click All Contacts . 

Choose Import Google Contacts . 

Click Connect Google Account in the pop-up. 

Select your Google Account and allow permissions as prompted. 

Wait for confirmation—your Google contacts now appear inside roomvu → Email Marketing → Contacts . 

Tips & troubleshooting 

Don’t see “Other contacts”? Make sure you’re on desktop Google Contacts, not the mobile app. 

Contacts missing from Google? Ensure your phone contacts are syncing to your Google Account (Settings → Accounts → Google → Sync Contacts on Android). 

Prefer to keep Gmail from auto-saving future addresses to “Other contacts”? Adjust Gmail’s Create contacts for auto-complete setting.

Setup roomvu to Manage Campaigns and Contacts for Constant Contact 

roomvu’s Integration with Constant Contact Email Marketing 

How to Edit Contacts for Email Marketing in Roomvu

🏡 How to Enhance Your Listings with Voice, Avatar, and Immersive Tour 

🏡 How to Enhance Your Listings with Voice, Avatar, and Immersive Tour 

Create more engaging, personalized, and professional property videos using Roomvu’s latest Listing updates. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Tags: listings, immersive tour, avatar, voice clone, video marketing, real estate videos, roomvu tutorial 

🔊 Add Voice Clone to Listings 

Give your listing videos a personal touch by adding your AI Cloned Voice — so every narration sounds just like you. 

To add your voice clone: 

Go to your Dashboard . 

Click the Settings (⚙️ gear icon) at the top-right corner. 

From the left-side menu, select Voice Over . 

In front of Listing Videos , choose Cloned Voice from the dropdown. 

If you don’t already have a cloned voice, read this article to learn how to create one. 

Once set, your future listing videos will automatically use your cloned voice. 

🎙 Edit or Update Your Voice Clone 

If you want to refresh or re-record your cloned voice: 

In the Voice Clone section, click Update Voice Clone . 

Follow the prompts to record or upload a new voice sample. 

Your updated voice will automatically apply to future listing videos. 

🏠 Immersive Tour: What It Is & How to Create It 

The Immersive Tour feature transforms your property listing into an interactive, virtual walkthrough that gives viewers the feeling of touring the home in person. 

To create an Immersive Tour: 

From your dashboard, click MLS Listings on the left-side menu. 

Find any listing and click the "Immersive /tour" 

Wait a few minutes while Roomvu’s system automatically generates your immersive video. 

Click Here to view a sample video 

If you don’t yet have any listings imported, read this article to learn how to import them. 

Your immersive video will be ready shortly — you’ll be notified once it’s generated. 

👩‍💼 How to Add Avatar to Listings 

Your Avatar is your digital twin — it uses your headshot and cloned voice to represent you in your property videos. 

How it works: 

If you have uploaded a headshot and have a cloned voice , Roomvu will automatically include your avatar when you request an Immersive Tour . 

No extra steps are required — the avatar is created and inserted automatically into your video. 

💎 Who Can Use These Features 

Platinum users: can fully use this feature — download, share, and schedule videos with their avatar. 

All other users: the avatar video can still be generated for preview, but cannot be downloaded, shared, or scheduled . 

These tools help you stand out, connect with clients, and make every property video truly feel like you.

## How to Change Your Address on Google My Business | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/12976282-how-to-change-your-address-on-google-my-business

How to Change Your Address on Google My Business | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Tutorials 

How to Change Your Address on Google My Business 

How to Change Your Address on Google My Business 

December 2, 2025 

Table of contents 

Keeping your business address accurate helps customers find you easily on Google Maps and Google Search. Follow this guide to update, correct, or remove your address in your Google Business Profile. 

If you proceed with this action, Google will require you to verify your location. Your page will not be visible until this verification is completed. 

Before You Start: Address Requirements 

Google requires a complete and verifiable address for businesses that serve customers at a physical location. Make sure your address meets the following guidelines: 

Enter a full street address (for example, 1600 Amphitheatre Parkway, Mountain View, CA, 94043). 

Include building, suite, floor, or unit numbers if applicable. 

Only add official address details. If your region has unclear addressing, you may add nearby cross-streets or landmarks. 

Do not use descriptions like “Across from Central Park” or “Corner of Main St and Broadway Ave.” 

If your business does not have a street number or Google cannot verify your address, you can place a pin on the map instead. 

If you are a service-area business and do not serve customers at your physical address, you can hide your address and display only your service area. 

How to Add or Edit Your Address 

Open your Google Business Profile. 

Select Edit profile and then Location . 

Next to Business location , select Edit (pencil icon). 

Enter your complete address. 

If Google can’t verify your entry, you’ll see a warning. Re-enter the highlighted sections. 

If the system still cannot find your address, select Adjust to place a map pin manually. 

Select Save . 

Processing Time 

Most updates appear within 10 minutes. 

Some changes may take up to 30 days if Google reviews them. 

Special Situations 

If your business operates inside another business (for example, a store inside a mall), you can request this detail to show on your profile. 

Some profiles display an automatic location description (near a landmark or nearby business). This cannot be edited. 

How to Adjust Your Pin on the Map 

If your address has no street number or Google cannot locate it: 

Open your Google Business Profile. 

Select Edit profile and then Location . 

Next to Business location , select Edit . 

Select Adjust . 

Move the map so the pin is placed exactly on your business location. 

Select Done , then Save . 

How to Remove Your Address (Service-Area Businesses Only) 

Only choose this option if you do not serve customers at your physical location. 

Open your Google Business Profile. 

Select Edit profile and then Location . 

Next to Business location , select Edit . 

Turn off Show business address to customers . 

Select Save . 

If you remove your address, Google will display your service area instead. If you don’t set one, Google assigns a general area automatically. You can update it later.

## How to Export Contacts in Outlook | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/12976293-how-to-export-contacts-in-outlook

How to Export Contacts in Outlook | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Tutorials 

How to Export Contacts in Outlook 

How to Export Contacts in Outlook 

December 2, 2025 

Table of contents 

You can export your Outlook contacts into a Comma Separated Values (.csv) file and import them into your roomvu Email Marketing campaigns. Follow the steps below to complete the export. 

Export Your Outlook Contacts 

Open Outlook and select File . 

Choose Open & Export , then select Import/Export . 

In the wizard, choose Export to a file , then select Next . 

Select Comma Separated Values , then choose Next . 

Under the email account you want to export from, select Contacts . 

Select Browse and choose the location where you want to save the .csv file. 

Enter a file name, then select OK . 

Select Finish to complete the export. 

Review Your Exported File 

We recommend opening the exported .csv file in Excel before importing it into another program. This allows you to review, clean, or adjust the contact data as needed. 

Notes 

If you are exporting contacts to another Outlook program that is not using Microsoft 365 or Microsoft Exchange, you should export and save your data as a .pst file instead. 

The .csv format is best for transferring contacts to non-Outlook platforms. 

How to Export Contacts from Outlook via Web 

If you use Outlook through a web browser (Outlook.com or Outlook “on the web”), follow these steps to export your contacts as a CSV file before importing to Roomvu. 

Sign in to your Outlook.com or Outlook on the web account. 

In the left-side navigation panel, click the People (or Contacts ) icon to open your contacts list. 

On the toolbar, click Manage contacts (or Manage ) → then select Export contacts . 

Choose whether you want to export All contacts or only contacts from a specific folder. 

Click Export . The contacts will download as a .csv file to your computer (typically into your Downloads folder). 

Open the downloaded .csv file (for example in Excel), review the data, then clean or reformat it as needed before importing into Roomvu.

## How to Clean and Optimize Your CSV Contacts for Email Marketing Using ChatGPT | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/12985903-how-to-clean-and-optimize-your-csv-contacts-for-email-marketing-using-chatgpt

How to Clean and Optimize Your CSV Contacts for Email Marketing Using ChatGPT | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Tutorials 

How to Clean and Optimize Your CSV Contacts for Email Marketing Using ChatGPT 

How to Clean and Optimize Your CSV Contacts for Email Marketing Using ChatGPT 

A step-by-step guide on cleaning, formatting, and standardizing your contact CSV files with AI so they can be successfully imported into Roomvu’s Email Marketing and CRM Lite tools. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Overview 

For best performance, Roomvu requires your contacts to follow a clean and consistent structure. Contacts that come from platforms like Google, Yahoo, Outlook, Apple, or CRM exports usually include many unnecessary columns, missing fields, duplicates, or multiple phone and email formats. 

This guide explains how to use ChatGPT (or any AI text assistant) to quickly clean, standardize, and format your CSV contact files so they are ready for import into Roomvu’s Email Marketing and CRM Lite tools. 

Why You Need a Clean CSV 

Roomvu requires a simple and strict column structure for contacts. Your CSV file must include these four fields only: 

First Name 

Last Name 

Email 

Phone Number 

Any other fields should be removed, and inconsistent data must be consolidated. AI tools such as ChatGPT can perform this cleanup automatically. 

Step 1: Prepare Your CSV File 

Export your contacts from the source platform (Google, Yahoo, Outlook, etc.). 

Save the file as CSV (comma-separated values) . 

Upload the CSV file into your ChatGPT conversation or the AI tool you are using. 

Most exported CSV files contain dozens of columns such as “Home Phone”, “Business Phone”, “Mobile”, “E-mail Address 2”, “Company”, “Notes”, etc. The goal is to simplify these into the four fields required by Roomvu. 

Step 2: Give ChatGPT the Correct Cleaning Instructions 

Use the following instruction template when you upload your CSV: 

Instruction Template: 

​ 

“Please clean this CSV file and restructure it for Roomvu import. Create a new CSV with only these columns: First Name, Last Name, Email, Phone Number. 

For Email, choose the best available value by prioritizing: E-mail Address, then E-mail Address 2, then E-mail Address 3. 

For Phone Number, choose the best option by prioritizing: Mobile Phone, then Home Phone, then Business Phone, then Business Phone 2. 

Remove rows that contain neither email nor phone. 

Keep the formatting clean. 

Save the result as a new CSV file.” 

ChatGPT will analyze all columns and automatically pick the correct fields. 

Step 3: Review and Download the Cleaned CSV 

After ChatGPT cleans the file: 

Review the preview to ensure names, emails, and phone numbers look correct. 

Download the final cleaned CSV file provided by ChatGPT. 

This new CSV is now compatible with Roomvu’s systems. 

Step 4: Import the File Into Roomvu 

Once the file is cleaned: 

Open your roomvu dashboard. 

In the left sidebar, go to Email Newsletters . 

Click "Contacts List" 

Click " Upload Contact CSV" 

Click " Choose your email contacts csv" 

Browse for the file, choose it and it is done. 

​ 

3. Remove duplicates 

AI tools can identify and remove duplicate rows or duplicate emails. 

​ 

4. Prioritize mobile numbers 

Mobile numbers convert better for SMS campaigns and lead follow-up. 

5. Avoid blank email or blank phone rows 

Roomvu requires at least one usable field. 

Example: What ChatGPT Did For You 

Here is the exact logic used when cleaning your sample file: 

Extracted First Name and Last Name as-is. 

Selected Email from three possible columns. 

Selected Phone Number from four different phone number fields. 

Removed empty and unusable rows. 

Exported a clean file: 

First Name | Last Name | Email | Phone Number 

This same process can be applied to any user’s CSV file regardless of the source. 

Advanced Tip: Ask ChatGPT to Validate Data 

You can also ask the AI to: 

Identify invalid emails 

Format phone numbers to international standards 

Detect missing names 

Flag contacts that may be duplicates 

Normalize capitalization (e.g., “john SMITH” → “John Smith”) 

Example instruction: 

“Please clean the CSV and also standardize phone formatting, fix capitalization in names, and give me a list of rows that might be duplicates.” 

Conclusion 

Using ChatGPT to clean contact lists saves significant time and removes the risk of invalid uploads. Once your CSV is simplified to Roomvu’s required structure, your email marketing and CRM features will work smoothly and efficiently.

## What To Do With Leads Roomvu Generates | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/12986037-what-to-do-with-leads-roomvu-generates

What To Do With Leads Roomvu Generates | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Lead Management 

What To Do With Leads Roomvu Generates 

What To Do With Leads Roomvu Generates 

December 2, 2025 

Table of contents 

When Roomvu generates a lead, many agents expect the person to be ready to buy or sell immediately. In reality, most leads are early-stage contacts who need time, visibility, and consistent nurturing before they are ready to work with you. 

This article explains how the lead journey works, why most leads are not ready right away, and what you should do to activate and convert them using Roomvu’s automated tools and your personal engagement. 

Understanding the Lead Funnel 

Roomvu helps you capture new leads, but converting them requires moving them through several stages of the lead funnel. Each stage has a different purpose and expectation. 

Stage 1: Unaware 

People encounter you for the first time. They may see your content, meet you at an open house, or come across your ads. At this point, they do not know who you are. 

Stage 2: Connection 

This is where Roomvu generates the lead. 

Your only goal here is to bring them into your ecosystem . 

Examples: 

Collect emails at open houses 

Have them follow you on social media 

Capture basic contact details through Roomvu ads 

At this stage, they are not ready to buy or sell yet . They simply entered your world. 

Stage 3: Awareness 

The priority now is to stay visible so they remember your name. This phase typically lasts 6 to 9 months . 

Actions that matter: 

Posting consistent, high-value content 

Appearing on their feed regularly 

Sharing educational, local, and market-relevant updates 

Roomvu supports you here by publishing hyper-local content to keep you top-of-mind. 

Stage 4: Engagement 

This is where lead activation truly begins. 

A lead clicks, opens an email, follows your page, or interacts with your content. They enter your CRM journey. 

Roomvu’s automated nurture system helps with: 

Weekly email newsletters 

Auto-sending follow-up content 

Reminders and lead notes in CRM Lite 

Your role: 

Respond when they engage 

Start conversations 

Build rapport and trust over time 

Engagement is the bridge between a passive contact and a future client. 

Stage 5: Validation 

Before reaching out, people will: 

Google your name 

Check your social media 

Look at your recent posts 

Judge whether you appear credible and active 

This is why consistent content matters. It strengthens your online presence, which directly impacts whether leads trust you. 

Why Most Leads Are Not Ready Immediately 

Only a very small percentage of leads are ready to buy or sell right away. Most people are: 

Researching 

Exploring options 

Watching the market 

Comparing agents 

Getting familiar with your brand 

📊 What the Data Shows on Lead Conversion Rates 

For the real estate industry the “lead to sale” (i.e. lead becoming a paying client) conversion rate tends to be very low on average: about 0.4% to 1.2% . realoffice360.com 

Some sources of “internet leads” (online leads) report typical conversion ranges between 1% and 3.5% . Ylopo 

Lead quality and source make a substantial difference. For “lower-intent” online leads (e.g. broad PPC or social-media traffic), conversion tends to be on the lower end (≈ 1%). For “higher-intent” leads (for example from portals, direct inquiries, or warm traffic), conversion can rise to 7–9% under high-performing agents/climates. Ylopo 

✅ What “Hot Leads Ready to Take Action Immediately” Typically Means — And How Rare They Are 

Using the above data and industry norms: 

If you capture 100 online leads via broad awareness campaigns (social ads, content marketing, etc.), statistically only about 1–3 leads (1–3 %) will convert into clients, assuming average follow-up and funnel conversion. 

If your leads come from more intent-driven sources (portals, referrals, high-trust ads) and you follow best practices, you might see 7–9 potential clients per 100 leads (7–9 %). 

The vast majority — 90 % to 99 %+ of leads — are not “hot” at first. They require nurturing, follow-up, trust-building, education, and multiple touches over time. 

⚠️ Why the Percentage of “Ready-to-Act” Leads is Usually Very Low 

Real estate is a high-value, low-frequency purchase: buying a house is a major commitment; most people take time to research and reflect before acting. realoffice360.com 

Online leads often enter at the “top of the funnel” — they may know little about you or the market; they need time, content, engagement, and trust building. 

Conversion depends heavily on following a structured nurturing process: frequent contact, consistent content delivery, responsiveness, and credibility. Without that, even high-quality leads remain cold. 

🎯 What This Means for Roomvu Users 

Treat each lead generated by Roomvu as a potential , not a guarantee — expect only a small fraction to be ready to act immediately. 

Use Roomvu’s automated nurture tools to stay visible — but supplement automation with personal outreach, timely follow-ups, and trust-building interactions . 

Focus on lead quality: leads sourced from high-intent channels or with clear purchase/sale signals are more likely to convert than broad awareness-driven leads. 

Manage expectations: conversion is a marathon, not a sprint. Most value comes over time, not immediately after lead generation. 

What You Should Do After Leads Are Generated 

1. Do not expect instant readiness 

A lead entering your system is the start of the relationship, not the end. 

2. Let Roomvu run the automated nurture 

Your leads will: 

Receive weekly emails 

See your automated posts 

Stay in your long-term awareness loop 

This keeps you visible without requiring manual effort. 

3. Engage personally when they interact 

If a lead: 

Opens an email 

Likes your content 

Replies to a message 

Visits your page 

Use it as an opportunity to: 

Start a friendly conversation 

Ask what they are looking for 

Offer helpful information 

Lead activation is a two-way process . 

4. Build trust over time 

Your consistency creates familiarity, and familiarity builds trust. 

Clients choose agents they: 

Recognize 

Remember 

Feel comfortable with 

Your long-term presence is what converts leads into real clients. 

Summary 

Roomvu generates leads so you can fill the top of your funnel. But leads become clients only through consistent nurturing and engagement. 

Leads enter at the Connection stage. 

Your visibility builds Awareness over months. 

Automated nurture and personal outreach create Engagement . 

Your online presence supports Validation . 

Consistency converts strangers into clients. 

Roomvu activates leads for you, but your relationship-building completes the process. 

If you have questions about nurturing your leads or using Roomvu's CRM tools, you can contact our support team anytime. 

Related Articles 

roomvu Leads Journey Builder: Tutorial 

How to Connect Your CRM and Other Tools to roomvu

How Roomvu Landing Pages Capture and Convert Leads Automatically 

Understanding the Lead Funnel and How Roomvu Helps You Nurture Leads

## Why is my TikTok video muted or silent? | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13118635-why-is-my-tiktok-video-muted-or-silent

Why is my TikTok video muted or silent? | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Social media 

Why is my TikTok video muted or silent? 

Why is my TikTok video muted or silent? 

December 10, 2025 

Table of contents 

TikTok may remove or mute your audio if the system detects a copyright issue or a violation of its rules. When this happens, you might see a notice on your video that says the sound was removed or muted. 

What are your options after your sound is muted 

If your video loses its audio due to copyright, you can replace the audio by choosing a new track from TikTok’s music library. This is the fastest way to “revive” your video without deleting it. 

How to replace the audio on a muted TikTok video (step-by-step) 

Follow these steps to restore a muted video with a new audio track: 

Open the TikTok app and go to your muted video. 

Tap the notice on the video that explains the audio was removed. 

If the removal was due to copyright, select “Change sound” or “Replace sound.” 

Browse TikTok’s audio library and choose a new track. If available, trim the sound and adjust volume. 

Tap “Post” or “Save changes” to apply the new audio. 

Note: The new sound applies only to this individual video. If you posted the same original audio in multiple videos, you will need to repeat the process for each.

Vu Card: Your Online Business Card 

Create, customize, and share a powerful online business card that helps people instantly connect with you. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

What Is Vu Card and Why an Online Business Card Matters 

An online business card is no longer optional. People discover you through social media, websites, ads, and emails, and they expect instant access to your information. 

Vu Card is roomvu’s built-in online business card that gives every user a unique, shareable link. Anyone who clicks that link can view your professional profile and contact you within seconds. No downloads, no ads, and no paid upgrades. 

Click to see Vu Card in action 

Unlike many standalone online business card tools that charge monthly fees or display ads, Vu Card is completely free for all roomvu users. 

From Instagram bios to email signatures, wherever you can paste a link, your online business card can live there. 

What Makes Vu Card a Powerful Online Business Card 

Vu Card is designed to be simple, fast, and conversion-focused. It works perfectly on mobile screens and desktop devices, so your online business card always looks professional. 

Here is what your Vu Card includes: 

Your profile photo or AI Avatar 

Your full name and brokerage information 

One-tap call and email buttons 

Links to all your social media profiles and pages 

A button to download and share your VCF contact file 

A share button to send your online business card instantly 

Your total number of listings 

Your online review ratings 

Your professional bio 

Everything someone needs to know about you is available in one clean, responsive online business card. 

Click to see the Vu Card 

Why Vu Card Is Better Than Other Online Business Card Tools 

Most online business card platforms come with limitations. Some require payment. Others add ads. Many do not integrate well with your existing marketing tools. 

Vu Card is different. 

It is completely free 

It has no ads 

It is already connected to your roomvu profile 

It is optimized for mobile screens 

It is easy to update anytime 

Your online business card stays up to date without extra tools or subscriptions. 

How to Access Your Vu Card in roomvu 

Setting up your online business card takes only a few minutes. 

Follow these steps to access Vu Card: 

Log in to your roomvu account 

Click the Gear icon in the top-right corner 

Scroll all the way down to find the Vu Card section 

Click on Vu Card to open your online business card settings 

From here, you can review and customize everything that appears on your online business card. 

How to Customize Your Online Business Card for Better Results 

To make your Vu Card more effective, take time to complete each section carefully. 

Update Your Profile Photo 

Make sure your profile photo or AI Avatar looks professional and approachable. This is often the first thing people notice on your online business card. 

Add Your Business Information 

Check your name, brokerage details, and contact information. Accuracy builds trust and avoids missed opportunities. 

Connect Your Social Media Accounts 

Add the URLs to your social media profiles so visitors can explore your content and follow you easily from your online business card. 

Write an Engaging Bio 

Your bio should explain who you help, what you do, and why people should trust you. A strong bio increases conversions and encourages contact. 

Add Your Slogan and Website 

Your slogan reinforces your brand, and your website link gives visitors a deeper look into your services. 

Every update you make improves how your online business card performs. 

How to Share Your Vu Card Everywhere 

Each Vu Card comes with a unique link. 

Click the copy button in front of your link and share this online business card link anywhere, including: 

Social media bios 

Direct messages 

Email signatures 

Websites and landing pages 

Digital ads 

QR codes 

Once someone clicks your online business card link, they can call, email, save your contact, or explore your profile instantly. 

Turn Every Click Into a Connection 

Vu Card is more than just an online business card. It is a simple way to turn attention into real conversations. 

With one free link, you give people instant access to your contact details, social presence, listings, reviews, and story. No friction. No distractions. Just a clean and professional online business card that works wherever you share it. 

If you are already using roomvu, your online business card is ready. All you need to do is customize it and start sharing.

## How to Find and Share Your Google Business Review Link | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13187038-how-to-find-and-share-your-google-business-review-link

How to Find and Share Your Google Business Review Link | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Video Guides 

How to Find and Share Your Google Business Review Link 

How to Find and Share Your Google Business Review Link 

Learn how to find and share your Google Business Profile review link so clients can leave a Google review quickly and easily with one click. 

February 2, 2026 

Table of contents 

What This Is and Why It Matters 

A Google review link is a special URL that takes someone directly to your Google Business Profile’s review form. When a past client clicks this link, they don’t have to search for your business or navigate Google — they go straight to leaving a review. This is especially useful for real estate agents who want to ask clients for feedback after a sale or closing. 

Before You Begin: Make Sure You Have a Google Business Profile 

To use this feature, your business must have: 

A Google Business Profile (formerly known as Google My Business) 

Your business profile verified on Google 

If you haven’t set one up yet, you can create it for free at business.google.com. Reviews can only be left on verified listings. Google Help 

Step-by-Step: Get Your Direct Review Link 

Make sure that you are signed in to the same Google account on your browser. 

Option 1: From Google Search (Easiest) 

Open Google Search 

On a desktop or mobile browser, search your business name exactly as it appears on your Google Business Profile. 

Find Your Business Panel 

Your business’s profile should appear in the search results panel. 

Click “Write a review” or “Ask for reviews” 

This button opens the review prompt. 

Copy the URL 

When the review window pops up, copy the URL from the browser’s address bar — this is your direct review link. 

Option 2: From Your Google Business Profile Dashboard 

Sign in to business.google.com 

Use the Google account that manages your business listing. 

Select your business 

(Only necessary if you manage multiple locations.) 

This will take you to your business profile above. Follow the same steps. 

Option 3: Use Google Maps or Place ID (Alternative) 

If you don’t see a direct review link in the dashboard: 

Search for your business in Google Maps 

Open your business listing 

Click the Share button 

Copy the link from the share popup — this will take users to your business profile where they can hit “Write a review.” 

Alternate advanced option 

Use the Google Place ID Finder tool and generate a direct review URL using this format: 

https://search.google.com/local/writereview?placeid=YOUR_PLACE_ID 

Replace YOUR_PLACE_ID with the ID for your business listing. This also creates a direct review form link. 

Tips to Share Your Review Link 

Once you have your review link, you can share it many ways to encourage reviews: 

✔ In follow-up emails to clients 

✔ SMS or text message after closing or service 

✔ Thank-you cards or printed materials 

✔ Email signature 

✔ Social media posts 

✔ QR codes on business cards or signage (generate a QR from your link) 

Best Practices for Agents 

Always follow up soon after a positive client experience when reviews are most fresh. 

Keep your message personal and polite (don’t offer incentives — Google’s policies prohibit that). 

Explain how much reviews help your business and other home buyers/sellers. 

Summary 

Getting your Google review link is a simple but powerful way to boost your online reputation and collect more client feedback . The direct review link brings clients straight to your review form — no extra searching or steps required, making it far more convenient for them to leave a review. 

Related Articles

## Roomvu Website Product: Setup, Ownership, and What to Expect | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13224775-roomvu-website-product-setup-ownership-and-what-to-expect

Roomvu Website Product: Setup, Ownership, and What to Expect | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Features 

Roomvu Website Product: Setup, Ownership, and What to Expect 

Roomvu Website Product: Setup, Ownership, and What to Expect 

Learn how the Roomvu Website works, including domain responsibility, hosting limitations, MLS fees, and what happens if your subscription ends. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Website Offering Overview 

roomvu provides a templated, managed website with daily hyper-local content publishing to the website blog. This product is not a fully custom website build and is delivered as a managed service. 

Value: $300/year 

Customization: Limited (layout, structure, and core features are standardized) 

A. Domain Ownership & Responsibility 

Option 1: Agent purchases their own domain (recommended) 

The agent is fully responsible for purchasing and maintaining their domain. 

The agent must point DNS settings to roomvu following published instructions. 

roomvu does not manage domain purchases, renewals, or DNS accounts . 

Instructions: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/9492466-how-to-set-your-website-dns 

Option 2: roomvu purchases the domain (optional) 

If roomvu purchases the domain on behalf of the agent: 

roomvu remains the legal owner of the domain. 

The domain is licensed to the agent only while their Platinum subscription is active . 

If the subscription ends, the domain and website are terminated unless otherwise agreed in writing. 

Hosting, Integration & Limitations 

The website is: 

Hosted on roomvu infrastructure 

Delivered as a managed service 

Agents cannot migrate the website to their own hosting environment. 

Core structure, templates, and automation cannot be altered . 

A WordPress-based blog interface is provided for optional manual posting by the agent. 

Third-party plugins, themes, or custom backend access are not supported . 

Termination, Ownership & Transition 

Website Content 

roomvu retains ownership of: 

Website framework 

Templates 

Automation systems 

Agent retains rights to: 

Their branding 

Their authored content (subject to platform format limitations) 

If the agent cancels: 

Website hosting is terminated. 

If the agent wishes to retain the website : 

They may continue the website at $300/year 

PLUS any applicable MLS IDX fees 

Website migration to external hosting is not available . 

Connecting an Existing Website 

roomvu does not connect to or host existing websites . 

Existing WordPress, Magento, Wix, Squarespace, or custom websites: 

Cannot be integrated or mirrored 

Cannot receive roomvu automation natively 

Only DNS routing to a roomvu-hosted site is supported. 

Email & Domain-Based Email 

roomvu does not provide email hosting . 

Agents are responsible for: 

Google Workspace 

Microsoft 365 

Or other email providers 

DNS email records (MX) remain under the agent’s control. 

SEO & Search Rankings 

roomvu websites include: 

Consistent publishing 

SEO-friendly structure 

No guarantees are made regarding: 

Rankings 

Traffic 

Lead volume 

SEO performance depends on: 

Domain age 

Market competition 

Agent activity 

Upon termination: 

Search rankings may decline 

URLs may de-index over time 

MLS / IDX Fees (Important) 

If an MLS provider: 

Does not charge for website/IDX URLs → roomvu does not charge 

Does charge (e.g. $15 per URL) → Agent must pay MLS directly 

MLS fees are: 

Not included in the $300 website fee 

Non-refundable 

Subject to MLS rules and changes 

Using roomvu with an Existing Website 

If you already have a website, Roomvu does not replace or take over your existing hosting. Roomvu offers a WordPress plugin that can be installed on your own WordPress site to publish content. For non-WordPress websites, Roomvu provides API access only . API usage requires your own development resources, as Roomvu does not provide custom implementation, programming, or technical support for third-party integrations. Roomvu is not responsible for compatibility, performance, or SEO outcomes on externally hosted websites using the plugin or API. 

Brokerages and Teams: Website Integration Options 

Website integration options beyond the WordPress plugin are available only for brokerages and teams . These integrations may include expanded content distribution or API-based connections, subject to separate agreements and technical requirements. Individual agents are supported exclusively through the WordPress plugin and do not have access to brokerage- or team-level integrations. Any API usage for brokerages or teams must be implemented and maintained by their own technical resources, as Roomvu does not provide custom development or ongoing support for external website environments. 

2. Website Product – FAQ 

What exactly am I getting? 

A professionally branded website with daily hyper-local blog content , hosted and managed by roomvu. 

Can I fully customize the website? 

No. This is a templated product designed for speed, automation, and consistency. 

Who owns my domain? 

You own it if you buy it. 

roomvu owns it if we buy it for you. 

Can I move my website to another host later? 

No. The website is a managed service and cannot be exported. 

Can I connect my existing website? 

No. Existing sites cannot be hosted or synced. 

What happens if I cancel my subscription? 

Website is terminated 

You may continue it for $300/year + MLS fees 

Domains owned by roomvu are released 

Do you manage my MLS IDX fees? 

No. All MLS IDX fees are paid directly by you to your MLS. 

Will this help my SEO? 

It supports SEO best practices, but results are not guaranteed . 

Website Product Terms 

1. Website Service Description 

roomvu provides a managed website product consisting of a standardized website framework with automated content publishing. Custom development, custom hosting, or migration services are not included. 

2. Domain Registration 

Customers are responsible for purchasing and maintaining their own domain unless explicitly purchased by roomvu. Domains purchased by roomvu remain the sole property of roomvu Technologies Inc. and are licensed to the customer only for the duration of an active subscription. 

3. DNS Configuration 

Customers are solely responsible for configuring DNS settings in accordance with roomvu’s published instructions. roomvu does not provide domain registrar support or DNS troubleshooting beyond documentation. 

4. Hosting & Access 

All websites are hosted on roomvu infrastructure. Customers may not export, clone, or transfer the website to third-party hosting environments. 

5. Content & IP 

roomvu retains all rights to website templates, layouts, automation systems, and proprietary technology. Customers retain rights to their branding and authored content submitted through the platform. 

6. Termination 

Upon cancellation or expiration: 

Website hosting may be terminated 

Continued hosting may be offered at roomvu’s then-current pricing 

No refunds are provided for unused periods 

7. MLS & IDX Fees 

MLS and IDX fees are not included unless explicitly stated. Any MLS-imposed charges must be paid directly by the customer and are subject to MLS rules and changes. 

8. SEO Disclaimer 

roomvu does not guarantee search engine rankings, traffic levels, or lead generation outcomes. 

9. Email Services 

roomvu does not provide email hosting or domain-based email services.
