Why You’re Receiving Calls from the Roomvu Support Team 

Why You’re Receiving Calls from the Roomvu Support Team 

March 30, 2026 

Table of contents 

When you log into your roomvu account, our Support & SDR (Sales Development Representative) team may reach out to you. These calls are not sales pressure —they’re part of our onboarding and support process to make sure you’re getting full value from the platform. 

Here’s how it works: 

Calls are triggered only after you log in to the Roomvu platform 

Our team’s role is to: 

Help you get fully onboarded 

Walk you through features and benefits included at no cost , courtesy of your brokerage (if your brokerage has an agreement with us) 

Answer questions and make sure your account is set up properly 

Support outreach happens at most once every two weeks 

No agent is contacted more than once for the same reason or conversation 

The goal is to ensure you can confidently use the platform and enjoy all included benefits 

Want Fewer or No Calls? 

That’s completely okay. 

You can simply tell our team that you’d like to be added to our Do-Not-Disturb (DND) list 

Once noted, we’ll respect that preference moving forward 

Important to Know 

These calls are support-initiated , not random 

They exist to help you succeed with the tools already available to you 

If you ever have questions, our team is there as a resource—not an obligation

## How to Manage Your AI Portraits in roomvu | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13351022-how-to-manage-your-ai-portraits-in-roomvu

How to Manage Your AI Portraits in roomvu | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard

How to Manage Your AI Portraits in roomvu 

How to Manage Your AI Portraits in roomvu 

Learn how to edit your AI Portraits or add new ones. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

AI Portraits let you create professional, on-brand profile images using AI. You can generate new portraits, change the photo used to create them, set a default image, download them, or turn the feature off at any time. 

This guide shows you exactly how to manage everything in one place. 

Where to Find Your AI Portraits 

All AI Portrait controls are inside your account settings. 

To open them: 

Click the Gear icon in the top-right corner of your roomvu dashboard to enter " Settings " 

In the left menu under Profile , click AI Portraits . 

You will now see all of your generated AI Portrait images in one gallery. 

How to Generate New AI Portraits 

You can generate new AI portraits every week using your current profile photo. 

To create new portraits: 

Click Generate . 

The system will create new AI portraits based on your current profile photo. 

Adjust the settings and Generate Portrait. 

Want different results? 

Change your profile photo first, then click Generate again. The AI will use the new photo to create a different style of portraits. 

How to Set a Default AI Portrait 

Your default AI portrait is the one used across roomvu in videos, profiles, and content. 

To set a default: 

Go to Settings > Profile > AI Portraits . 

Click the three-dot menu on any image. 

Click Set as default . 

That image is now your main AI portrait. 

How to Download an AI Portrait 

You can download any portrait to use on other platforms. 

Click the three-dot menu on the image. 

Click Download . 

Save it to your device. 

How to Delete an AI Portrait 

If you do not like an image, you can remove it. 

Click the three-dot menu on the image. 

Click Delete . 

Confirm the action. 

The image will be permanently removed from your gallery. 

How to Disable AI Portraits 

If you want to stop using AI Portraits completely: 

Go to Settings > Profile > AI Portraits . 

Toggle Disable AI-Portraits . 

This turns off the feature and prevents AI portraits from being used in your content. 

You can re-enable it later at any time. 

What You Can Do from the AI Portraits Page 

From Settings > Profile > AI Portraits , you can: 

View all your AI portraits 

Generate new portraits 

Change which photo is used 

Set a default portrait 

Download images 

Delete unwanted images 

Disable AI Portraits 

Everything is managed from this one screen.

## Organic vs Paid Advertising | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13397065-organic-vs-paid-advertising

Organic vs Paid Advertising | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Lead Management 

Organic vs Paid Advertising 

Organic vs Paid Advertising 

Understanding how each one works inside roomvu 

January 15, 2026 

Table of contents 

What is Organic Advertising 

Organic advertising is when your content reaches people naturally, without paying for distribution. 

On roomvu, this means your videos, posts, and updates are shared on your social media profiles and discovered by people who already follow you or find your content through platform algorithms. 

Examples of organic reach include: 

Your followers seeing your Instagram Reel 

Someone discovering your post through hashtags 

A past client watching your video on Facebook 

A LinkedIn connection seeing your market update 

You are not paying the platform to show this content. The reach comes from engagement, consistency, and how relevant the content is to viewers. 

Organic content builds trust over time. People get familiar with your face, your voice, and your message. This is how personal brands grow. 

What is Paid Advertising 

Paid advertising is when you pay a platform like Facebook, Instagram, or Google to show your content to specific people. 

Instead of waiting for algorithms or followers, you choose: 

Who sees your ad 

Where they live 

Their age range 

Their interests 

Their behavior 

roomvu uses your videos, AI Avatar, listings, and branding to create ads that are delivered to targeted audiences. 

Paid ads allow you to reach: 

People who do not follow you 

Homeowners in specific ZIP codes 

Buyers or sellers in your market 

People actively browsing real estate 

This is how you get new leads, not just views. 

The Core Difference 

The simplest way to understand it is this: 

Organic 

Paid 

Uses your social media audience 

Uses advertising platforms 

Free distribution 

Budget-based distribution 

Grows slowly 

Scales fast 

Builds long-term trust 

Drives immediate exposure 

Depends on algorithms 

You control who sees it 

Both use the same content. The difference is how that content is delivered. 

How roomvu Uses Both 

roomvu is designed to combine organic and paid advertising into one system. 

When you publish a video: 

It posts organically to your social profiles 

The same content can also be turned into paid ads 

Your AI Avatar, voice, and branding stay consistent across both 

This means your audience sees you everywhere in a unified way. 

Your followers see your posts. 

New people see you through ads. 

Both reinforce each other. 

Why Organic Alone Is Not Enough 

Organic reach is limited by platform algorithms. 

Even if you have 5,000 followers: 

Only a small percentage see each post 

New people rarely find you 

Growth is slow 

Organic is great for staying visible. 

It is not reliable for generating leads. 

Why Paid Alone Is Not Enough 

Ads without organic presence feel less trustworthy. 

When someone sees your ad, they often: 

Click your profile 

Look for more content 

Want to see if you are real and active 

If your social pages are empty or inconsistent, trust drops. 

That is why roomvu always runs both together. 

How This Affects Your Results 

The highest performing agents use this model: 

Organic builds familiarity. 

Paid creates discovery. 

When people see you in ads and also see you posting regularly, your brand becomes recognizable and credible. 

That is how strangers turn into leads. 

Summary 

Organic advertising helps you stay visible to people who already know you. 

Paid advertising helps you reach people who have never heard of you. 

roomvu connects both into one system so your content works everywhere without extra effort.

roomvu Smart Ads 

roomvu Referral Program: Empower Your Network and Reap Rewards 

Why Your Facebook Business Page Doesn’t Get Organic Engagement 

What Is the Difference Between roomvu's Organic Content and Smart Ads?

## How to Modify Content Topics on Your Content Calendar | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13430529-how-to-modify-content-topics-on-your-content-calendar

How to Modify Content Topics on Your Content Calendar 

How to Modify Content Topics on Your Content Calendar 

Learn how to update your roomvu content calendar topics, adjust language and business settings, and add custom or AI-generated content when needed. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Your content calendar is fully customisable. If the topics you see do not match your business, language, or audience, you can easily adjust them from your calendar settings or add custom content at any time. 

This guide shows you how to do both. 

Accessing Your Content Calendar Settings 

Log in to your roomvu account. 

From your main dashboard, click Content Calendar in the left-hand menu. 

On the Content Calendar page, find Calendar Settings . 

Click Edit next to it. 

A popup window will open with multiple configuration sections. 

Content Tab Settings 

Inside the popup window, go to the Content tab. This is where you control the type of content that appears on your calendar. 

Second Language Content 

If you want content in more than one language, you can manage it here. 

Choose a second language from a list of more than 20 available languages 

Adjust how often second-language posts appear on your calendar 

Set the frequency from Low to High based on your audience needs 

This is useful if you serve multilingual communities or want to expand your reach. 

Account Type (Business Type) 

Your account type determines the topics and messaging used in your content. 

You can select the business category that best fits your work, such as: 

Real estate agent 

Broker 

Mortgage broker 

Financial advisor 

Insurance agent 

And more 

If your content does not feel relevant, your account type may be misconfigured. Updating this setting ensures your calendar delivers content aligned with your profession. 

Adding a Specific Topic or Custom Content 

If you ever need content on a very specific topic, you do not have to rely only on automatic calendar settings. 

You can add custom content directly from your Content Calendar. 

Go to Content Calendar from the left menu. 

Click Add Content . 

From here, you have multiple options: 

Choose from available roomvu content types 

Add content using a link 

Use AI to generate a unique piece of content based on your chosen topic 

This gives you full control when you want to cover timely updates, niche topics, or custom messaging. 

Save and Review Your Calendar 

After updating your settings or adding custom content: 

Save your changes 

Review your calendar to confirm the topics match your goals 

Your calendar will update automatically based on your selections. 

When to Review These Settings 

It is a good idea to check your calendar settings if: 

Your content feels off-topic 

You change industries or roles 

You want to add or fine-tune multilingual content 

You need to publish content around a specific topic 

Keeping these settings up to date ensures your content calendar stays aligned with your business and audience.

How to Manage Your Listings in roomvu 

How to Manage Your Listings in roomvu 

Learn how to import, organise, edit, promote, and share your MLS listings in roomvu, including Listing Studio, Immersive Tours, co-branding, and Facebook Ads. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Managing your listings in roomvu is simple and flexible. From importing properties to creating videos, running ads, and sharing listings across channels, everything is handled from one place. This guide walks you through every option available so you can get the most visibility and value from your listings. 

Accessing Your MLS Listings 

Log in to your roomvu account. 

From the home page, click MLS Listings in the left-hand menu. 

This section is your central hub for importing, editing, promoting, and sharing all your property listings. 

Enable or Disable Co-Branding to Increase Reach 

When you enter the MLS Listings page, you may see a prompt asking if you would like to increase your reach by sharing your listings with qualified local professionals, such as mortgage brokers and insurance agents. 

Co-branding allows these professionals to co-promote your listings to their own audiences, helping your properties reach a broader and more relevant local market. 

To turn this feature on or off, use the Enable Co-Branding toggle at the top left corner of the page. 

You can enable or disable this option at any time. 

Importing Your Listings 

To add new listings, click Import Listing at the top right corner of the page. You have several ways to import listings, depending on your preference. 

Option 1: Import Using MLS Listing ID 

Paste the MLS Listing ID into the field at the top. 

roomvu will automatically pull the listing data and media. 

Option 2: Import Automatically From Supported Platforms 

You can automatically pull your listings from supported platforms, including: 

Zillow 

Realtor.com 

Realtor.ca 

Zillow Profile 

This is the recommended method, as it ensures your listing details and photos are imported accurately and quickly. 

Option 3: Add a Listing Manually 

You can also add listings manually by uploading photos and entering all listing information yourself. 

This method requires manual entry of all details. 

It is not recommended unless other import options are unavailable. 

Filtering and Organising Your Listings 

Once your listings are imported, you can easily organise them by status using the available filters. Listing types include: 

Active 

Inactive 

Under Contract 

Just Sold 

Leased 

Each listing type comes with its own content templates, allowing roomvu to generate more relevant and timely content automatically. 

Managing Individual Listings 

Each listing includes multiple tools and actions to help you customise, promote, and distribute your content. 

Delete a Listing 

Click the Trash icon to permanently delete a listing you no longer need. 

Edit Listings and Use Listing Studio 

By clicking Edit or Listing Studio , you can fully customise your listing content: 

Select brand colours 

Change video or image templates 

Add a personal intro for the listing (highly recommended) 

Virtually stage or redecorate listing photos 

Add a unique agent headshot for the listing 

Edit listing information and details 

Edit, reorder, or replace listing photos 

Write a custom outro text for the listing video 

These options allow you to tailor each listing to your personal brand and marketing style. 

Create an Immersive Tour 

roomvu’s Immersive Tour feature allows you to create a short listing video with your AI speaking avatar and cloned voice. 

Click the Immersive Tour button on a listing. 

The video is generated automatically in about a minute. 

This feature helps you present your listings in a more engaging and personalised way, without manual recording or editing. 

Run Ads for Your Listings 

You can promote your listings using roomvu’s Facebook Ads directly from the listing page. 

With just a few clicks, you can: 

Set or edit the ad location 

Choose the duration of the campaign 

Define a daily ad budget 

roomvu handles the content creation, ad setup, and optimisation for you. You will also see estimated reach and performance metrics before launching the ad. 

Additional Actions Using the Three-Dots Menu 

By clicking the three-dots menu on a listing, you can access more sharing and scheduling options: 

Include the listing in a newsletter 

Schedule open house content 

Schedule the listing content to be shared later on your content calendar 

Copy the roomvu listing link to share manually via social media, email, or other channels 

Download Listing Content 

If you prefer to share your content manually, you can download your listing assets at any time. 

Click the Download button on the listing. 

Use the downloaded content for manual posting on social media, email campaigns, or other platforms. 

Final Notes 

Your MLS Listings section in roomvu is designed to give you full control over how your properties are presented, promoted, and shared. By using automated imports, personalized content, immersive tours, and built-in advertising tools, you can maximise exposure while saving time and effort.

## How to Reschedule Your Roomvu VIP Support Session | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13515743-how-to-reschedule-your-roomvu-vip-support-session

How to Reschedule Your Roomvu VIP Support Session | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Tutorials 

How to Reschedule Your Roomvu VIP Support Session 

How to Reschedule Your Roomvu VIP Support Session 

Learn how to reschedule your Roomvu VIP Support Session by booking a new time through Get VIP Help, plus tips to prepare for your video call and avoid cancellations. 

March 24, 2026 

Table of contents 

VIP Support Sessions are live video calls where our support team helps you step by step. To keep the experience smooth and high-quality for everyone, we offer a limited number of sessions per day. That’s why we strongly recommend booking a time you are 100% sure you can attend. 

Before You Book (Important) 

To get the most out of your VIP Support Session, please make sure you are fully prepared before your call. 

✅ Pick a time you can attend with no interruptions 

VIP Support Sessions are reserved just for you. If you miss your session, that time slot cannot be easily replaced. 

✅ Have your login details ready 

Before your session starts, prepare any necessary credentials, such as: 

Social media usernames and passwords 

Email login details (if needed) 

Any tools/accounts connected to your Roomvu account 

✅ Use an up-to-date computer and browser 

For the best experience, we recommend: 

A working laptop or desktop computer 

Google Chrome installed (preferred) 

A stable internet connection 

Camera and microphone working properly 

Avoid Cancelling Unless It’s Truly Necessary 

Because VIP Support Sessions are limited daily, we ask users to avoid cancelling unless it is absolutely unavoidable. 

Cancelling last minute can prevent other users from getting help sooner, and it may delay your own support progress as well. 

How to Reschedule Your VIP Support Session 

If you still need to reschedule, you’ll need to book a new time through your dashboard. 

Step 1: Log in to your Roomvu account 

Go to your Roomvu dashboard. 

Step 2: Click Get VIP Help 

On the top-right corner on your dashboard, click Get VIP Help . 

Step 3: Choose a new day and time 

This will take you to the booking page, where you can view the latest available time slots. 

Step 4: Confirm your booking 

Pick the new time that works for you and complete the booking. 

Can Roomvu Reschedule Sessions Manually? 

At the moment, we cannot reschedule sessions manually. 

This means: 

We cannot adjust your booked time by a few minutes 

We cannot move your session to the next hour or next day 

We cannot accept rescheduling requests through support chat or email 

VIP Support availability changes constantly, and the only accurate schedule is shown on the booking page. 

To reschedule, you must book again through Get VIP Help in your dashboard. 

Quick Tips for a Successful Session 

Before your call starts, we recommend you: 

Log in to your Roomvu account in advance 

Log in to your social accounts if needed 

Keep your passwords ready (or saved securely) 

Close unnecessary apps and tabs to avoid slowing down your system

## How to Stop roomvu From Posting to Your Social Media | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13531944-how-to-stop-roomvu-from-posting-to-your-social-media

How to Stop roomvu From Posting to Your Social Media | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Tutorials 

How to Stop roomvu From Posting to Your Social Media 

How to Stop roomvu From Posting to Your Social Media 

Learn how to pause Roomvu content sharing, so roomvu stops auto-posting to Instagram, Facebook, LinkedIn, and more anytime you need. 

Updated yesterday 

Table of contents 

Sometimes you may need to pause your roomvu content from being shared to social media. This can happen for different reasons, such as: 

You updated your contact info and want your designs to reflect the new details 

You need a break from posting for personal reasons 

You want to stop posting on one platform only (like Instagram, Facebook, or LinkedIn) 

✅ You can Pause your content calendar up to 90 days right from your dashboard. 

Important to Know Before You Start 

roomvu cannot stop posting on your behalf, even if you contact our team. 

To pause your content sharing, you need to Pause your calendar yourself. 

How to Stop Roomvu From Posting (Disconnect Social Media) 

Step 1: Log in to your Roomvu account 

Go to your Roomvu dashboard and make sure you are logged in. 

Step 2: Click Content Calendar 

On the left menu, click " Content Calendar ". 

Step 3: Pause Calendar 

On top of your Content Calendar , click "Pause Calendar". 

Then enter a time period for your calendar to pause. You can Pause your Calendar up to 90 days. 

What Happens After You Disconnect? 

When your Pause your Content Calendar: 

✅ Roomvu will stop auto-sharing new posts for you. 

✅ Your content calendar can still continue generating content inside your account 

✅ You can resume your calendar anytime when you are ready to start posting again. 

Need to Pause Posting Temporarily? 

If you are only taking a short break, you can Pause your calendar now and resume later whenever you are ready to resume posting. 

If you are pausing because your branding or contact details changed, pausing prevents old info from being posted until everything is updated.

How to Update Your Branded Video Intro (Contact Info, Photo, or Brokerage Logo) 

Learn how to update your Roomvu branded video intro if your contact info, headshot, or brokerage logo has changed, including how to email info@roomvu.com. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Your branded intro is the custom-designed section that appears at the beginning of your Roomvu videos. It includes your personal branding elements such as your name, contact details, headshot, and brokerage logo. 

Sometimes, users need to update these details, especially when they: 

Change their phone number, email, or website 

Update their headshot or profile photo 

Join a new brokerage or rebrand with a new logo 

Want new branding information added to their intro 

This guide explains how to request an updated branded intro. 

​ 

Important: Branded Intros Are Not Updated Automatically 

Your branded video intro is designed by the Roomvu team and is not dynamic . 

That means even if you update your profile info or logo inside your Roomvu account, those changes will not automatically apply to your existing branded intro. 

​ 

✅ To update your branded intro, our team needs to create a new version for you. 

Email Our Team 

To request changes to your branded intro, email us at: 

info@roomvu.com 

What to include in your email 

To avoid delays, make sure your email includes: 

A clear request (what you want updated) 

Your new contact details (exactly how you want them shown) 

Your new logo or brokerage logo attached (if applicable) 

Your updated headshot/profile photo attached (if needed) 

✅ The more complete your email is, the faster our team can process your request. 

Please Note: Updates May Take Some Time 

Because your branded intro requires manual design work, updates are not immediate . 

⏳ Your request may take a little while to complete depending on the design workload and the details needed. 

Need Help Choosing the Best Option? 

If you already have your updated logo and information ready, emailing info@roomvu.com is usually the quickest option.

## How to Exclude Topics or Remove Posts from Your Content Calendar | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13545152-how-to-exclude-topics-or-remove-posts-from-your-content-calendar

How to Exclude Topics or Remove Posts from Your Content Calendar 

How to Exclude Topics or Remove Posts from Your Content Calendar 

This article explains how to exclude specific words, topics, or public figures from your roomvu Content Calendar using Blacklist Keywords, and how to manually delete a scheduled post from your calendar. 

Updated over a week ago 

Table of contents 

Sometimes you may want to remove a post from your Content Calendar because it includes a certain topic, keyword, public figure, or theme you do not want to share. 

Roomvu allows you to: 

Exclude keywords/topics from future posts using Blacklist Keywords 

Manually delete a post that is already scheduled 

Option 1: Exclude Topics from Your Content Calendar (Recommended) 

If you want roomvu to stop generating content related to specific topics, the best option is to add those words to your Blacklist Keywords . 

​ 

Steps to Add Blacklist Keywords 

Log in to your roomvu dashboard 

Click Content Calendar from the left-side menu 

Find Content Calendar Settings 

Click Edit 

Open the Advanced tab 

Find Blacklist Keywords 

Click Edit List 

Add the words or topics you want to exclude 

Save your changes 

✅ After this, roomvu will avoid creating new calendar posts that include those keywords. 

Examples of Blacklist Keywords you can add: 

Names of public figures 

Specific topics (politics, crypto, etc.) 

Words you do not want to appear in your content 

Option 2: Manually Remove a Scheduled Post 

If a post is already scheduled on your Content Calendar and you do not want it to be published, you can delete it manually. 

Steps to Delete a Post 

Go to Content Calendar 

Find the post you want to remove 

Click the trash bin icon on the post 

🗑️ This removes that specific post from your calendar. 

Quick Notes (Common Questions) 

“Can you remove one post for me?” 

You can remove any post yourself by clicking the trash bin icon on the post. 

“How do I stop roomvu from posting about a topic again?” 

Use Blacklist Keywords in your Content Calendar settings to exclude that topic from future content. 

“Will Blacklist Keywords remove posts that are already on my calendar?” 

Blacklist Keywords help prevent future content from being generated. 

For posts that are already scheduled, delete them manually using the trash bin icon.

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard

English 

Your Dashboard

Search for articles...

Tutorials 

How to Fix Slideshow Issues (Empty Slides, Overlapping Text, Wrong Photos, or Template Problems) 

How to Fix Slideshow Issues (Empty Slides, Overlapping Text, Wrong Photos, or Template Problems) 

This guide explains what to do if your roomvu slideshow has issues such as empty slides, overlapping text or branding, irrelevant photos, wrong slide order, or template problems. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

In rare cases, you may notice problems in your slideshows, such as: 

Empty slides (example: only a photo with no text or design elements) 

Text or branding overlaps important parts of the image (example: AI Portrait face is blocked) 

Irrelevant or incorrect photos 

Design not matching your preference 

Template needs to be changed 

Slide order is not correct 

If this happens, you can usually fix it quickly using one of the options below. 

Option 1: Update Your Branding and Contact Info (Recommended First Step) 

If the issue is caused by your branding details (name, contact info, logo, etc.), you can update your profile and your slideshows will use the latest information moving forward. 

Steps to Update Your Profile Info 

Log in to your roomvu dashboard 

On the main page, click your profile photo 

In your profile window, update any details you need, such as: 

Name 

Email address 

Phone number / contact info 

Logo 

Brokerage logo 

Click Save 

✅ This is the best option if your slideshow issue is related to incorrect branding or outdated details. 

Option 2: Manually Edit the Slideshow (Fix Slides, Photos, Templates, or Layout) 

If you want to fix the slideshow design itself (layout, slide order, photos, or overlapping elements), you can edit the slideshow manually. 

Steps to Edit Your Slideshow 

Go to your Content Calendar 

Find the slideshow post you want to fix 

Click the post to open it 

Click Edit Slides 

You will now see your slideshow slides on the right side. 

How to Edit Each Slide 

Click a slide (one by one) to select it 

Use the left-side menu to make changes 

Change the Slide Template (Fix Layout or Overlap Issues) 

If text or branding is covering an important part of the image (like your AI Portrait face), try changing the template first. 

After selecting a slide, choose a different Template 

This changes the order and placement of elements on that slide 

✅ This is the fastest way to fix layout issues without redesigning the slide. 

Replace a Photo in a Slide 

If you do not like the photo used in the slideshow (or it is irrelevant), you can replace it. 

Steps to Replace the Photo 

Click the slide you want to edit 

Click the photo element in the slide 

Choose a new image from one of these options: 

Location (location-based images) 

Your Brand (your AI Portraits) 

Upload your own content (from your computer) 

✅ This helps fix slides that look off-topic or visually incorrect. 

Edit Text or Elements Colors 

After selecting a slide, you can click on any element to edit its color, such as: 

Text boxes 

Design banners 

Other content blocks 

This is helpful when: 

A slide looks incomplete 

Text feels too long 

Important parts of the image are blocked 

Change Slideshow Colors 

If you do not like the colour style of the slideshow, you can change it easily. 

Steps to Change Colours 

Open your slideshow and click Edit Slides 

From the left-side menu, go to the Colour section 

Select your preferred colours for the slideshow 

✅ This helps make your slideshow look more on-brand and consistent. 

Quick Answers (For Common User Questions) 

“My slideshow has empty slides. What should I do?” 

Open the slideshow from your Content Calendar and click Edit Slides to adjust the slide template and elements. 

“My text is covering my AI Portrait face.” 

In Edit Slides , select the slide and choose a different Template so the elements move to a better position. 

“I do not like the photos used in my slideshow.” 

In Edit Slides , click the photo and replace it using Location , Your Brand (AI Portraits) , or Upload your own content . 

“Can I change the slideshow template?” 

Yes. In Edit Slides , select each slide and choose a different Template . 

“How do I change the colours of my slideshow?” 

In Edit Slides , go to the Colour section and pick your preferred colours. 

Still Need Help? 

If you tried the steps above and your slideshow still looks incorrect, you can contact our support team for help.

## Why Does My Facebook Connection Keep Dropping and How to Link Facebook via Instagram | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13559189-why-does-my-facebook-connection-keep-dropping-and-how-to-link-facebook-via-instagram

Why Does My Facebook Connection Keep Dropping and How to Link Facebook via Instagram | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Tutorials 

Why Does My Facebook Connection Keep Dropping and How to Link Facebook via Instagram 

Why Does My Facebook Connection Keep Dropping and How to Link Facebook via Instagram 

Understand why Facebook personal connections disconnect frequently on Roomvu and learn how to link your Facebook through Instagram for a more stable and reliable posting experience. 

January 29, 2026 

Table of contents 

Many roomvu users ask us why their Facebook connection drops frequently — especially when connecting a personal Facebook account . 

Unfortunately, Facebook doesn’t provide a fully reliable API for personal profiles, so automatic posting tools like Roomvu can experience frequent disconnections or failures. Because this is a limitation on Facebook’s side, Roomvu cannot permanently fix or prevent this on its own. 

The most reliable way to keep your Instagram and Facebook connection stable is to link them properly through Instagram — ideally linking your Instagram to a Facebook Page instead of a personal Facebook profile. 

Why Facebook Keeps Disconnecting 

📌 Facebook personal profile connections are unstable — personal accounts lack the official, stable API support that Pages and Business accounts have. Third-party tools must rely on access tokens that expire, permissions that change, or security limits that Meta applies automatically, causing frequent drops. 

Because of these limitations, the best long-term solution is to connect your Instagram to a Facebook Page , not just a personal profile. 

How to Link Your Instagram to Facebook (for Better Stability) 

Step 1: Make sure you have a Professional Instagram account 

To link Instagram to Facebook properly (especially to a Page instead of a personal profile), your Instagram needs to be a Business or Creator account . 

How to switch: 

Open the Instagram app 

Go to your profile 

Tap the menu (three lines) → Settings 

Tap Account 

Choose Switch to professional account 

Follow the steps to choose Business or Creator 

Step 2: Link Instagram to Facebook via Instagram App 

Open the Instagram app 

Go to your profile 

Tap Edit Profile 

Under Public Business Information , find Page 

Tap Connect or Create 

Log in to Facebook when prompted 

Select the Facebook Page you want to connect to 

Tap Connect 

This links your Instagram to a Facebook Page instead of a personal profile, which is more stable for posting and scheduling. 

Step 3: Confirm the Connection in Meta Accounts Center 

After linking: 

On Instagram, go to Settings 

Tap Accounts Center 

Make sure both your Facebook Page and Instagram are shown 

Enable Sharing across profiles if you want automatic cross-posting 

Linking in Accounts Center ensures both platforms recognize the connection as official. 

If You Don’t Have a Facebook Page Yet 

You can create one during the linking process : 

When Instagram asks you which Page to connect to, choose Create New 

Follow the prompts to set up your Page 

Once created, complete the linking steps 

This gives you access to a more stable connection and lets Roomvu post reliably. 

Summary: Best Practices for Stable Connections 

✅ Use a Facebook Page instead of a personal profile 

✅ Make sure your Instagram is a Business or Creator account 

✅ Link accounts through Instagram’s Edit Profile → Page 

✅ Connect and confirm the link in Meta Accounts Center 

If your connection drops often on personal Facebook, it’s normal — it’s due to Meta’s API limitations, not Roomvu. Connecting via Instagram to a Facebook Page makes your integration much more stable and reduces disconnections. 

Related Articles 

How to Connect Instagram To Facebook and Sync Contacts 

Connect Facebook Page to Instagram Business Account 

How to Connect Your Instagram Page to Your roomvu Account 

How to reauthorize your Facebook permissions for Roomvu dashboard? 

How to enable Facebook personal auto‑sharing?

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13559235-how-to-exclude-a-city-or-area-from-your-roomvu-content

How to Exclude a City or Area From Your roomvu Content 

How to Exclude a City or Area From Your roomvu Content 

Learn how to exclude specific cities or areas from your Roomvu content by blocking locations in your Marketing Location settings to keep your posts focused on the markets you serve. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Sometimes you may want Roomvu to cover a general market but exclude specific cities or areas within or near that location. 

This usually happens when: 

You serve a main city but not certain nearby areas 

You want to avoid content about locations you do not work in 

Your profile location includes multiple sub-areas and you want more control 

The good news is that excluding specific areas from your content is quick and easy. 

How to Block Content From a Specific Location 

Step 1: Log in to your Roomvu account 

Sign in to your Roomvu dashboard. 

Step 2: Open your Profile settings 

Click the gear icon on the top right section of your account. 

Step 3: Scroll to Market Location 

Scroll down until you find the Marketing Location section. 

Here you will see: 

Your main account location 

Your 2nd City/County 

Submarket 

Block Content by Location 

Step 4: Block the area or city you want to exclude 

In the Block Content by Location field: 

Start typing the name of the city or area you want to exclude 

Select the correct option from the list 

You can block multiple locations if needed. 

Step 6: Save your changes 

Click Save at the bottom of the page. 

Once saved, Roomvu will stop generating content related to the blocked area(s). 

What Happens After You Block a Location? 

✅ Your main market coverage stays the same 

✅ Content from the excluded city or area will no longer appear 

✅ You can update or remove blocked locations anytime

How to Disable AI Portraits in Your roomvu Account 

How to Disable AI Portraits in Your roomvu Account 

Learn how to disable AI Portraits in your roomvu account if you do not want AI-generated images, including step-by-step instructions and an alternative email request option. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Some users prefer not to use AI-generated images or portraits in their Roomvu content. This can be for different reasons, including: 

Privacy or consent concerns 

The AI portraits do not look like you 

You do not like the pose, clothing, or style 

You want to modify or replace the images 

You simply prefer not to use AI portraits 

If you want your AI portraits removed, you can disable this feature directly from your account. This is the fastest and recommended option. 

Option 1: Disable AI Portraits From Your Account (Recommended) 

Step 1: Log in to your Roomvu account 

Sign in and stay on the main dashboard. 

Step 2: Open Settings 

Click the gear icon on the top right corner of the page to enter Settings . 

Step 3: Go to AI Portraits 

From the left menu, under the Profile section, click AI Portraits . 

Step 4: Disable AI Portraits 

Click Disable AI-Portraits . 

Once disabled, Roomvu will stop generating and using AI portraits for your account. 

Option 2: Email Our Team (If You Cannot Access Your Account) 

If you are unable to log in to your account for any reason, you can email us at: 

info@roomvu.com 

Please include: 

Your regisreted account email 

A clear request to disable AI portraits 

⚠️ Please note: Email requests may take longer to process. If you have access to your account, disabling the feature yourself is the fastest option. 

What Happens After You Disable AI Portraits? 

✅ AI portraits will no longer be generated or used 

✅ Your content will not include AI-generated images of you 

✅ You can re-enable the feature later if you change your mind 

Need Help With AI Portrait Settings? 

If you want to adjust, regenerate, or review your AI portraits instead of disabling them, our support team can help you explore the available options.

Video Content: Disabling AI Portraits in roomvu 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

This video tutorial explains the straightforward process for users to disable AI-generated portraits in the roomvu platform, highlighting user control, privacy considerations, and flexibility. 

Key Insights 

User Control and Privacy 

Users may want to disable AI portraits due to **privacy concerns**, **personal preferences**, or dissatisfaction with the AI-generated style. RoomView prioritizes giving users control over their content presentation. 

Reversibility 

Once disabled, AI portraits will no longer appear, but users can **reenable the feature at any time**, ensuring flexibility. 

### Step-by-Step Process to Disable AI Portraits 

| Step Number | Action Description | 

|-------------|-------------------------------------------------------| 

| 1 | Log in to your RoomView account and go to the main dashboard. | 

| 2 | Click the gear icon to open the settings menu. | 

| 3 | Locate the " AI portraits " option under the profile section. | 

| 4 | Click the option to disable AI portraits. | 

| 5 | The AI portraits feature is now disabled. | 

Additional Information 

Account Access Issues 

Users unable to log in should email ** info@roomvu.com ** with their request. 

- Note: Email requests are slower than direct in-app changes. 

After disabling, **AI-generated portraits will no longer appear** in the user’s profile or related content areas until reenabled. 

The video clearly emphasizes RoomView’s commitment to user choice by enabling a simple toggle for AI portraits. This feature supports privacy and personalization without permanent commitment, as users can revert their settings anytime. The process is user-friendly, requiring minimal navigation within the platform’s settings, with support provided for account access issues.

## How to Pause Auto Posting and Disconnect Social Platforms in Roomvu | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13571306-how-to-pause-auto-posting-and-disconnect-social-platforms-in-roomvu

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Video Guides 

How to Pause Auto Posting and Disconnect Social Platforms in Roomvu 

How to Pause Auto Posting and Disconnect Social Platforms in Roomvu 

Updated over a week ago 

This tutorial explains how to pause roomvu auto posting by disconnecting your social media platforms. It covers common situations where you may want to stop automatic sharing, such as updating your contact information, changing branding assets, taking a personal break, or temporarily disabling posting on a specific network. 

The video walks through the exact steps inside the Roomvu dashboard. You will see how to open the main dashboard, go to the More section in the bottom left corner, and access your social media connection settings . From there, you can disconnect individual platforms or remove all connected accounts, depending on how broadly you want to pause distribution. 

It also clarifies what happens after disconnection. Auto sharing stops immediately for the selected platforms, while your content calendar continues generating posts in the background. This keeps your upcoming content available for review and future publishing without sending anything live. 

The process is fully reversible, and platforms can be reconnected later to resume normal posting with your existing content pipeline.

## Why Am I Not Getting Engagement or Leads From Roomvu? | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13572145-why-am-i-not-getting-engagement-or-leads-from-roomvu

Why Am I Not Getting Engagement or Leads From Roomvu? | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Video Guides 

Why Am I Not Getting Engagement or Leads From Roomvu? 

Why Am I Not Getting Engagement or Leads From Roomvu? 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Some agents reach out and say they are not seeing enough engagement or leads after using Roomvu. This can be frustrating, especially when you are posting consistently. 

In most cases, this is not a platform issue. It is usually related to how Roomvu features are being used and how social media works as a long-term system . 

Below are the most common reasons and the fixes that help our successful users get better results. 

1. Not Using All Roomvu Features 

Roomvu works best when all of its reach-expanding features are used together. 

Connect all your social media platforms 

Roomvu strongly recommends connecting all available social media platforms to your account. 

Each platform has a different audience: 

Facebook often attracts an older audience 

Instagram reaches lifestyle-focused users 

TikTok reaches a younger, video-first audience 

LinkedIn is strong for professional visibility 

If you only post on one or two platforms, you are likely missing people who do not use the others. 

The more platforms you are present on, the more chances your content has to be seen. 

Use landing pages and email marketing 

Features like landing pages and email marketing help extend your reach beyond social media. 

​ 

The more places your message appears, the more opportunities you create for engagement and leads. 

2. Not Having Enough Followers Yet 

If your social media accounts have very few followers, your content has limited reach. 

This is very common for users who are new to social media. 

When there is no audience yet, even great content will not perform well. 

​ 

What you should do 

Focus on growing your followers alongside posting content. 

These guides can help: 

How to increase your social media followers 

​ https://www.roomvu.com/academy/how-to-increase-social-media-followers/ 

How to transfer followers across platforms 

​ https://www.roomvu.com/academy/transfer-followers/ 

Growing your audience is a critical step before expecting consistent engagement or leads. 

3. Not Personalizing Content Enough 

Social media platforms favor personal and human content . 

If your feed only contains business posts, engagement is usually lower. 

What works better 

Post personal content about your lifestyle, hobbies, or daily activities 

Show the person behind the business 

Be relatable, not just promotional 

When people engage more with your personal content, social media algorithms favor your account overall. This helps all your content , including your business posts, perform better. 

4. Not Using Personal Intros or Showing Your Face 

One of the most effective actions you can take is adding a personal intro to your Roomvu content. 

When people see a face on social media: 

They stop scrolling more often 

They watch longer 

They feel a stronger personal connection 

Adding a short personal intro helps your audience recognize you and trust you over time. 

Many of our top-performing users consistently use personal intros and see significantly better engagement. 

Final Note: Social Media Is a Long Game 

Social media and digital marketing do not produce instant results. 

Strong engagement and leads come from: 

Consistency 

Personalization 

Showing up on multiple platforms 

Gradually growing your audience 

Many Roomvu users who follow the steps above see great results over time. If you stay consistent and use the platform fully, your chances of success increase significantly. 

If you need help reviewing your setup or strategy, our support team is always here to guide you.

How to optimize your Roomvu account after upgrading? 

Why Connect All Platforms on roomvu

Why Does a Lead Show a Foreign Country and Should I Contact Them? 

Why Does a Lead Show a Foreign Country and Should I Contact Them? 

Learn why some leads show foreign countries or international phone numbers, how Facebook auto-registers contact details, and when it is safe to contact these leads using email first. 

February 2, 2026 

Table of contents 

Some agents reach out with concerns when a lead appears to be from another country (for example China or elsewhere) and ask whether the lead is authentic or safe to contact. 

This guide explains why this happens and what you should do. 

Why a Lead May Appear From Another Country 

Seeing a foreign country attached to a lead is very common and does not automatically mean the lead is fake. 

Here are the most common reasons this happens: 

​ 

The person may be travelling or living between countries 

Many buyers search for properties while travelling or while living part-time in another country. It is very common for people to: 

Travel to Canada or the US 

Search for homes while abroad 

Own or plan to own properties in more than one country 

Facebook auto-registers phone numbers 

When leads come through Facebook, the platform often auto-registers the phone number based on the user’s original or “home” country. 

This means: 

The phone number may show a foreign country code 

The person may still be physically located in your market 

The lead can still be genuine and interested 

Because of this, phone numbers alone are not always reliable indicators of a lead’s location. 

Why Email Is Often the Best First Contact 

In cases like this, we strongly recommend contacting the lead by email first . 

Email helps you: 

Confirm the person’s interest 

Understand their actual location and intent 

Avoid unnecessary phone calls before verification 

This is exactly why our team usually suggests email outreach when a lead appears international. 

Should You Contact the Lead? 

✅ Yes, you can contact them 

✅ Start with email rather than calling 

✅ Ask simple qualifying questions (location, timeline, interest) 

​ 

A foreign country label does not mean the lead is a scam or inauthentic. 

Key Takeaway 

Foreign country indicators are often caused by Facebook’s auto-registration 

Many genuine buyers search while travelling or living abroad 

Email is the safest and most effective first step 

These leads can still turn into real opportunities 

If you ever feel unsure about a specific lead, our support team is always here to help review it with you. 

Did this answer your question?

What Is My Username and Password for roomvu? 

What Is My Username and Password for roomvu? 

This article explains how to log in to roomvu without a username or password by using a one-time password (OTP) sent to your email or phone for secure access. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Some users contact our team asking for their username or password so they can share it with an assistant or admin. 

​ 

Although traditional usernames or passwords are available , roomvu recommends one-time password (OTP) login system , which means you never need to remember or share a password. 

How roomvu OTP Login Works 

You can log in to your Roomvu account using either: 

Your email address , or 

Your phone number 

Each time you log in, roomvu sends you a one-time verification code (OTP) . 

How to Log In Using Email or Phone (OTP Login) 

Step 1: Go to the Roomvu login page 

Enter your email address or phone number associated with your account. 

Step 2: Request the verification code 

Click to receive a login code. 

Roomvu will send a one-time password (OTP) to your email or phone. 

Step 3: Enter the OTP 

Enter the code you received to securely access your account. 

No password is required. 

Forgot Which Email or Phone You Used? 

If you are unsure which email or phone number is linked to your account, reach out to our support team by sending us an email to support@roomvu.com and we will help you verify it securely. 

Need Help Logging In? 

If you are not receiving the OTP or cannot access your account, contact our support team and we will assist you step by step.

## How to Clean and Prepare Contact CSV Files Using ChatGPT for Roomvu Email Marketing | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13600380-how-to-clean-and-prepare-contact-csv-files-using-chatgpt-for-roomvu-email-marketing

How to Clean and Prepare Contact CSV Files Using ChatGPT for Roomvu Email Marketing | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content

How to Clean and Prepare Contact CSV Files Using ChatGPT for Roomvu Email Marketing 

How to Clean and Prepare Contact CSV Files Using ChatGPT for Roomvu Email Marketing 

Learn how to use ChatGPT to clean, deduplicate, and format contact CSV or Excel files into the exact First Name, Last Name, and Email structure required for Roomvu email marketing uploads. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

roomvu email marketing uses CSV contact files with a very specific format. 

Your file must include only three columns , in this exact order: 

First Name 

Last Name 

Email Address 

Many agents already have contact files, but they often include: 

Duplicate contacts 

Empty rows or missing emails 

Extra columns not used by Roomvu 

Incorrect column order 

Mixed formats from Excel, Google Sheets, or CRMs 

This guide shows you how to use ChatGPT to quickly clean, fix, and generate a ready-to-upload CSV file for Roomvu. 

What Roomvu Requires for Email Marketing Contacts 

Before uploading, make sure your file follows these rules: 

✅ CSV format 

✅ Exactly 3 columns 

✅ Column order must be: 

First Name 

Last Name 

Email Address 

❌ No phone numbers 

❌ No extra columns 

❌ No empty email cells 

❌ No duplicate email addresses 

Step-by-Step: Clean Your Contact File Using ChatGPT 

Step 1: Prepare your existing contact file 

You can use: 

CSV files 

Excel files (.xlsx) 

If your file is in Excel, that is fine. ChatGPT can handle both. 

Step 2: Open ChatGPT 

Go to ChatGPT and start a new chat. 

Step 3: Upload your contact file 

Use the file upload option in ChatGPT and upload your CSV or Excel file. 

Step 4: Use this prompt (copy and paste) 

Use the prompt below exactly as written, then upload your file if you have not already. 

ChatGPT prompt: 

I want you to clean and optimize this contact file for upload to email marketing platforms. 

Requirements: 

Remove duplicate contacts based on email address 

Remove rows with missing or invalid email addresses 

Remove all columns except First Name, Last Name, and Email Address 

Reorder the columns to be exactly: First Name, Last Name, Email Address 

Fix formatting issues (extra spaces, capitalization) 

Leave first or last name blank if missing, but never include blank emails 

Output the final result as a downloadable CSV file 

Please generate a clean CSV file that is ready to upload. 

Step 5: Download the optimized CSV 

ChatGPT will: 

Clean your data 

Remove unnecessary fields 

Fix column order 

Generate a new CSV file 

Download the file once it is ready. 

Step 6: Upload the CSV to Roomvu 

Go to your Roomvu dashboard and upload the cleaned CSV file into Email Marketing . 

Your contacts are now ready to use. 

Common Mistakes to Avoid 

Uploading files with extra columns 

Uploading files with duplicate emails 

Uploading files with empty email fields 

Changing the column order 

Using ChatGPT helps you avoid all of these issues in minutes. 

Why This Method Works Well 

Saves time cleaning data manually 

Prevents upload errors 

Ensures Roomvu accepts the file on the first try 

Works with large contact lists

## Increase Your Social Media Engagement 7X With AI Avatars | Roomvu Help Center

Increase Your Social Media Engagement 7X With AI Avatars 

Increase Your Social Media Engagement 7X With AI Avatars 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Your AI Avatar is your digital clone inside roomvu. It helps you add your face + voice to your content automatically, so your posts look and feel like you created them, even when you’re not recording. 

This is one of the fastest ways to fix low reach, improve engagement, and stay visible without constantly filming yourself. 

Why your content may be getting low reach 

Social platforms are prioritising content that feels human, personal, and recognisable . 

That means the algorithm looks for signals like: 

Your face 

Your voice 

Your identity 

Your consistent presence 

When your content does not include these signals, it can look like generic or faceless content, and that type of content often gets pushed down in the feed. 

✅ The key question to ask is: Does this look like you created it? 

What your AI Avatar helps you do 

When your AI Avatar is active, your content becomes more personal and recognisable because it includes: 

Your face (AI Avatar visual) 

Your voice (AI voice clone) 

Your identity across posts 

📈 On average, content with your AI Avatar can get up to 7x more engagement compared to typical content without your identity. 

What Platinum members get (Automatic weekly deployment) 

If you're a Platinum member , once your Avatar is activated: 

✅ roomvu will deploy your AI Avatar once per week automatically 

✅ Your content stays personal, recognisable, and consistent 

✅ You show up without needing to record yourself every time 

This is how you stay visible even when life gets busy. 

How to activate your AI Avatar (Step-by-step) 

You can activate your Avatar in a few minutes inside your roomvu dashboard. 

Step 1: Open AI Settings 

Log in to your roomvu account 

Go to your Dashboard 

Click Settings 

Open Talking Avatar 

​ 

Step 2: Review your base photo 

You will see the photo roomvu will use to generate your AI Avatar. 

Confirm it looks like you 

Replace it if you want a newer look 

Step 3: Verify your voice clone 

To activate your voice clone: 

Follow the voice setup prompt 

Read the provided script out loud 

Save and confirm the voice clone 

Once done, your AI Avatar is activated and ready to deploy in your content. 

Bonus tip (After setup): Connect all your social accounts 

After your AI Avatar is active, connect all your social media accounts inside roomvu. 

This helps your content stay consistent across platforms and supports AIO (AI Optimisation) , which improves how AI search tools recognise and recommend you. 

When your content consistently includes your face and voice, AI search engines like ChatGPT and Perplexity can better understand who you are and surface you more often. 

Troubleshooting 

I cannot find AI Settings 

Make sure you are inside the Dashboard , then go to Settings and look for AI Settings . 

​ 

My photo does not look right 

Update your base photo to a clearer, front-facing image with good lighting. 

​ 

My voice setup fails 

Try using Chrome, allow microphone access, and re-read the script in a quiet space. 

Need help? 

If you need help activating your AI Avatar, book a VIP support session and our team will guide you step-by-step.

## How to Activate and Use Roomvu AI Voice Clone | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13610336-how-to-activate-and-use-roomvu-ai-voice-clone

How to Activate and Use Roomvu AI Voice Clone | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Video Guides 

How to Activate and Use Roomvu AI Voice Clone 

How to Activate and Use Roomvu AI Voice Clone 

Learn how to activate roomvu AI Voice Clone, record your voice sample, generate your cloned voice, and troubleshoot common issues when the voice does not sound accurate. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

roomvu’s AI Voice Clone lets your content sound like it was spoken by you, even when you do not record a voiceover for every video. 

​ 

By cloning your voice once, Roomvu can automatically use it across your content, helping you stay personal, consistent, and recognisable without extra effort. 

This guide explains how to activate your AI Voice Clone and how to fix common issues. 

What Is the Roomvu AI Voice Clone? 

The AI Voice Clone replicates your voice using a short voice sample. 

Once activated, Roomvu uses this cloned voice to narrate your videos as if you recorded them yourself. 

This helps: 

Keep your content personal 

Maintain consistency 

Save time on repeated voice recordings 

How to Activate Your AI Voice Clone 

Step 1: Log in to your roomvu account 

Sign in and stay on your main dashboard. 

Step 2: Open Settings 

Click the gear icon on the top right corner of the page to enter Settings . 

Step 3: Go to Voice Over 

From the left menu, click Talking Avatar 

Step 4: Record your voice 

Click Clone My Voice 

A short script will appear on the screen. 

Step 5: Record your voice sample 

Press Record 

Read the script shown on the screen 

You can record for up to one minute 

You may also speak in your own words if you prefer 

The longer and clearer your recording is, the better the voice clone quality will be. 

Step 6: Generate your voice clone 

Once recording is complete: 

Listen to your recording 

If everything sounds clear and correct, click Generate Voice 

If there are microphone issues or mistakes, click Retake and record again 

After generation, your AI Voice Clone will be ready to use. 

Where Your Voice Clone Is Used 

Once activated, your AI Voice Clone is used in your Roomvu content wherever voiceovers are applied, making videos sound as if you personally narrated them. 

Troubleshooting: My Voice Clone Does Not Sound Like Me 

If your AI Voice Clone does not sound accurate, this is usually due to an issue during the recording or cloning process. 

Recommended fixes 

We strongly recommend recording your voice again and making sure that: 

You use a high-quality microphone 

You record in a quiet environment with no background noise 

You record closer to the full one-minute limit to better train the AI engine 

You speak clearly and at a natural pace 

Better input results in a more accurate voice clone. 

Can I Re-record My Voice Clone? 

Yes. You can re-record and regenerate your AI Voice Clone at any time by returning to Settings → Voice Over and recording a new sample.

## Why Can’t I Generate More AI Portraits? | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13610794-why-can-t-i-generate-more-ai-portraits

Why Can’t I Generate More AI Portraits? | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard

Why Can’t I Generate More AI Portraits? 

Why Can’t I Generate More AI Portraits? 

This article explains why AI Portrait generation is limited by plan, what the current limits are, why these limits exist to manage system resources, and what flexibility is planned for the future. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Some agents ask why they are unable to generate more AI Portraits and why they see limits based on their plan. This guide explains how AI Portrait limits work, why they exist, and what to expect going forward. 

Why AI Portraits Have Generation Limits 

AI Portrait generation is a resource-intensive process . Each portrait requires advanced AI computing power to analyse facial features, lighting, pose, and styling. 

To keep the platform stable and reliable for everyone, Roomvu applies weekly or monthly limits based on subscription plans. These limits help prevent system overload and ensure fair usage across all users. 

AI Portrait Limits by Plan 

Your AI Portraits are randomly used in your slideshows, and the number you can generate depends on your plan: 

Free : 1 AI Portrait total 

Basic : 1 AI Portrait per month 

Premium : 1 AI Portrait per week 

Platinum & Diamond : 10 Portraits per week 

Once you reach your limit, you’ll need to wait until the next reset period before generating more. 

Why It’s Important to Be Intentional When Generating AI Portraits 

Because of these limits, we strongly encourage users to pay close attention to details before generating AI Portraits. 

Before you generate, make sure: 

You are happy with the overall style you want 

The look, pose, and clothing match your brand 

You are confident in the idea you have in mind 

Being intentional helps reduce the need to regenerate portraits and ensures you get the best possible result within your available limit. 

Can I Redo or Generate More Portraits Right Away? 

If you’ve reached your plan limit, additional portraits cannot be generated until your limit resets. This is expected behaviour and not an error. 

If you do not want AI Portraits to be used at all, you can disable the feature from your account settings. 

What’s Coming Next 

We understand that users want more flexibility and control. 

In the future, Roomvu plans to introduce a credit-based system . This will give users more freedom to decide how many AI Portraits they generate and when to use them, based on available credits. 

Key Takeaway 

AI Portrait limits exist to protect system performance 

Limits vary by subscription plan 

Being intentional reduces the need for redoing portraits 

More flexible options are planned for the future

How to Control Where AI Portraits Appear in Your Content 

How to Control Where AI Portraits Appear in Your Content 

This article explains what AI Portraits are and how to control where AI Portraits appear in Roomvu content, including video covers and news slideshows. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Roomvu allows you to control how AI Portraits are used for different content types . If you prefer AI Portraits to appear only in certain places, or not at all for specific content, you can easily manage this from your account settings. 

This guide shows you how to turn AI Portraits on or off for Video Covers and News Slideshows . 

What Are AI Portrait Settings? 

AI Portrait Settings let you decide whether your AI Portrait is used in: 

Video Covers (the intro or cover frame of your videos) 

News Slideshows 

These settings give you more flexibility and control over how your brand appears across different types of content. 

How to Change AI Portrait Usage Settings 

Step 1: Log in to your Roomvu account 

Sign in and stay on the main dashboard. 

Step 2: Open Settings 

Click the gear icon on the top right corner of the page to enter Settings . 

Step 3: Go to AI Avatar & Voice 

From the left menu under Profile , click Talking Avatar 

Step 4: Find AI Portrait Settings 

Scroll down until you see the AI Portrait Settings section. 

Step 5: Choose where AI Portraits are used 

Here, you can toggle AI Portraits on or off for: 

Video Covers 

News Slideshows 

Adjust each option based on how you want your content to appear. 

Step 6: Save your changes 

After making your selections, click Save Settings at the top of the page. 

Your changes will apply to future content. 

Need to Update These Settings Later? 

You can return to Settings → AI Avatar & Voice → AI Portrait Settings at any time to update your preferences as your branding or content strategy changes. 

If you have questions about which option works best for your content, our support team is always happy to help.

roomvu gives you control over where AI Avatars are used across different content types. If you want AI Avatars to appear only in certain videos, or not at all in others, you can manage this easily from your account settings.

## How to Set Up Your AI Avatar in Roomvu | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13632723-how-to-set-up-your-ai-avatar-in-roomvu

How to Set Up Your AI Avatar in Roomvu 

How to Set Up Your AI Avatar in Roomvu 

This article explains how to set up an AI Avatar in roomvu, the difference between AI Avatars and AI Portraits, and the available options for creating an avatar using AI Portraits, a selfie, or an uploaded photo. 

Updated over a week ago 

Table of contents 

Roomvu allows you to create an AI Avatar so your content can feature a realistic, animated version of you. When setting up your AI Avatar, you can choose how it’s created based on your preference and comfort level. 

This guide explains what AI Avatars and AI Portraits are, and how to set up your AI Avatar step by step. 

What Are AI Avatars? 

AI Avatars are animated, hyper-realistic digital versions of you. They can move and speak using your cloned voice, making your videos feel as if you personally presented them without having to record yourself each time. 

AI Avatars help you: 

Add a strong personal presence to your content 

Stay consistent across videos 

Save time while remaining recognisable 

What Are AI Portraits? 

AI Portraits are static, AI-generated images created from your profile photo. They are visual representations of you and are often used in slideshows or video covers. 

AI Portraits do not move and do not speak, but they can also be used as a base to create an AI Avatar. 

How to Set Up Your AI Avatar 

Step 1: Open Settings 

Log in to your Roomvu account and click the gear icon on the top right corner of the page to enter Settings . 

Step 2: Go to AI Avatar & Voice 

From the left menu, click Talking Avatar 

​ 

Access Talking Avatar in Settings 

Step 3: Update your AI Avatar 

Click Update My Avatar . 

A pop-up window will appear with multiple options. 

Step 4: Choose how to create your AI Avatar 

You have three options: 

Option 1: Pick from AI Portraits 

This option creates your AI Avatar using one of your existing AI Portraits, which are generated from your profile photo. 

Option 2: Take a Selfie 

This option uses the camera on your device to take a photo and generate a more hyper-realistic AI Avatar. 

Option 3: Upload a Photo 

You can upload a photo from your computer to generate your AI Avatar instead of using the camera. 

Choose the option that best matches how you want your avatar to look. 

After Your Avatar Is Generated 

Once your AI Avatar is created, it will be available for use in supported Roomvu content, helping your videos feel more personal and engaging.

## Why Can’t I Change My Name on My roomvu Account? | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13632944-why-can-t-i-change-my-name-on-my-roomvu-account

Why Can’t I Change My Name on My roomvu Account? 

Why Can’t I Change My Name on My roomvu Account? 

This article explains why name changes on Roomvu require approval, how the name change review process works, and why updates may take time before appearing on your account. 

March 30, 2026 

Table of contents 

Some agents reach out asking why they are unable to immediately change their name on their Roomvu account, or why the change does not apply right away. 

This guide explains how name changes work on Roomvu and what to expect during the process. 

Can I Change My Name on Roomvu? 

Yes, you can request a name change on your Roomvu account. 

However, name changes are reviewed and approved by the Roomvu support team before they are applied. 

This review step is intentional and helps protect account integrity and branding accuracy. 

Why Name Changes Require Approval 

Your name appears across multiple areas of the platform, including branded content, videos, and marketing assets. 

Because of this, Roomvu reviews name change requests to: 

Prevent errors or misuse 

Ensure branding consistency 

Confirm the reason for the change if needed 

In some cases, our support team may ask why the name needs to be changed before approving the request. 

What Happens After You Request a Name Change? 

Once you submit a name change request: 

The request is sent to the Roomvu support team 

The team reviews the request 

Approval may require clarification or confirmation 

The change is applied manually 

⏳ Because this is a manual process, it may take some time before the new name appears on your account. 

Why the Change Is Not Immediate 

Unlike basic profile edits, name changes affect multiple systems and content elements. For that reason: 

The update is not automatic 

Processing time depends on support review and workload 

This is expected behaviour and not a technical issue. 

What You Should Do If You Need a Name Update 

If you need your name updated: 

Submit the request through the appropriate support channel 

Provide the correct new name exactly as you want it displayed 

Be ready to confirm the reason if asked 

Our team will take care of the rest. 

Need Help? 

If you are unsure about the status of your name change or need guidance on submitting a request, our support team is always happy to help.

How to Personalize Your roomvu Content So It Truly Sounds and Feels Like You 

This article explains how Roomvu personalizes content to sound and feel like you by using profile details, appearance preferences, interests, and voice settings to guide AI-generated scripts, visuals, and voiceovers. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

The About You section helps roomvu create content that truly sounds and feels like you. Everything you enter here is used by Roomvu’s AI engine to personalize scripts, visuals, voiceovers, and overall messaging. 

The more accurate and detailed this section is, the better your content will reflect your personality, profession, and style. 

What Is the “ About You ” Section? 

The About You section is part of your account settings and includes four main tabs: 

Profile 

Appearance 

Interests 

Voice DNA 

Each tab plays a different role in shaping how Roomvu creates AI-powered content for you. 

Profile Tab 

Bio 

The Bio section is one of the most important parts of your profile. 

This information is used by Roomvu’s AI to: 

Write video scripts 

Create introductions 

Generate AI-powered content 

We highly recommend writing a detailed and descriptive bio . The more context you provide about who you are, what you do, and who you serve, the better the AI can tailor content to you. 

Identity and Language 

This section helps Roomvu introduce you correctly and adapt content to your preferences. 

It may include: 

Gender 

Pronouns 

Ethnicity 

Preferred language 

These details help ensure your content feels natural, respectful, and aligned with how you want to be represented. 

Appearance Tab 

The Appearance tab controls how you look in AI-generated visuals. 

Appearance Preferences 

These settings are applied automatically when creating: 

AI Portraits 

AI Avatars 

You can define preferences such as: 

Outfit style 

Body style 

Accessories 

Background Preferences (Optional) 

This section sets default backgrounds for: 

AI Avatars 

Immersive Tours 

Available options may include: 

Studio 

Modern office 

Cozy home 

Outdoor 

City skyline 

These backgrounds help keep your visuals consistent with your brand and style. 

Interests Tab 

Professional Topics 

This section tells Roomvu what type of professional content you want to share more often. 

Examples for real estate agents include: 

Buyer Representation 

Commercial Real Estate 

Condos 

Construction 

Development 

Financing 

First-Time Home Buying 

Home Upgrades 

Investments 

Land and Acreage 

Leasing 

Available topics may vary depending on your profession, such as insurance, mortgage, or financial services. 

Personal Interests 

Personal interests are used to humanize your content and personalize visuals and casual avatars. 

Examples include: 

Travel 

Photography 

Cooking 

Fitness 

Reading 

Music 

Sports 

Art 

Yoga 

Hiking 

Cycling 

Dancing 

Gardening 

Fashion 

These preferences help your content feel more relatable and personal. 

Voice DNA Tab 

The Voice DNA tab controls how your AI voice and written content sound. 

Speaking Pace 

You can choose how fast your AI speaks: 

Slow 

Medium 

Fast 

Voice Tone 

Set the tone of your AI voice, such as: 

Professional 

Confident 

Friendly 

Calm 

These settings apply to all AI voice outputs. 

Communication Style 

This section defines how your AI communicates in both: 

Voice 

Written content 

It helps shape sentence structure, clarity, and overall delivery. 

Language Preferences 

Here, you can add: 

Custom phrases 

Catchphrases 

Slogans 

Specific wording preferences 

This helps the AI sound more like you and maintain consistency with your personal brand. 

Why “About You” Matters 

The About You section exists to make Roomvu content feel authentic. 

By filling it out carefully, you help Roomvu: 

Create content that sounds like you 

Match your visual and communication style 

Deliver more accurate and engaging AI-generated content 

For best results, review and update this section whenever your branding, focus, or preferences change.

## How to Customize Your AI Portraits in roomvu | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13672808-how-to-customize-your-ai-portraits-in-roomvu

How to Customize Your AI Portraits in roomvu | Roomvu Help Center
