How to Customize Your AI Portraits in roomvu 

How to Customize Your AI Portraits in roomvu 

Updated today 

Table of contents 

Many users ask how they can customize their AI Portraits to better match their body type, clothing preferences, posture, or background. Roomvu gives you control over these details during the AI Portrait generation process. 

This guide explains how to customize your AI Portraits and what to do if you want a specific look, such as different clothing, posture, or background. 

Before You Start: Use the Right Profile Photo 

AI Portraits are generated based on your profile photo , so this step is critical. 

For best results, make sure: 

Your profile photo is high quality 

The photo is recent 

Your face is clearly visible 

You are happy with how you look in the photo 

If you want your AI Portraits to look different, update your profile photo before generating new portraits. 

How to Customize Your AI Portraits 

Step 1: Open Settings 

Log in to your roomvu account and click the gear icon on the top right corner of the dashboard. 

Step 2: Go to AI Portrait 

From the left menu, click AI Portrait . 

Step 3: Click Generate 

Click Generate to start creating new AI Portraits. 

This is where customization options appear. 

AI Portrait Customization Options 

Framing 

This setting controls how much of your body appears in the portrait. 

You can choose: 

Headshot (close-up face) 

Full body 

You may also see an option to include a fictional client in the portrait if you want a more lifestyle-oriented image. 

Posture 

This setting controls how you appear in the portrait. 

Available options include: 

Standing 

Sitting 

Working 

Relaxing 

Choose the posture that best fits how you want to present yourself. 

Outfit 

This setting controls the style of clothing used in your AI Portrait. 

Options may include: 

Suit 

Casual 

Dress 

Resort wear 

Luxury 

If you prefer specific clothing (for example, dresses instead of pants, or a more formal or modest look), this is where you should choose the closest option and add clarification using Add More Details . 

Background 

This setting controls where your portrait appears. 

Available options include: 

Office 

Beach 

Rooftop 

Countryside 

Other 

If you are not happy with backgrounds used in previous portraits, selecting a different background here can significantly change the result. 

Add More Details (Important) 

If you have something specific in mind that is not covered by the options above, use the Add More Details field. 

This is where you can describe preferences such as: 

Clothing you do or do not want (for example, dresses or skirts instead of pants) 

Include or exclude a certain feature, item, like glasses, hats, wedding rings, etc 

More formal or more casual styling 

Background adjustments 

Overall vibe or look you prefer 

Please note that while Roomvu’s AI is powerful, there may be limitations on what can be generated. Clear and realistic requests produce the best results. 

If You’re Not Happy With the Result 

If your AI Portrait does not look the way you expected, it is usually due to: 

The profile photo used 

Missing or unclear customization details 

Choosing options that do not match your intended look 

You can adjust your settings, update your profile photo, and generate new portraits when your plan allows. 

Key Tips for Better AI Portraits 

Always start with a strong profile photo 

Be intentional with framing, outfit, and posture 

Use Add More Details for specific requests 

Keep requests realistic and clear

## How to Edit Your Tagline in roomvu | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13673070-how-to-edit-your-tagline-in-roomvu

How to Edit Your Tagline in roomvu 

How to Edit Your Tagline in roomvu 

This article explains how to edit your roomvu tagline, where it appears in video outros, and how to update it from the Video Intro & Outro settings so it shows in the last seconds of your videos. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Your tagline appears in the outro slide of your Roomvu videos. This outro is shown during the last 3 seconds of every video , making it an important place to reinforce your brand message. 

If you want to update or change your tagline, you can do this directly from your account settings. 

What Is the Tagline Used For? 

The tagline is part of your video outro and is displayed consistently across all your videos. It’s commonly used for: 

A short brand message 

A slogan or positioning statement 

A call-to-action style phrase 

Because it appears at the end of every video, keeping it accurate and relevant is important. 

How to Edit Your Tagline 

Step 1: Log in to your Roomvu account 

Sign in and stay on the main dashboard. 

Step 2: Open Settings 

Click the gear icon on the top right corner of the dashboard to enter Settings . 

Step 3: Go to Video Intro & Outro 

From the left menu under Content Customization , click Video Intro & Outro . 

Step 4: Edit your tagline 

In this section, you can update your tagline text to whatever you want displayed in the outro of your videos. 

Step 5: Save your changes 

Make sure to click Save after editing your tagline. 

Your updated tagline will be applied to future videos. 

When Will the Change Take Effect? 

Once saved, your new tagline will appear in the outro of newly generated videos. Existing videos may not update retroactively.

## What Is the Difference Between Platinum Design and Premium Branding on roomvu? | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13673431-what-is-the-difference-between-platinum-design-and-premium-branding-on-roomvu

What Is the Difference Between Platinum Design and Premium Branding on roomvu? | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Video Guides 

What Is the Difference Between Platinum Design and Premium Branding on roomvu? 

What Is the Difference Between Platinum Design and Premium Branding on roomvu? 

This article explains why profile changes may not appear in roomvu content, the difference between video branding and slideshow or news images, and how to update each correctly. 

Updated over a week ago 

Table of contents 

roomvu offers two types of branding for your content, and understanding the difference between them is important, especially when you need to make updates to your profile information, photo, or logo. While both use your personal details to brand your content, they work very differently and are updated in different ways. 

​ 

Platinum Design 

Platinum Design is available exclusively to Platinum and Diamond plan subscribers. These are professionally crafted, custom video and image themes built by roomvu's in-house design team. They incorporate many elements of your personal brand including your colors, fonts, name typography, logo, brokerage logo, and profile photo, and allow for a high level of customization that is handled by the design team on your behalf. 

Platinum Design Submition Form 

​ Important: Because Platinum Designs are custom-built by our team, changes you make to your roomvu profile, such as updating your profile photo, logo, or other information, are not automatically applied to your Platinum Design. Your social media content will continue using the previous design until you submit an update request. 

To update your Platinum Design, follow these steps: 

Log in to your roomvu account and go to your Profile . 

In the left menu on your dashboard, click Brand Theme . 

Click Update Design . 

You will be taken to the Platinum Design engine where you can submit your update request. 

For a full guide on how to submit your request, visit this guide. 

​ 

Premium Branding 

Premium Branding is available to users on the Basic, Pro, and Premium (Omni-Presence) plans. It is a set of ready-made templates and color sets available directly on your roomvu dashboard. Like Platinum Design, these templates use your profile photo, logo, brokerage logo, name, email, phone number, and other profile details to brand your content. 

Unlike Platinum Design, Premium Branding updates are made directly by you from your dashboard. There is no design team involved and no request process. However, customization options are more limited. You can select from available templates and color sets, but further adjustments such as custom fonts, typography, or bespoke design elements are not available. 

​ 

When you update your profile information on roomvu, those changes will reflect in your Premium Branding templates automatically. 

​ 

Quick Comparison 

Platinum Design 

Premium Branding 

Available on 

Platinum and Diamond plans 

Basic, Pro, and Premium (Omni-Presence) plans 

Design type 

Custom-built by roomvu's design team 

Ready-made templates and color sets 

Customization 

High, including fonts, colors, typography 

Limited to available templates and colors 

Uses profile photo and logo 

Yes 

Yes 

Profile updates apply automatically 

No, requires an update request 

Yes, updates apply automatically 

How to update 

Submit a request via Brand Theme section 

Adjust directly on your dashboard 

Which one do I have? 

Your branding type is determined by your roomvu plan: 

Platinum Design: Platinum and Diamond plan subscribers 

Premium Branding: Basic, Pro, and Premium (Omni-Presence) plan subscribers 

If you are unsure which plan you are on, check your plan details in your account settings. 

​ 

Note: A common source of confusion is that both designs display your photo, logo, and personal information on your content. This can make it easy to assume that updating your profile will automatically refresh your branding everywhere. For Premium Branding this is true, but for Platinum Design you will always need to submit an update request for changes to take effect on your content.

## Where Your AI Voice Clone Is Used in roomvu Content | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13686135-where-your-ai-voice-clone-is-used-in-roomvu-content

Where Your AI Voice Clone Is Used in roomvu Content | Roomvu Help Center

Where Your AI Voice Clone Is Used in roomvu Content 

Where Your AI Voice Clone Is Used in roomvu Content 

This article explains where AI Voice Clone can be used in Roomvu content, the difference between system voices and cloned voices, and how to improve voice clone quality if it doesn’t sound accurate. 

February 10, 2026 

Table of contents 

Many users ask where their AI Voice Clone can be used and why they sometimes hear different voices in their videos. This guide explains which content types support AI Voice Clone, how system voices work, and what to do if you’re not happy with the results. 

Content Types That Support AI Voice Clone 

Roomvu currently allows AI Voice Clone to be used in two types of videos : 

1. Listing Videos 

Your AI Voice Clone can narrate listing videos, making them sound as if you personally recorded the voiceover. 

2. Editable Videos 

Editable videos also support AI Voice Clone, allowing you to apply your voice across customizable video content. 

For both video types, you can choose whether to use: 

Your AI Voice Clone , or 

A system voice 

Using System Voices 

If you do not use AI Voice Clone, Roomvu will apply system voices . 

Important to know: 

System voices rotate between different voices 

This is intentional and designed to add variety to content 

You may hear different voices across different videos 

If you prefer consistency or want your content to sound more personal, using your own AI Voice Clone is the best option. 

Why Use AI Voice Clone Instead of System Voices? 

Using your AI Voice Clone helps: 

Keep your content recognisable 

Sound more personal and authentic 

Avoid rotating system voices 

If you don’t like how system voices sound, cloning your own voice gives you full control. 

Not Happy With Your AI Voice Clone? 

Roomvu uses best-in-class AI voice generation technology , so most issues are related to the recording process, not the system itself. 

If your cloned voice doesn’t sound right, we strongly recommend re-cloning your voice and making sure that: 

You record in a quiet environment 

You use a high-quality microphone 

You speak clearly and at a natural pace 

You record closer to the maximum allowed time for better results 

Better input leads to a more accurate voice clone. 

Can I Re-clone My Voice? 

Yes. You can re-record and regenerate your AI Voice Clone at any time from your account settings if you want to improve the quality. 

Summary 

AI Voice Clone can be used in Listing Videos and Editable Videos 

System voices rotate for variety 

Cloning your own voice gives you consistency and personalisation 

Re-recording in a quiet space improves voice quality 

If you need help choosing the best option for your content, our support team is always here to help.

How to Set the Posting Frequency on Your Content Calendar 

How to Set the Posting Frequency on Your Content Calendar 

This article explains how to set and adjust content posting frequency in the Roomvu content calendar, where to find frequency settings, and best practices for choosing the right posting schedule. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Roomvu lets you control how often content is scheduled on your content calendar, based on your posting goals and comfort level. Adjusting your frequency helps you stay consistent without overwhelming your audience. 

This guide explains where to find the frequency settings and how to choose the right posting pace. 

Why Content Frequency Matters 

Posting too little can limit visibility, but posting too much can sometimes backfire on social media and reduce engagement. Finding the right balance helps your content perform better and keeps your audience interested. 

Roomvu gives you the flexibility to choose how often content is scheduled so it fits your strategy. 

How to Change Your Content Calendar Frequency 

Step 1: Open Content Calendar 

Log in to your Roomvu account and click Content Calenda r from the right menu on the main dashboard. 

Step 2: Edit Content Calendar Settings 

At the top of the page, find Content Calendar Settings and click Edit . 

Step 3: Go to the Frequency tab 

Inside the settings panel, click the Schedule tab. 

Step 4: Set your posting frequency 

Here, you can set how often Roomvu schedules content for: 

Local Videos & Images 

Local Videos & Images 

Adjust each frequency based on how active you want your social media presence to be. 

Step 5: Save your changes 

Once you’re happy with the frequency, save your settings. Your content calendar will update going forward based on your preferences. 

Best Practice: Don’t Max Out Frequency 

While it may be tempting to schedule as much content as possible, we recommend: 

Testing different frequencies 

Avoiding maximum posting levels right away 

Focusing on consistency over volume 

A well-optimized posting schedule usually performs better than high-volume posting. 

Can I Change This Later? 

Yes. You can return to Content Calendar → Content Calendar Settings → Frequency at any time and adjust how often your content is scheduled as your needs change. 

Need Help Choosing the Right Frequency? 

If you’re unsure how often you should post, our support team can help you choose a frequency that aligns with your goals and platform best practices.

How to Choose and Control the Topics Used in Your Content 

How to Choose and Control the Topics Used in Your Content 

This article explains how to choose and manage content topics in Roomvu, where to select topics for your content calendar, and how specialties and professional interests guide AI-generated content. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Roomvu creates content for many types of professionals, including real estate agents, mortgage brokers, insurance agents, financial advisors, and more. Each of these businesses covers a wide range of topics, but not every topic is relevant to every user. 

That’s why Roomvu allows you to choose which topics are used when content is scheduled on your calendar and when AI generates content for you. 

This guide explains where to manage topic settings and how different sections work together. 

Why Topic Selection Matters 

Choosing the right topics helps: 

Keep your content aligned with your services 

Avoid posts about areas you don’t focus on 

Improve relevance and engagement with your audience 

Roomvu uses your topic selections to decide what type of content appears on your content calendar and how AI writes and frames your messaging. 

How to Select Content Topics for Your Calendar 

Step 1: Open Content Calendar 

Log in to your Roomvu account and click Content Calendar from the right menu on the main dashboard. 

Step 2: Edit Content Calendar Settings 

Find Content Calendar Settings and click Edit . 

Step 3: Go to the Content tab 

Inside the settings panel, open the Content tab. 

Step 4: Select your topics 

Here, you can check or uncheck topics based on the services you offer. 

Only the selected topics will be used when scheduling content on your calendar. 

Step 5: Save your changes 

Once updated, save your settings. Future scheduled content will follow your selected topics. 

Additional Topic Controls in “About You” 

Roomvu also uses topic preferences from your About You settings to further personalise content. 

Specialties 

In the About You section, you can define your specialties . This helps Roomvu understand your main focus areas and tailor content accordingly. 

Professional Topics 

Under the Interests tab in the same section, you can select Professional Topics you want the AI to prioritise when creating content. 

These topics guide: 

AI-written scripts 

Introductions 

Messaging style 

How These Settings Work Together 

Content Calendar → Content tab controls what gets scheduled 

About You → Specialties defines your core focus 

About You → Interests → Professional Topics guides AI-generated content 

Using all three ensures your content stays relevant, consistent, and aligned with your business goals. 

Can I Change Topics Anytime? 

Yes. You can update your topic selections at any time. Changes will apply to newly scheduled and newly generated content.

## How to Disable AI Portraits in Video Covers | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13700786-how-to-disable-ai-portraits-in-video-covers

How to Disable AI Portraits in Video Covers 

How to Disable AI Portraits in Video Covers 

This article explains how to disable AI Portraits in video covers, where to find AI Portrait Settings, and how to control whether AI Portraits appear in video covers and news slideshows. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

roomvu automatically adds a video cover to content scheduled on your content calendar. In many cases, this cover includes your AI Portrait to help make your videos more personal and recognisable. 

However, some users prefer not to use AI Portraits in their video covers. If you want to remove AI Portraits from your video covers, you can easily control this in your settings. 

This guide explains how to turn AI Portraits off for video covers. 

What Is a Video Cover? 

A video cover is the opening visual frame of your scheduled videos. It appears before the main video content starts and helps grab attention. 

By default, AI Portraits may be included in video covers depending on your settings. 

If you do not want your AI Portrait to appear there, you can disable it. 

How to Disable AI Portraits for Video Covers 

Step 1: Open Settings 

Log in to your Roomvu account and click the gear icon on the top right corner of your main dashboard. 

Step 2: Go to AI Avatar & Voice 

From the left menu under Profile , click Talking Avatar . 

Step 3: Find AI Portrait Settings 

Scroll down until you see the AI Portrait Settings section. 

Step 4: Turn Off AI Portraits for Video Cover 

In this section, you can choose how AI Portraits are used for each content type. 

You will see options to turn AI Portraits on or off for: 

Video Cover 

News Slideshow 

News Image 

Toggle off Video Cover if you do not want your AI Portrait to appear in video covers. 

Step 5: Save Your Changes 

After adjusting your preferences, click Save Settings at the top of the page. 

Your changes will apply to future scheduled content. 

Important to Know 

Changes apply to future content 

Already scheduled posts may still use previous settings 

You can re-enable AI Portraits anytime

What Can I Get With a Free Roomvu Account? 

What Can I Get With a Free Roomvu Account? 

This article explains what is included in a Free Roomvu account, including one downloadable video, one AI Portrait, and one downloadable news slide. 

February 16, 2026 

Table of contents 

If you’re using a Free Roomvu account , you still get access to a limited set of powerful features so you can try the platform before upgrading. 

This guide explains exactly what’s included in the Free plan and what you can download. 

What’s Included in a Free Account? 

With a Free Roomvu account, you can: 

​ 

1. Download One Video 

You can generate and download one video to test the quality and see how Roomvu content looks when shared. 

This allows you to: 

Experience the platform 

Review branding and style 

Share a sample video 

2. Generate One AI Portrait 

Free users can generate one AI Portrait . 

AI Portraits are static AI-generated images designed to look like you. They can be used in slideshows and video visuals. 

This gives you the opportunity to: 

See how AI-generated branding looks 

Test how your likeness appears in content 

3. Download One News Slide 

You can download one news slideshow to evaluate the style and layout of Roomvu’s static content. 

This helps you: 

See how branded news posts look 

Review visual consistency 

Try sharing content manually 

What Happens After You Use These? 

Once you’ve used your free downloads: 

Additional downloads require upgrading 

AI Portrait generation is limited to the Free plan allowance 

Upgrading unlocks higher limits, automation, and advanced features. 

Why Start With Free? 

The Free plan is designed to: 

Let you test content quality 

Explore AI features 

Experience the platform risk-free 

Want More? 

If you’re ready to unlock more downloads, more AI Portraits, and automated scheduling, you can upgrade your subscription anytime from your account settings.

## How to Add Your AI Avatar to Editable Videos | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13745740-how-to-add-your-ai-avatar-to-editable-videos

How to Add Your AI Avatar to Editable Videos 

How to Add Your AI Avatar to Editable Videos 

This article explains how to add an AI Avatar to editable videos, required setup steps such as voice cloning and AI Portrait creation, and how AI Avatars are automatically added to scheduled editable videos. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

roomvu allows you to add your AI Avatar to editable videos, so your content begins with a short, automated introduction that looks and sounds like you. 

Your AI Avatar is a speaking, animated version of your AI Portrait that uses your cloned voice. It appears at the beginning of eligible videos and delivers an introduction as if you personally recorded and edited the clip yourself. The entire process is automated. 

​ 

Please note: 

​ 

AI Avatars are currently supported only in editable videos that are scheduled on your content calendar . 

What Is an AI Avatar? 

An AI Avatar is: 

A speaking, animated version of you 

Created from your AI Portrait 

Powered by your AI Voice Clone 

Automatically added to the beginning of supported videos 

It creates the impression that you recorded a professional intro without needing to film anything. 

Before You Add Your AI Avatar 

To use AI Avatars in editable videos, you must first: 

Clone your voice 

Generate your AI Portraits 

Create your AI Avatar using your AI Portrait 

If any of these steps are incomplete, the avatar cannot be added. 

How to Add Your AI Avatar to an Editable Video 

Step 1: Go to Your Content Calendar 

Log in to your roomvu account and open your Content Calendar . 

Step 2: Find or Schedule an Editable Video 

Locate an editable video already scheduled on your calendar. 

If you don’t have one scheduled, schedule an editable video first. 

Step 3: Open the Video 

Click on the editable video in your calendar. You can find them by the purple tag they have that says "Add talking avatar" 

Step 4: Click “Add My Avatar” 

Inside the video settings, click Add My Avatar . 

Roomvu will begin generating your AI Avatar and attaching it to the video automatically. 

Important to Know 

You may not immediately see the AI Avatar preview inside the editor. 

The AI Avatar will be included when the video is posted or downloaded. 

Avatar generation may take a short processing time. 

How It Works 

Once added, your AI Avatar will: 

Appear at the beginning of the video 

Deliver a short introduction 

Look and sound like you 

Be fully automated 

This helps increase engagement and adds a stronger personal presence to your content. 

Need Help? 

If the AI Avatar option does not appear or you are unsure whether your setup is complete, our support team is happy to help review your account and guide you.

## How to Use AI Introduction Videos in roomvu | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13761504-how-to-use-ai-introduction-videos-in-roomvu

How to Use AI Introduction Videos in roomvu 

How to Use AI Introduction Videos in roomvu 

This article explains how to use AI Introduction Videos in Roomvu, where to find the feature, how to choose characters, topics, and content angles, and best practices for using AI intros alongside personal recorded intros. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

The AI Introduction Videos feature allows you to add a short, AI-generated intro to the beginning of your videos. Instead of recording yourself, fictional AI characters read a script and generate a professional introduction automatically. 

​ 

This feature is designed to help users add a human face to their videos without going through the process of filming and editing an intro. 

​ 

However, while this feature is convenient, it should be used as a complement to personal intros , not a replacement. Appearing in your own videos helps humanize your brand and build credibility. We strongly recommend using personal recorded intros regularly whenever possible. 

What Are AI Introduction Videos? 

AI Introduction Videos: 

Use fictional AI characters 

Read a script based on selected topics and angles 

Generate a short intro video 

Are added to the beginning of your content 

They are especially helpful for users who: 

Are camera-shy 

Do not have time to record 

Want a quick, professional intro 

Where to Find the Feature 

You can access AI Introduction Videos directly at: 

https://www.roomvu.com/dashboard/introduction-video 

Once on the page, you’ll see a variety of AI characters in different settings and environments. 

We continuously add new characters and styles to better match the needs of our diverse user base. 

How to Create an AI Introduction Video 

Step 1: Choose a Character Style 

Browse through the available AI characters and select a style you like. 

When you click on a character, a pop-up window will show: 

A sample script 

The tone and setting of the video 

This gives you an idea of the overall feel before generating. 

Step 2: Choose a Topic 

Click Choose a topic . 

Available topics may vary depending on your account type, such as real estate, mortgage, insurance, or financial services. 

Step 3: Choose a Content Angle 

After selecting a topic, choose a content angle . 

Based on your selections, roomvu will generate a script automatically. 

You can edit this script if needed to better match your message. 

Step 4: Use This Style 

Once you’re satisfied with: 

The character 

The topic 

The content angle 

The script 

Click Use This Style . 

Step 5: Agree to Terms and Conditions 

You will be asked to agree to the following: 

​ 

“I hereby confirm that I will not use the platform-generated content for any illegal, fraudulent, or harmful purpose. I reaffirm my obligation to abide by the Terms of Service and Privacy Policy.” 

​ 

You may also choose to: 

Schedule the generated video on your calendar for this week 

Then click Generate Video . 

Generation Process 

Video generation may take a few minutes. 

Once ready, the video will appear in the Your Videos section. 

From there, you can: 

Download the video 

Schedule it on your content calendar 

Important Best Practice 

While AI Introduction Videos are useful and convenient, they should not replace your personal presence. 

​ 

For long-term credibility and engagement: 

Continue using personal intros where you record yourself 

Use AI Introduction Videos as an additional tool, not your only intro method 

Showing your real face and voice builds trust and strengthens your brand. 

Future Updates 

Currently, AI Introduction Videos use fictional AI characters. 

In future updates, users will be able to use their own AI Avatars in these settings and styles. 

Need Help? 

If you’re unsure which style or topic works best for your brand, our support team is happy to guide you.

## Why Doesn’t the Voice-Over in My Video Sound Like Me? | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13762229-why-doesn-t-the-voice-over-in-my-video-sound-like-me

Why Doesn’t the Voice-Over in My Video Sound Like Me? 

Why Doesn’t the Voice-Over in My Video Sound Like Me? 

This article explains why some Roomvu videos use system voice-overs instead of your cloned voice, the difference between system AI voices and voice clone narration, and why this is not a bug. 

February 18, 2026 

Table of contents 

Some users contact us after hearing a voice-over in their video that doesn’t sound like them, especially if they have already cloned their voice. In most cases, this is not a bug. 

Roomvu uses two different types of voice-overs across videos: 

System Voice-Overs 

Cloned Voice Voice-Overs 

This guide explains the difference and why you may hear a voice that is not your own. 

Two Types of Voice-Overs in Roomvu 

1. System Voice-Overs 

Some Roomvu videos come with default system voice-overs . 

Important to know: 

These use a variety of professional AI voices 

The voices rotate intentionally for variety 

They are not connected to your account or your cloned voice 

They appear in certain pre-designed videos 

Even if you have cloned your voice, some videos in your library may still use system voices by design. 

This is normal behaviour. 

2. Cloned Voice Voice-Overs 

When you clone your voice, Roomvu can use your AI Voice Clone in supported video types. 

​ 

Currently, cloned voices are only applied to: 

Listing Videos 

Editable Videos 

If a voice-over appears in any other type of video, it is a system voice-over , and it will naturally sound different from your voice. 

​ 

Your cloned voice: 

Is generated from your own voice sample 

Sounds like you 

Is applied only to supported video types 

Not all videos automatically use your cloned voice. 

Why You’re Hearing a Voice That Isn’t Yours 

If a video voice-over does not sound like you, it is usually because: 

The video is using a system voice 

That video type does not support cloned voice 

This does not mean your voice clone failed or that the system has a bug. 

Important Clarification 

This article explains the difference between system voices and cloned voices . 

If your cloned voice itself does not sound accurate, that is a separate issue covered in another help article about improving voice clone quality. 

Summary 

Roomvu uses both system voice-overs and cloned voice voice-overs 

Cloned voices are currently applied only to Listing Videos and Editable Videos 

Other videos use rotating system AI voices. 

If you’re unsure whether a specific video is using your cloned voice or a system voice, our support team is happy to check it for you.

## My roomvu Content Feels Repetitive and I’m Not Getting Engagement. What Should I Do? | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13786387-my-roomvu-content-feels-repetitive-and-i-m-not-getting-engagement-what-should-i-do

My roomvu Content Feels Repetitive and I’m Not Getting Engagement. What Should I Do? | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content

My roomvu Content Feels Repetitive and I’m Not Getting Engagement. What Should I Do? 

My roomvu Content Feels Repetitive and I’m Not Getting Engagement. What Should I Do? 

This article explains why engagement can drop when content feels repetitive, how personalization and content mix impact performance, and a step-by-step plan to improve results without cancelling. 

February 20, 2026 

Table of contents 

If you feel like your content is starting to repeat and engagement is dropping, you are not wrong to raise this. When posts feel too similar, audiences can scroll past them more often. 

​ 

The good news is this is usually fixable without cancelling. In most cases, the issue is not “posting more,” it is posting the right mix with more personalization . 

This guide explains why it happens and gives you a clear fix plan. 

Why This Happens 

1. roomvu gives consistency, but engagement comes from personalization 

roomvu helps you show up consistently with hyper-local content, which solves a major challenge for most agents. 

​ 

But social platforms reward content that feels personal and recognisable, including: 

Your face 

Your voice 

Your opinion 

Your local take 

Your timing 

If your feed is only automated content without personal signals, platforms can treat it like generic content, even if the information is useful. 

2. Repetition is usually a content mix issue, not a platform issue 

Most “repetitive content” complaints come from posting too much of one type of content, such as: 

Only market updates 

Only generic tips 

Only branded slides 

No personal intros 

No local stories or opinions 

The fix is usually a better weekly mix, not stopping content. 

A Practical Fix Plan 

A. Do a quick content audit 

Review your last 20 to 30 posts and check: 

Post types used (video, slideshow, carousel, local update, listing, testimonial, etc.) 

Which posts included your face or voice 

Which posts had a local angle 

Which posts had a clear CTA 

Which posts performed best 

This moves the conversation from frustration to data and shows exactly what is repeating and what is missing. 

B. Add more personal signals 

This is the biggest improvement. 

Start using: 

Face-on-camera intros when possible 

Roomvu intro video tools (when available) 

AI Avatar (if available on your plan) for a consistent presence 

AI Portraits for recognisable branding 

A short personal caption before posting (1 to 2 sentences) 

Simple personal hooks you can add: 

“This is happening in [city] right now.” 

“I’m seeing this with buyers this week.” 

“If you own in [area], pay attention to this.” 

“Here’s what this means in plain English.” 

Even when the base topic is similar, this personal layer makes it feel new. 

C. Improve the weekly content mix 

Try a balanced weekly mix so your feed does not feel repetitive: 

Example mix: 

1 local market insight post 

1 educational post (buyer or seller tip) 

1 personal brand post (story, opinion, behind the scenes) 

1 listing or listing-related post 

1 community or local lifestyle post 

If your feed only includes market stats or generic videos, engagement usually flattens. 

D. Use stronger captions and clearer CTAs 

Low engagement is often a caption problem, not a content problem. 

Try: 

Ask one clear question 

Add one local reference 

Share one short opinion 

Include one simple CTA 

Example: 

Instead of: “New market update for this week” 

Try: “Inventory is shifting in North Vancouver and buyers are taking longer to decide. Are you seeing the same in your neighbourhood?” 

E. Narrow your local relevance 

Roomvu performs best when your content feels specific. Focus on: 

Neighbourhoods you actually serve 

Price ranges you specialise in 

Client types you work with (first-time buyers, downsizers, investors, etc.) 

More specific content often gets fewer low-quality likes, but better real leads. 

F. Add one manual post per week 

A simple hybrid strategy works fast: 

Keep Roomvu automation for consistency 

Add one manual post weekly (selfie video, opinion, listing story, client question) 

Automation keeps you visible. Manual posts create connection. 

G. Track the right metrics 

Many agents judge performance only by likes. Track: 

Profile visits 

DMs 

Saves and shares 

Link clicks 

Replies and comments 

Listing inquiries 

Email opens, if you use email campaigns 

Real estate content often converts quietly. 

H. Use a 14-day reset plan 

If you want a quick test before making big decisions: 

Audit your last 20 posts 

Refresh your content mix 

Add a personal intro to 2 videos 

Rewrite captions with local hooks 

Add 1 manual post 

Review results after 2 weeks 

This usually reveals what actually drives engagement for your audience.

roomvu Content Calendar: A Comprehensive Guide 

Create Stand‑Out Videos in Seconds with roomvu’s AI Content Creation 

Why Am I Not Getting Engagement or Leads From Roomvu? 

How to Personalize Your roomvu Content So It Truly Sounds and Feels Like You

## Why Isn’t My MLS Listing Updating on roomvu? | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13788511-why-isn-t-my-mls-listing-updating-on-roomvu

Why Isn’t My MLS Listing Updating on roomvu? | Roomvu Help Center

Why Isn’t My MLS Listing Updating on roomvu? 

Why Isn’t My MLS Listing Updating on roomvu? 

This article explains the difference between live MLS ID imports and non-live Zillow or Realtor imports, clarifies why some listings do not update automatically, and outlines how to re-import and regenerate listing content. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Roomvu allows you to import your listings and automatically generate marketing content such as listing videos and immersive tours. 

​ 

However, not all imports behave the same way. 

​ 

Only direct MLS ID imports are live and can reflect updates automatically. 

All other import methods, including Zillow, Realtor, and other third-party sources, are not live feeds . 

​ 

This guide explains the difference and what you need to do if your listing details are not updating. 

Live vs Non-Live Listing Imports 

1. Direct MLS ID Import (Live) 

If you import your listing using the MLS ID directly inside Roomvu , the listing can stay synced with MLS updates. 

This means: 

Price changes may update 

Status updates may reflect 

Listing detail changes may sync 

Direct MLS ID imports are the only method that supports live syncing. 

2. Zillow, Realtor, and Other Imports (Not Live) 

If you import your listing from: 

Zillow 

Realtor 

Other third-party platforms 

These imports are static snapshots . 

Roomvu captures the listing details at the time of import and generates content based on that version. It does not continuously sync with those platforms. 

If you later change: 

The price 

The description 

The photos 

The property details 

Those updates will not automatically reflect in Roomvu. 

This is expected behaviour and not a system error. 

How to Update Your Listing on Roomvu 

If your listing was imported from Zillow, Realtor, or another non-MLS-ID method and you made updates, you will need to: 

​ 

Step 1: Delete the Existing Listing 

Go to your listings section and remove the outdated listing. 

Step 2: Import the Listing Again 

Re-import the listing from MLS so the system captures the updated information. 

Step 3: Regenerate Content 

After re-importing, the listing video will be regenerated. You will also need to manually regenerate Immersive tours. 

​ 

These assets are created based on the imported listing data, so they must be rebuilt after updates. 

Important to Remember 

Only direct MLS ID imports are live 

Zillow and Realtor imports are not live 

Non-live listings require deletion and re-import to update 

Listing videos and immersive tours must be regenerated after re-import 

When Should You Re-Import? 

You should re-import your listing if: 

The price changes 

Major details are updated 

New photos are added 

Property status changes 

Keeping your content aligned with your MLS data ensures your marketing stays accurate and professional.

I Need Help. How Can I Contact Roomvu Support? 

I Need Help. How Can I Contact Roomvu Support? 

This article explains how to get help in Roomvu, including accessing tutorial videos, using the chat box, emailing support, and booking a support session. 

February 23, 2026 

Table of contents 

If you’re feeling stuck or need assistance, you’re not alone. Whether you have a question about a feature, need help troubleshooting, or want guidance on using the platform, there are several ways to get support. 

This guide explains the fastest and most effective ways to get help inside Roomvu. 

​ 

Option 1: Start with Tutorial Videos on Your Dashboard 

We highly recommend starting with the Knowledge Base and Tutorial Videos available directly in your account. 

To access them: 

Log in to your Roomvu account 

Click Tutorial Videos on your dashboard 

These video guides explain: 

How different features work 

How to activate tools 

What you may be missing 

Step-by-step walkthroughs for common tasks 

In many cases, you’ll find your answer immediately without needing to contact support. 

Option 2: Use the Chat Box Inside Your Account 

If you still need help, use the chat box inside your dashboard. 

How it works: 

The chatbot is the first line of response 

It answers questions based on our Knowledge Base 

If it cannot resolve your issue, your message is forwarded to a human agent 

Please note: 

Human agent availability may vary depending on the time and day. Response times can differ during weekends or outside business hours. 

Option 3: Send Us an Email 

You can email us directly at: 

info@roomvu.com 

When sending your email: 

Use the email address registered on your Roomvu account 

Clearly describe your issue or request 

Include screenshots if possible 

Using your registered email helps us locate your account quickly and respond faster. 

Option 4: Book a Support Session 

You can also book a support session directly from your dashboard. 

However, this is typically the last option we recommend because: 

Same-day availability may not always be possible 

Booking depends on schedule availability 

In over 90 percent of cases, using Tutorial Videos, Chat, or Email results in faster assistance. 

What Is the Fastest Way to Get Help? 

For most users, the fastest path is: 

Check Tutorial Videos 

Use the Chat Box 

Send an email if needed 

Support sessions are best for more complex cases that require walkthroughs. 

Summary 

If you need help: 

Start with Tutorial Videos on your dashboard 

Use the chat box for quick responses 

Email info@roomvu.com with details and screenshots 

Book a support session if other options do not resolve your issue 

We’re here to help and want to make sure you get the support you need as quickly as possible.

## roomvu Refund Policy Explained | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13846528-roomvu-refund-policy-explained

roomvu Refund Policy Explained | Roomvu Help Center

roomvu Refund Policy Explained 

roomvu Refund Policy Explained 

This article explains Roomvu’s refund policy, including the 7-day subscription guarantee, non-refundable conditions, automatic renewals, Facebook Ads refund eligibility, and billing terms. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

This article explains Roomvu’s refund policy in simple terms, including subscriptions, Facebook Ads, and special conditions such as the 7-day guarantee. 

Please read carefully before requesting a refund. 

1. Subscription Refund Policy 

No Refunds After Payment Is Processed 

All subscription sales are final. 

Roomvu does not provide prorated refunds for partially used subscription periods. Once a billing cycle has started, your subscription will continue until the end of that billing term. 

If you cancel: 

Your plan will remain active until the end of your current billing period. 

Your account will be downgraded to the Free plan once the paid term expires. 

You will not receive a partial refund for unused time. 

7-Day Guarantee 

Roomvu offers a 7-day refund window from the original purchase date only. 

​ 

Annual Subscriptions 

Cancel within 7 days of original purchase → Full refund 

Cancel after 7 days → No refund 

Service continues until the end of the annual term 

Monthly Subscriptions 

Cancel within 7 days of original purchase → Full refund 

Cancel after 7 days → No refund 

Service continues until the end of that billing month 

Important: 

The 7-day guarantee applies only to the original purchase, not to renewals. 

When the 7-Day Refund Does NOT Apply 

You are not eligible for a refund if any of the following actions have occurred: 

You have downloaded or published a video 

You have shared a video on social media 

You have used email marketing to send emails to contacts 

If any of the above actions are taken, the subscription becomes non-refundable even within the 7-day window. 

2. Automatic Renewal Policy 

Subscriptions renew automatically at the end of each billing period unless cancelled before the renewal date. 

To prevent renewal, you must cancel: 

Through your Roomvu account before the renewal date 

Or by contacting support@roomvu.com before renewal 

If you subscribed through: 

App Store → Cancel through your App Store settings 

Google Play → Cancel through Google Play settings 

Failure to cancel before the renewal date will result in automatic billing for the next subscription period. 

3. Facebook Ads Refund Policy 

Refund requests for Facebook Ads may be granted only if: 

The ad has not been activated 

The ad budget has not been spent 

The request is made within 14 days from the date the ad order was placed in the Roomvu system 

If the advertising funds have already been spent on your behalf, including: 

Lead generation campaigns 

Display advertisements 

No refund will be granted. 

You can verify ad spend activity on your dashboard. 

4. Fees and Billing 

Fees are auto-invoiced monthly on your signup date unless otherwise specified. 

Roomvu may modify pricing with at least 30 days’ notice. 

Once payments are processed, fees are non-refundable. 

Summary 

Subscription refunds: 

7-day refund available only for original purchase 

No refunds after 7 days 

No refunds if platform features were used 

No prorated refunds 

Facebook Ads: 

Refund only if budget is not spent 

Must request within 14 days 

No refund once ad spend occurs 

Automatic renewal: 

Subscriptions renew unless cancelled before renewal date

How to Receive Non-Hyperlocal Content in roomvu 

How to Receive Non-Hyperlocal Content in roomvu 

This article explains how brokerages and insurance users can enable non-hyperlocal content in Roomvu, where to find the location settings, and how to receive broader industry content alongside hyper-local posts. 

February 25, 2026 

Table of contents 

roomvu is designed to generate hyper-local content tailored to your selected market. However, some users may want to receive broader, non-local content in addition to their location-based posts. 

If you prefer to receive non-hyperlocal content as well, this option is available for certain account types. 

Currently, this feature is available for: 

Brokerages 

Insurance professionals 

This guide explains how to enable it. 

What Is Hyper-Local Content? 

By default, Roomvu generates content based on the location selected in your account. This ensures: 

Local market relevance 

Area-specific updates 

Community-focused content 

Geographic targeting 

This approach helps position you as the local expert in your area. 

What Is Non-Hyperlocal Content? 

Non-hyperlocal content includes: 

Broader industry topics 

General educational insights 

National-level trends 

Content not tied to a specific city or neighbourhood 

This type of content can help diversify your feed and expand your audience beyond a specific location. 

How to Enable Non-Hyperlocal Content 

Step 1: Log in to Your Account 

Sign in to your Roomvu dashboard. 

Step 2: Click the Location Icon 

On the top left corner of your dashboard, click the Location icon. 

Step 3: Adjust Your Content Preference 

In the pop-up menu, you will see your selected content location. 

If you want to receive non-local content as well, check the option: 

“I want non-local content as well” 

Once selected, your content calendar may begin including broader industry content alongside your hyper-local posts. 

When Should You Use This Option? 

You may consider enabling non-hyperlocal content if: 

You operate in multiple regions 

You want broader industry visibility 

You want more content variety 

Your business model is not limited to one geographic market 

However, we recommend keeping a balance between local authority and broader relevance. 

Important Notes 

This feature is currently available only for brokerages and insurance accounts. 

Hyper-local content remains the foundation of Roomvu’s strategy. 

Enabling non-local content supplements your calendar, it does not remove local content unless you change your location settings.

How to Email Your Listings to Your Audience Using roomvu 

How to Email Your Listings to Your Audience Using roomvu 

This article explains how agents can email their listings using Roomvu’s email marketing feature, including selecting listings, choosing contacts, customizing templates, and scheduling delivery. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

roomvu allows all real estate agents to email their listings directly to their contact list using built-in email marketing tools. 

​ 

For Platinum and Diamond plans , email delivery is powered by Constant Contact , providing enhanced email infrastructure and performance. 

​ 

This feature helps you professionally promote your listings, stay top of mind with your audience, and increase visibility for your properties. 

What Is the Listing Email Feature? 

The Listing Email feature allows you to: 

Send your property listings to your contact list 

Use ready-to-send, professionally designed templates 

Automatically personalize emails with contact information 

Include listing images and descriptions 

Edit subject lines and email content before sending 

Templates are professionally designed and optimized for readability and engagement. 

Before You Start 

Before sending a listing email, make sure: 

Your listing has already been imported into your Roomvu account 

Your contacts are uploaded inside Email Campaigns 

If your listing is not imported yet, you must import it first before using this feature. 

How to Send a Listing Email 

Step 1: Go to Email Campaigns 

Log in to your Roomvu account and click Email Newsletters from the left menu. 

Step 2: Open the Listings Tab 

Click the Listings tab inside Email Campaigns. 

Step 3: Choose When to Send 

Select the date and time you want your email to be sent. 

You can schedule it or send it sooner depending on your strategy. 

Step 4: Select the Listing 

From the dropdown menu, choose the listing you want to promote. 

Roomvu will automatically populate the email template with the listing details and images. 

Step 5: Select Your Contacts 

Choose the contact list you would like the email to be sent to. 

Make sure your contacts have opted in to receive marketing emails. 

Step 6: Review and Customize 

You can: 

Edit the subject line 

Modify the email body text 

Adjust messaging to match your tone 

While templates are professionally structured, personalization can increase engagement. 

Step 7: Send a Test Email (Recommended) 

Send a test email to yourself before final delivery to: 

Check formatting 

Review images 

Confirm personalization 

Ensure everything appears correctly 

Step 8: Send Email 

Once everything looks good, click Send Email . 

Your listing email will be delivered at the scheduled time. 

Why Use Listing Emails? 

Listing emails help you: 

Increase exposure for your property 

Reach buyers directly in their inbox 

Stay top of mind with your database 

Create additional touchpoints beyond social media 

Email marketing often generates high-quality engagement and serious inquiries.

How to Set Your Business Location for Accurate Hyper-Local Content 

How to Set Your Business Location for Accurate Hyper-Local Content 

This article explains how to set and update your business marketing location in Roomvu, including primary city or zip code, secondary location, submarket selection, and excluding specific areas from hyper-local content. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

One of roomvu’s core strengths is the hyper-local content it creates for businesses. Because of this, it is extremely important that your account reflects the correct service area. 

​ 

Your marketing location determines: 

The city or zip code used for your content 

Local market update videos 

Area-specific insights and statistics 

Community-based posts 

Roomvu allows you to: 

Set a Primary Location 

Add a Second Location (optional) 

Select submarkets 

Exclude specific areas from your content 

This guide explains how to configure these settings properly. 

Why Your Location Settings Matter 

Roomvu’s content engine generates posts based on your selected location. If your location is incorrect or too broad, your content may not align with the areas you actively serve. 

Setting your location correctly ensures: 

More relevant local content 

Better audience engagement 

Stronger local positioning 

Improved credibility in your target market 

How to Set Your Primary Location 

Step 1: Open Settings 

Log in to your Roomvu account and click the gear icon in the top right corner of your dashboard. 

Step : Enter Your Location 

In the Market Location section, you can: 

Enter your City or Zip Code as your Primary Location 

Add a 2nd City or County if you operate in more than one area 

Be precise. Use the exact city or zip code where you primarily serve clients. 

Selecting Submarkets for Update Videos 

After setting your main location, some content types such as submarket update videos may offer multiple location options. 

You can choose the appropriate submarket from the drop-down menu when creating or scheduling those videos. 

This allows you to tailor updates even more specifically within your broader service area. 

How to Exclude a Specific Area 

If there is a neighbourhood or city you do not want included in your content: 

Use the option to exclude locations within the Marketing Location settings 

Add the specific area you wish to block 

This ensures your content calendar does not generate posts related to that area. 

Best Practice Recommendations 

We recommend: 

Setting your most active service city as your primary location 

Adding a second location only if you consistently work there 

Excluding areas that do not align with your business focus 

Accurate location settings are essential for getting the best results from Roomvu’s hyper-local content engine.

## How Long Does It Take to Set Up My Personalized roomvu Account? | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/13927166-how-long-does-it-take-to-set-up-my-personalized-roomvu-account

How Long Does It Take to Set Up My Personalized roomvu Account? | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard

Video Guides 

How Long Does It Take to Set Up My Personalized roomvu Account? 

How Long Does It Take to Set Up My Personalized roomvu Account? 

March 4, 2026 

Table of contents 

The short answer: one hour of your time to onboard, content produced the same day, and full custom branding ready within a week. 

​ 

The longer answer covers exactly what happens during that process, what you need to prepare, and why the system is designed to require as little of your time as possible going forward. 

​ 

The Onboarding Call: One Hour, One Time 

Roomvu setup begins with a dedicated one-hour onboarding call . This is not a generic group session or a self-serve tutorial. It is a one-on-one call with a Roomvu team member who walks you through every step of account configuration. 

Here is what gets covered in that hour: 

​ 

Voice Sample Recording 

You record a voice sample that Roomvu uses to clone your voice with ElevenLabs technology. Each agent gets their own dedicated voice account. The cloned voice is used alongside your AI avatar in all video content, so every video sounds and looks like you. 

​ 

This takes a few minutes. You do not need professional recording equipment. The onboarding team guides you through the process to ensure the sample captures your natural tone and cadence. 

​ 

Avatar Setup 

Your AI avatar is configured during onboarding. This is the visual component that pairs with your cloned voice in video content. The combination creates videos where your audience sees your face and hears your voice delivering market insights and educational content. 

Branding Configuration 

Your logo, brand colors, contact information, and preferred calls to action are loaded into the system. These elements are automatically applied to every piece of content Roomvu produces for your account. No manual formatting required on your end. 

​ 

Geographic Targeting 

Your specific market area is configured so the platform automatically matches content to your territory. Market update videos will feature data from your neighborhoods, cities, and zip codes — not generic national statistics. This geographic matching is what makes the content hyper-local and relevant to your actual audience. 

​ 

Content Preview 

Before the call ends, you see a preview of what your personalized content will look like. Your voice, your branding, your market data, all assembled into a finished piece. This is the moment most agents realize the system genuinely produces content that feels like their own work. 

​ 

The Timeline After Onboarding 

Here is what happens after your one-hour call: 

Same day: Content production begins. Your first pieces of personalized content are created using the voice, avatar, and branding configured during onboarding. 

Within one week: Full custom branding and account setup is complete. Your content pipeline is live and producing. 

Ongoing: Content is populated two weeks in advance . You receive an email notification every two days before content goes live, giving you time to review, edit, or approve each piece. 

That is the entire commitment on your end. One hour to set up. A few minutes every couple of days to review what is coming. The system handles everything else. To explore the different plan levels and what each includes, visit the Roomvu pricing page . 

​ 

Addressing the "I Don't Have Time" Objection 

This is the most common reason agents hesitate. Not because they doubt the product, but because they have been burned by tools that promise automation and then demand hours of weekly management. 

Roomvu is built around the opposite principle. The system is designed to give you time back, not take more of it. 

William Hopton's data makes this concrete. In a single month using Roomvu, William achieved: 

30,701 impressions 

221 posts published 

74+ hours saved 

Seventy-four hours. That is nearly two full work weeks returned to prospecting, client meetings, showings, and the activities that directly generate revenue. The system did not add to his workload. It eliminated one of the biggest time drains in his business. 

You can read the full breakdown in the William Hopton case study . 

​ 

What You Can Customize After Setup 

A fast onboarding does not mean a rigid system. Once your account is live, you have full control to customize content on an ongoing basis: 

Rewrite scripts — adjust language, add personal insights, or change the angle on any piece of content 

Add your own templates — upload custom designs or import directly from Canva 

Change CTAs — update calls to action based on current listings, open houses, or seasonal campaigns 

Swap background footage — replace default visuals with local imagery or property-specific content 

Every customization option is accessible through your dashboard. For step-by-step guidance, the Roomvu tutorials cover each feature in detail. 

The Review Workflow: Two Minutes, Not Two Hours 

After onboarding, your ongoing time investment is minimal. The content review cycle works like this: 

Roomvu produces content matched to your market, voice, and branding 

Content is loaded into your queue two weeks before the publish date 

You receive an email notification every two days with upcoming content to review 

You approve, edit, or let it publish as-is 

Most agents spend a few minutes per review cycle. The content is already personalized to their market and brand, so edits are optional rather than necessary. The system is doing the production work. You are doing the quality control — only if and when you choose to. 

​ 

From Setup to Results 

The speed of Roomvu's onboarding is not about cutting corners. It is about removing friction between your decision to invest in content and the moment that content starts working for you. 

​ 

Agents who follow the recommended setup and posting cadence are backed by Roomvu's guarantee of 5,000 views . The Diamond plan includes a 100-lead guarantee . These are not hypothetical projections. They are commitments tied to a system that has been refined across thousands of agent accounts. 

​ 

Nick Libert used Roomvu to double his sales volume and increase transactions by 50% year over year. That trajectory started with the same one-hour onboarding call every agent gets. You can learn more about his approach in the Nick Libert case study . 

​ 

Ready to Start 

One hour to onboard. Content the same day. Full branding within a week. Seventy-four hours a month returned to your business. 

If you have been waiting for a system that respects your time while consistently building your brand, review the plan options and see which level fits where you are right now.

## How to Change the Photos Used in Your Listing Video | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/14018641-how-to-change-the-photos-used-in-your-listing-video

How to Change the Photos Used in Your Listing Video | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English

How to Change the Photos Used in Your Listing Video 

How to Change the Photos Used in Your Listing Video 

This article explains why certain listing photos appear in Roomvu listing videos and how agents can manually reorder listing images in Listing Studio to regenerate the video with the preferred photo sequence. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Sometimes agents notice that the photos used in their listing video are not the ones they expected. This usually happens because listing photos are automatically imported along with the listing data. 

​ 

When a listing is imported into Roomvu, the images are pulled from the source (such as MLS or other listing platforms) in the same order they appear on that platform . Since listing videos use a selection of these images, there is a chance that similar or less important photos may be included. 

While our system works to select the most relevant images automatically, you can easily reorder the photos yourself to control which ones appear in the video. 

Why Your Listing Video May Show Certain Photos 

When a listing is imported: 

All listing photos are imported in their original order 

The listing video is generated based on that order 

If similar or less important photos appear earlier in the sequence, they may be used in the video 

Fortunately, you can adjust the order manually. 

How to Reorder Your Listing Photos 

Step 1: Go to MLS Listings 

Log in to your Roomvu account and click MLS Listing on the main dashboard. 

Step 2: Select Your Listing 

Find the listing you would like to update. 

Step 3: Open Listing Studio 

Click Listing Studio for that listing. 

Step 4: Go to Images 

Click the Images section. 

Here you will see all the photos that were imported with your listing and the order they appear in. 

Step 5: Reorder the Photos 

You can drag and drop the images to change their order. 

Place the most important photos first, such as: 

Exterior front photo 

Main living areas 

Kitchen highlights 

Key features of the property 

This helps the video focus on the strongest visuals. 

Step 6: Save Your Changes 

After adjusting the order, click Save . 

Roomvu will regenerate the listing video using the updated image order. 

Tips for Better Listing Videos 

To improve your listing video quality: 

Place your best photos at the top of the image order 

Avoid repeating similar images in the first few positions 

Prioritize photos that clearly showcase the property 

This gives the video a stronger visual flow and better presentation.

How to Add an Open House Banner to Your Listing Video or Image

## How to Choose and Submit Your Platinum Design | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/14034201-how-to-choose-and-submit-your-platinum-design

How to Choose and Submit Your Platinum Design | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Video Guides 

How to Choose and Submit Your Platinum Design 

How to Choose and Submit Your Platinum Design 

Learn what Platinum Designs are, how roomvu's handcrafted branding system works, and follow a step-by-step guide to browse design styles, submit your branding details, and get a personalized design. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

What Is a Platinum Design? 

Platinum Design is roomvu's handcrafted, personalized branding system for real estate professionals. Rather than offering a generic template, roomvu's design team creates a complete visual identity tailored specifically to you — incorporating your name, photo, logo, brand colors, market, and niche. This design system is then automatically applied across all the social media content Roomvu creates for you, including social posts, story layouts, cover images, video intros, video outros, and more. 

The key idea is brand consistency 

once your Platinum Design is set up, every piece of content roomvu produces for you will have a cohesive, professional look that makes your content instantly recognizable to your audience on platforms like Instagram, Facebook, and LinkedIn. 

Platinum Designs are created by real human designers (not auto-generated from cookie-cutter templates) and are optimized for social media formats. They are also automatically applied to every new piece of content Roomvu creates for you going forward, so there's no manual work on your end once the design is live. 

How It Works 

The process follows three simple steps: 

Step 1 — Choose Your Design Style 

You browse the Platinum Design gallery on the page and select a visual style that matches your vibe. Designs are organized into three categories depending on your use case: Individual, Team, and Brokerage. Each design has a preview thumbnail and a short description of its aesthetic. 

Step 2 — Submit Your Details 

After selecting a design, you scroll down to the submission form and provide your personal and branding information. This tells the Roomvu design team what they need to customize the design specifically for you. 

Step 3 — roomvu Personalizes and Applies It 

The roomvu team handcrafts the design to match your brand and applies it to your content stream. Most customizations are completed within 1–2 business days. The design goes live automatically — you won't receive a preview first, but you can always send comments afterward and the team will make adjustments. 

For videos specifically, every video gets the full Platinum treatment: a branded intro (your logo, name, and colors open every video), custom content overlays and design elements throughout, and a branded outro with your contact info and a call to action. 

Step-by-Step Guide 

1. Navigate to the Platinum Designs Page 

Go to the Platinum Designs page . You can also find the option in your settings under Branding Theme . 

2. Browse the Design Gallery 

Scroll down to the "Select Your Platinum Design" section. At the top of the gallery, you'll see three tabs: 

Individual 

Solo designs for individual agents. Each features a unique visual style, such as navy accents, cityscape backgrounds, teal highlights, geometric patterns, or gold luxury themes. 

Team 

Designs built for real estate teams and partnerships. These showcase multiple agent photos and unified team branding. 

Brokerage 

Designs tailored for brokerage-level branding. These prominently feature brokerage logos and corporate color schemes from brands like Primerica, Chubb, Farmers, ERA, Keyes, and more. 

Click on the tab that matches your situation, then browse the design previews. 

3. Select a Design 

Once you find a design you like, click the "Select" button underneath it. Then click "Continue to form" 

4. Fill Out the Submission Form 

Scroll down to the "Submit Your Selection" section. The form will show which design you selected at the top. Fill in the following fields: 

Full Name (required) — Your full name as you want it displayed. 

Email (required) — Your email address. 

Phone (optional) — Your phone number. 

Company / Brokerage (required) — The name of your brokerage or company. 

Role (required) — Select your role from the dropdown menu. 

City / Market (required) — The city or market area you serve. 

Color Preference (required) — Choose one of three options: "I have my own brand colors (I'll provide hex codes)," "Use my brokerage's official colors," or "Help me choose colors." 

Do you want custom background footage for videos? (required) — Choose whether you'd like custom city skyline or neighborhood footage in your videos, standard backgrounds, or if you'd like to discuss it. 

Additional Notes (optional) — A free-text field where you can mention specific logos to include, your desired vibe, niche, audience, or any Equal Housing/REALTOR® logo requirements. 

5. Confirm and Submit 

Check the confirmation box that reads "I confirm this is my final selection (we'll customize it to me)." Then click the **Submit Selection** button to send your request to the Roomvu design team. 

6. Wait for Your Design to Go Live 

Most Platinum Designs are completed within 1–2 business days. The design will be applied directly to your content; there is no preview step. Once it's live, you can send feedback or request adjustments. 

Additional Things to Know 

You don't need a logo or brand kit to get started. 

Many agents don't have one. Just mention it in the notes section and the Roomvu team will work with whatever you have; even if it's just your name and preferred colors. They can guide you through simple brand choices. 

Logos and compliance marks are supported. 

roomvu can embed any logos you need, including Equal Housing, REALTOR®, your brokerage logo, team logo, or personal brand mark. If you need multiple logos on your content, they can arrange them cleanly in a single design. 

You can switch designs later. 

roomvu recommends keeping a design for at least 2–3 months for brand consistency, but you can always ask to change your design or background afterward. 

Team and Brokerage designs scale. 

If you're on a Team or Brokerage plan, Roomvu can create variations for each team member while keeping consistent branding across the entire group. 

Need help choosing? 

If you're unsure which design is right for you, describe your vibe in the Additional Notes field and the Roomvu team will guide you to the right fit. You can also use the Contact link in the footer for direct assistance. 

What changed? 

Previously, setting up your Platinum Design required several manual steps and coordination with our team, which could extend the timeline. The new process replaces this with a streamlined intake page where you submit everything in one go. 

How it works 

Visit the intake page at extra.roomvu.com/platinum-designs 

Select your preferred design style. 

Submit your branding information and any relevant details. 

Our design team prepares your setup within 2 business days. 

Your finalized designs are automatically added to your content calendar, ready to go live. 

What stays the same? 

Your branding and personalization remain at the center of every design. The new process is simply a faster way to get your customized content live. 

Will more design styles be added? 

Yes. We are continuously expanding the styles available on the intake page, so you will see new options added over time. 

Does this apply to design updates too? 

Yes. Going forward, all new designs as well as updates to existing designs will be handled through the intake page at extra.roomvu.com/platinum-designs. 

If you have any questions about the new process, please reach out to our support team and we will be happy to help.

How to Edit Contacts for Email Marketing in Roomvu 

How to Edit Contacts for Email Marketing in Roomvu 

This article explains how to edit contacts in Roomvu email marketing, including accessing the All Contacts section, reviewing contact categories, editing contact details, and updating contact information. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

roomvu allows you to manage and update your contact list easily for your email marketing campaigns. If a contact’s name or email address needs to be corrected or updated, you can edit it directly from your contact list. 

This guide explains how to edit your contacts inside the Email Campaigns section. 

Why You May Need to Edit a Contact 

You may want to edit a contact if: 

The name is misspelled 

The email address needs to be updated 

You want to correct or organize your contact list 

Keeping your contacts accurate helps ensure your email campaigns reach the right people. 

How to Edit a Contact 

Step 1: Go to Email Campaigns 

Log in to your Roomvu account and click Email Newsletters from the left menu. 

Step 2: Open All Contacts 

Click All Contacts to view your contact lists. 

Step 3: Choose the Contact Category 

Select the contact category you want to edit and click Review . 

This will open the list of contacts in that category. 

Step 4: Edit the Contact 

Find the contact you want to update and click the pen icon next to their name. 

You can now edit: 

First Name 

Last Name 

Email Address 

Step 5: Save the Changes 

After making your updates, click Update Contact to save the changes. 

Your contact information will now be updated in your list. 

Tips for Managing Your Contacts 

Regularly review your contact lists to keep them accurate 

Correct misspelled names or outdated emails 

Maintain clean contact lists to improve email campaign performance 

Clean contact lists help improve deliverability and engagement. 

Need Help? 

If you are unable to edit a contact or need assistance managing your contact lists, contact our support team and we will help you.

## How to Upload Your Own Content to roomvu | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/14047139-how-to-upload-your-own-content-to-roomvu

How to Upload Your Own Content to roomvu | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard

Your Dashboard 
English

Search for articles... 

All Collections

How to Upload Your Own Content to roomvu 

How to Upload Your Own Content to roomvu 

This article explains how users can upload their own videos or images to Roomvu, write captions, select social media platforms, and schedule posts through the Content Calendar. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Many users ask if they can upload their own videos or images to Roomvu and share them through the platform. The answer is yes. 

Roomvu allows you to upload your own content and use its powerful publishing engine to distribute it across multiple social media platforms. This means you do not need to manually upload and post your content on each social network one by one. 

You can upload your content once and schedule it to be shared automatically. 

What Types of Content Can You Upload? 

You can upload: 

MP4 videos (up to 250MB) 

Images 

This feature is useful if you want to share: 

Personal videos 

Listing walkthroughs 

Market commentary 

Behind-the-scenes content 

Lifestyle posts 

It helps you combine your own content with Roomvu’s automated content strategy. 

How to Upload Your Own Content 

Step 1: Open Content Calendar 

Log in to your Roomvu account and click Content Calendar on your main dashboard. 

Step 2: Click Add Content 

In the top right corner of the Content Calendar page, click Add Content . 

Step 3: Select Upload Your Content 

Scroll down and find the option Upload Your Content , then click it. 

Step 4: Upload Your File 

Click Upload and select your file. 

You can upload: 

MP4 videos up to 250MB 

Image files 

Once uploaded, you will be able to preview the file. 

Step 5: Write Your Caption 

Add the caption you want to accompany the post. Make sure it is less than 160 characters. 

This caption will appear on the social media platforms where the content is shared. 

Step 6: Choose Social Media Platforms 

Select the social media accounts where you want the content to be posted. 

You can share the same content across multiple platforms at once. 

Step 7: Schedule Your Post 

Choose the date and time you want the content to be published. 

Roomvu will schedule the post on your content calendar. 

Step 8: Schedule the Content 

Once everything is ready, click Schedule . 

Your content will now appear in your Content Calendar and will be published automatically at the selected time. 

Why Upload Your Own Content? 

Uploading your own content allows you to: 

Share personal updates with your audience 

Post listing walkthroughs or announcements 

Combine automation with personal branding 

Save time by scheduling posts across multiple platforms 

Using both Roomvu-generated content and your own uploads creates a stronger and more balanced content strategy.

## How to Share Your VuCard as a QR Code | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/14075908-how-to-share-your-vucard-as-a-qr-code

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English
