How to Share Your VuCard as a QR Code 

How to Share Your VuCard as a QR Code 

Learn how to turn your free Roomvu VuCard link into a QR code using Bitly, and share it across social media, email signatures, and print materials. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Your VuCard is your free digital business card on Roomvu, and one of the most creative ways to share it is by turning your VuCard link into a QR code. Anyone who scans it will land directly on your VuCard page. You can place it on your social media posts, email signature, printed flyers, video content, and more. 

Here is how to do it in a few simple steps. 

Step 1: Copy Your VuCard Link 

Log in to your Roomvu account. 

Click the gear icon in the top right corner to open Settings. 

Scroll down the left menu until you find the VuCard section. 

Click the Copy button to copy your VuCard link. 

Step 2: Create a QR Code on Bitly 

Go to bitly.com and sign up for a free account, or log in if you already have one. 

Once inside your dashboard, click Create new and select QR Code from the options. 

Paste your VuCard link into the Destination URL field. 

Add a title if needed. 

Click "Design your code" 

On the next page customize the look of the QR code if needed. When done click "Create Your Code" 

Download your QR code in JPEG, PNG, or SVG format. 

Step 3: Share It 

You can now use your QR code anywhere: 

Add it to your social media posts or stories 

Include it in your email signature 

Place it on printed marketing materials like flyers or business cards 

Overlay it on your video content 

Good to Know: Bitly QR Code Limitations 

Bitly QR codes never expire. They will only stop working if you delete the link used to generate them. bitly 

All Bitly QR codes can be scanned an unlimited number of times, regardless of which plan you are on. bitly 

Free plan users can create up to 200 QR codes per month. bitly 

Customization options like branded colors, logos, and the ability to redirect your QR code to a new URL later are available on Bitly's paid plans. 

If you have any questions about your VuCard, contact our support team and we will be happy to help.

## Why Is My Uploaded Image Getting Cut Off in the Slideshow? | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/14087966-why-is-my-uploaded-image-getting-cut-off-in-the-slideshow

Why Is My Uploaded Image Getting Cut Off in the Slideshow? | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Tutorials 

Why Is My Uploaded Image Getting Cut Off in the Slideshow? 

Why Is My Uploaded Image Getting Cut Off in the Slideshow? 

Explains why custom uploaded images may appear cropped in Roomvu slideshows. Image cropping occurs when the uploaded photo dimensions do not match the slide frame size. Includes tips on how to prepare images correctly before uploading. 

March 17, 2026 

Table of contents 

If you notice that an image looks fine while editing a slide but appears cropped or cut off in the preview or final post, this is expected behavior and comes down to the difference between your image dimensions and the frame size used in that particular slide. 

Why does this happen? 

Each slide in a Roomvu slideshow uses a specific frame shape and size. When you upload a custom image, the system fits it into that frame. If your image dimensions do not match the frame, parts of the image will be cropped to fill it. 

For example, if the slide frame is vertical but your photo is square or horizontal, the top and bottom of the image may be cut off to fill the vertical frame correctly. The same applies in reverse. 

Why does it look fine while editing but cropped in the preview? 

The editing view gives you a general look at how your content is coming together, but the final preview and published post reflect the actual frame dimensions. This is why the crop may not be obvious until you hit preview. 

What can I do to avoid this? 

The best way to avoid unwanted cropping is to match your image to the frame before uploading. Here is what we recommend: 

Before uploading, take note of the frame shape in the slide you are editing. Is it vertical, square, or horizontal? 

Resize or crop your image to match that shape before uploading it. 

When uploading, use the built-in crop tool to adjust your image for the frame. However remember that this is only used to crop it considering the frame. 

Always check the preview before publishing to confirm the image looks the way you want. 

Key things to keep in mind 

The frame in the slide is the size that matters most. Always treat it as your reference point when preparing images. 

Images from the Roomvu library are already optimized for the slide frames, so if cropping is a concern, choosing from our library is a reliable alternative. 

Different slides within the same slideshow may use different frame sizes, so check each slide individually. 

If you are unsure about the correct dimensions for a specific frame or need help with your slideshow, reach out to our support team and we will be happy to assist.

How to Add, Remove, or Modify Your Hashtags on roomvu 

How to Add, Remove, or Modify Your Hashtags on roomvu 

Step-by-step guide on how to add, remove, and customize hashtags on Roomvu. Users can manage up to 10 hashtags through the Content Calendar settings to better match their brand and target audience. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Roomvu automatically assigns default hashtags to your social media content based on your business type and location. However, you have full control over these hashtags and can customize them to better fit your personal brand and target audience. 

​ 

How to update your hashtags 

From the main page, click Content Calendar in the left menu. 

Click Edit next to Calendar Settings. 

Click the Hashtags tab, which is the last tab in the settings. 

You will see your currently active hashtags displayed here. 

Add or remove hashtags as needed. You can either type your own or pick from the suggestions shown in the same window. 

Click Save when you are done. 

Things to keep in mind 

You can have up to 10 hashtags defined at a time. 

When typing hashtags, do not include spaces between words. Either remove the spaces entirely or use an underscore instead, for example #openhouse or #open_house. 

The suggestions shown in the hashtag window are a great starting point if you are not sure which hashtags to use for your market. 

Your hashtags will be applied to your upcoming content automatically once saved. 

If you have any questions or run into any issues while updating your hashtags, feel free to reach out to our support team and we will be happy to help.

How to Turn Any News Article into a Branded Video or Image Using News2Video 

Learn how to use Roomvu's News2Video feature to turn any news article into a branded video or image. Share relevant content with your audience across social media and email in just a few steps, complete with your branding and an optional personal intro. 

March 19, 2026 

Table of contents 

Staying relevant with your audience means sharing timely, valuable content. With Roomvu's News2Video feature, you can turn any news article you find interesting into a branded video or image and share it with your network in just a few steps. No design skills required. 

​ 

This is a great way to position yourself as a knowledgeable resource in your market while keeping your branding front and center on every piece of content you share. 

How to use News2Video 

Log in to your Roomvu account and scroll down to the More Tools section on the main page. 

Click News2Video .

Why use News2Video? 

Share timely news with your network without creating content from scratch. 

Every piece of content is automatically branded with your information.

Works across social media, email, and more, all from within Roomvu.

## How to Use Social Bio Coach to Improve Your Social Media Profile | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/14167068-how-to-use-social-bio-coach-to-improve-your-social-media-profile

How to Use Social Bio Coach to Improve Your Social Media Profile | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Video Guides 

How to Use Social Bio Coach to Improve Your Social Media Profile 

How to Use Social Bio Coach to Improve Your Social Media Profile 

Learn how to use Roomvu's Social Bio Coach to analyze and improve your social media profile. Upload a screenshot of your bio on Instagram, Facebook, LinkedIn, and more to get instant AI-powered feedback on branding, discoverability, and client attraction. 

March 23, 2026 

Table of contents 

Your social media bio is often the first impression a potential client gets of you. With Roomvu's Social Bio Coach, you can instantly analyze your profile on any major social media platform and get detailed, actionable feedback to improve your branding, boost your credibility, and attract more clients. 

​ 

This feature is available for real estate agents, mortgage brokers, insurance agents, and financial advisors. 

​ 

Why Your Social Media Bio Matters More Than You Think 

In today's digital-first world, potential clients do not wait for a referral or a cold call to form an opinion about you. They search for you online first. Whether someone finds you through a hashtag, a shared post, or a direct search, your social media profile is almost always the first place they land. And your bio is the first thing they read. 

Studies consistently show that people decide within seconds whether to follow, engage with, or move on from a profile. A vague, cluttered, or incomplete bio sends potential clients elsewhere, often straight to a competitor. On the other hand, a well-crafted bio that clearly communicates who you are, who you serve, and what makes you different can turn a casual profile visitor into a lead. 

​ 

For real estate agents, mortgage brokers, insurance agents, and financial advisors, this matters even more. Your clients are making some of the biggest financial decisions of their lives. Before they trust you with those decisions, they need to feel confident in your credibility. Your bio is where that trust either starts to build or falls apart. 

​ 

A strong bio does several things at once. It tells visitors exactly what you do and who you help. It positions you as an expert in your market. It gives people a reason to follow you and a clear next step to take. And it uses the right keywords so that the platform's search algorithm can actually surface your profile to the right audience. 

The problem is that most professionals set up their bio once and never revisit it. 

​ 

Platforms change, best practices evolve, and what worked two years ago may be actively hurting your discoverability today. Without an outside perspective grounded in current best practices, it is almost impossible to know what your bio is missing. 

This is exactly why Social Bio Coach exists. 

​ 

What platforms does Social Bio Coach support? 

Instagram 

Facebook 

LinkedIn 

TikTok 

Twitter / X 

Google My Business 

How to use Social Bio Coach 

From your Roomvu dashboard, scroll down to the More Tools section. 

Click Social Bio Coach . 

In the pop-up window, click Scan My Profile . 

Select your business field , for example Real Estate, Mortgage, Insurance, or Financial Advisory. 

Select the platform you want to analyze, for example Instagram or Facebook. 

Upload a screenshot of your bio section. You can either upload an image file or press Ctrl + V to paste a screenshot directly from your clipboard. 

The system will analyze your profile and generate a full report. 

What does the report include? 

Social Bio Coach provides an extensive breakdown of your profile, covering areas such as: 

What is working well in your current bio and profile setup 

Areas that need improvement, including your bio copy, call-to-action, and use of keywords 

Specific suggestions to improve discoverability and attract more profile visitors 

Tips tailored to your business type and the platform you are on 

Recommendations for content strategy and audience growth 

The feedback is based on proven social media best practices that increase profile visibility and build trust with potential clients. 

​ 

How often should I use Social Bio Coach? 

It is a good idea to scan your profile any time you make changes to your bio, rebrand, change your focus market, or simply want a fresh perspective. Running a scan every few months also helps you stay aligned with current best practices as platforms continue to evolve. 

​ 

Why does this matter for your business? 

Think of Social Bio Coach as having a social media strategist review your profile on demand, at no extra cost. Instead of guessing whether your bio is effective or paying for an expensive audit, you get instant, specific, and actionable feedback tailored to your profession and the platform you are on. 

​ 

Every improvement you make to your bio compounds over time. Better keyword placement means more people discover your profile. A clearer value proposition means more visitors choose to follow you. A stronger call-to-action means more of those followers actually reach out. These are not small gains. Over months and years, an optimized bio can be one of the most impactful and lowest-effort things you do for your business. 

​ 

If you have any questions about Social Bio Coach or need help interpreting your report, reach out to our support team and we will be happy to assist.

## How to Use AI Lead Receptionist to Capture and Follow Up with Leads Automatically | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/14182177-how-to-use-ai-lead-receptionist-to-capture-and-follow-up-with-leads-automatically

How to Use AI Lead Receptionist to Capture and Follow Up with Leads Automatically | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Video Guides 

How to Use AI Lead Receptionist to Capture and Follow Up with Leads Automatically 

How to Use AI Lead Receptionist to Capture and Follow Up with Leads Automatically 

Learn how to use Roomvu's AI Lead Receptionist to automatically capture, categorize, and follow up with leads from any platform. Set up your dedicated lead capture email to connect your CRM and never miss a lead again. 

March 24, 2026 

Table of contents 

Missing a lead is one of the most costly things that can happen in your business. With Roomvu's AI Lead Receptionist, you never have to worry about that again. This feature automatically captures leads from any platform, categorizes them, notifies you instantly, and even calls leads and books meetings on your behalf, so you can focus on closing deals while the system handles the follow-up. 

What does AI Lead Receptionist do? 

Captures leads from any platform automatically 

Categorizes and saves contacts to your account 

Notifies you instantly when a new lead comes in 

Calls leads and books meetings for you 

Your Dedicated Lead Capture Email 

Every Roomvu user gets a personal lead capture email address that looks like this: 

yourname-lead@updates.housing-trends.com 

This is the core of how the feature works. Any lead email forwarded to this address is automatically parsed and saved to your account as a contact, no manual data entry required. 

How to Find Your Lead Capture Email Address 

Log in to your Roomvu account and scroll down to the More Tools section on the main dashboard. 

Click AI Lead Receptionist . 

Your personal lead capture email address will be displayed in the pop-up window. 

Click Copy to copy it and use it as instructed in the setup steps below. 

How it works 

You receive a lead through your CRM, website contact form, or any other system. 

Forward that email to your dedicated lead capture email address. 

The system automatically extracts the lead's information including their name, email, phone number, and message. 

The lead is saved to your Roomvu account automatically. 

If the system is unable to parse the email, you will receive a notification so you never miss a lead. 

How to set it up in your CRM 

Most CRMs allow you to set up email forwarding or automated routing rules. Here are the general steps: 

Copy your personal lead capture email address from your Roomvu account. 

Go to your CRM's email settings or automation rules section. 

Set up email forwarding or create an automation rule that forwards incoming lead emails to your lead capture address. 

Send a test email to your lead capture address to confirm everything is working correctly. 

Email format best practices 

The system is designed to extract lead information from a variety of email formats. While vCard format provides the most reliable parsing, plain text formats work as well. Supported formats include structured text, standard email body format, and vCard format. 

What if the system cannot read the email? 

If the system is unable to automatically parse an incoming email, you will receive a notification at your registered email address. That notification will include the original email content, the sender's information, and the subject line, so you always have everything you need to follow up manually if necessary. 

​ 

Please note that these notification emails can sometimes end up in your spam folder, so it is worth checking there if you are expecting a lead notification that has not arrived. 

Need help setting it up? 

If you need assistance configuring email forwarding in your specific CRM or have any questions about this feature, contact our support team and provide the following: 

Your roomvu profile slug 

The CRM system you are using 

A description of the issue you are experiencing 

Our team will get you set up as quickly as possible.

## How to Get Help with Billing, Invoices, and Account Charges | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/14197715-how-to-get-help-with-billing-invoices-and-account-charges

How to Get Help with Billing, Invoices, and Account Charges | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content

All Collections

How to Get Help with Billing, Invoices, and Account Charges 

How to Get Help with Billing, Invoices, and Account Charges 

Billing issues including cancellations, invoices, refunds, and charge inquiries are handled exclusively via email at info@roomvu.com. Support sessions do not cover billing matters. 

March 25, 2026 

Table of contents 

For any questions or issues related to billing, we have a dedicated process to make sure your request reaches the right team as quickly as possible. 

​ 

What counts as a billing issue? 

Subscription cancellations 

Invoice details or clarification 

Refund requests 

Unexpected charges 

Payment failures 

Any other account charge related questions 

How to get help 

For all billing related issues, please send an email to info@roomvu.com describing your issue. Once your email is received, a support ticket is automatically created and assigned to our billing team who will address it as quickly as possible. 

This is the fastest and most reliable way to get your billing issue resolved. Emailing us creates a formal record of your request and ensures it is routed directly to the team best equipped to help you. 

​ 

Please note: Billing issues are not handled through support sessions 

Our support sessions are designed to help you get the most out of your Roomvu account, covering topics like setup, features, content, and technical questions. Billing related matters fall outside the scope of these sessions and cannot be addressed during a support call. 

​ 

If you book a support session and bring up a billing issue during the call, our support representative will ask you to follow up by sending an email to info@roomvu.com so it can be properly handled by the billing team. 

​ 

To save time, we recommend emailing us directly before booking a session if your question is related to billing. 

​ 

Summary 

Issue Type 

How to Get Help 

Billing, invoices, refunds, cancellations 

Email info@roomvu.com 

Account setup, features, technical issues 

Book a support session 

If you are unsure whether your issue is billing related, you are always welcome to email us at info@roomvu.com and our team will point you in the right direction.

## How to Use the Beauty Filter When Recording Your Intro or Face Message Videos | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/14198203-how-to-use-the-beauty-filter-when-recording-your-intro-or-face-message-videos

How to Use the Beauty Filter When Recording Your Intro or Face Message Videos | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Video Guides 

How to Use the Beauty Filter When Recording Your Intro or Face Message Videos 

How to Use the Beauty Filter When Recording Your Intro or Face Message Videos 

Learn how to use Roomvu's new Beauty Filter when recording intro and face message videos. Choose from a range of filter styles to enhance your on-camera appearance before recording. Works best with good lighting and a decent camera. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

When you record an intro or face message video on Roomvu, you want to look your best. That is why we have added the Beauty Filter feature to our video recording tools. With a range of filter options to choose from, you can enhance your on-camera appearance and present yourself more professionally to your audience, directly from within Roomvu. 

What is the Beauty Filter? 

The Beauty Filter is a camera enhancement tool that improves your appearance in real time while you record. It helps smooth out minor imperfections and compensates for small inconsistencies in image quality, giving your videos a more polished and professional look. 

This feature was inspired by similar tools used in major video conferencing platforms, and was added to Roomvu based on direct feedback from our users. 

Important things to know before you start 

The Beauty Filter works best when your recording environment is already set up well. Keep the following in mind: 

The filter can help with minor appearance imperfections and moderate image quality issues. 

It will not fully compensate for poor lighting. Make sure you are recording in a well-lit space, ideally with light facing you rather than behind you. 

It will not make up for a very low quality camera. For the best results, use the best camera available to you. 

How to access and use the Beauty Filter 

From your Roomvu dashboard, click on any video in your Content Calendar . 

Click Add Face Message . 

Choose between Intro Video or Face Message depending on your preference. 

Before you start recording, click Apply Effects . 

Here you will find a range of recording effects including background blur, mirror image, and virtual backgrounds. 

Click on the Beauty Filter option to see the available filter styles. 

Choose the filter that works best for your look and recording environment. 

Once you are happy with your selection, start recording. 

Available Beauty Filter options 

Roomvu offers a wide range of Beauty Filter styles to suit different looks, lighting conditions, and preferences: 

Off - No filter applied 

Natural - Subtle, everyday enhancement 

Studio - Clean and professional look suited for indoor recordings 

Interview - Polished appearance ideal for a formal or professional setting 

Soft Light - Gentle brightening with a soft tone 

Bright - Adds brightness and clarity to your image 

Pro Portrait - Professional-grade enhancement for a refined look 

Warm - Adds warm tones for a friendly and approachable feel 

Outdoor - Optimized for recordings in natural or outdoor light 

Cool - Adds cooler tones for a crisp, modern look 

Matte - Smooth, flat finish with reduced shine 

Vivid - Boosts color and contrast for a vibrant appearance 

Fresh - Light and clean look with a natural glow 

Crisp - Sharp and clear with enhanced definition 

Polished - Refined and camera-ready finish 

We recommend trying a few options before recording to find the one that works best for your specific lighting and camera setup. 

What other effects are available in Apply Effects? 

In addition to the Beauty Filter, the Apply Effects panel also gives you access to: 

Background Blur - Blurs your surroundings to keep the focus on you 

Mirror Image - Flips your camera image horizontally 

Virtual Backgrounds - Replace your background with a custom or preset image 

If you have any questions about the Beauty Filter or need help with your recording setup, reach out to our support team and we will be happy to help.

## Why Is roomvu Not Posting to My WordPress Website? | Roomvu Help Center

Why Is roomvu Not Posting to My WordPress Website? 

Why Is roomvu Not Posting to My WordPress Website? 

If roomvu is not posting to your WordPress website, an outdated Roomvu Marketing plugin is a common cause. Learn how to update the plugin and enable auto-updates in your WordPress admin dashboard to restore seamless posting. 

March 30, 2026 

Table of contents 

If Roomvu is not posting content to your WordPress website as expected, one of the most common causes is an outdated Roomvu Marketing plugin. Keeping your plugin up to date ensures a smooth and reliable connection between roomvu and your website. 

​ 

Why does this happen? 

As roomvu releases updates to improve performance and compatibility, older versions of the plugin may lose the ability to communicate properly with our platform. This can result in posts failing to publish or the integration appearing to stop working altogether. Updating to the latest version of the plugin resolves most of these issues. 

​ 

How to update the roomvu Marketing plugin 

Log in to your WordPress website's Admin Dashboard . 

In the left sidebar menu, click Plugins . 

Search for Roomvu Marketing in your plugin list. 

If an update is available, click Update to install the latest version. 

How to enable auto-updates 

To make sure this does not happen again in the future, we strongly recommend enabling automatic updates for the Roomvu Marketing plugin. This way, your plugin will always stay up to date without you having to check manually. 

In your plugin list, find the Roomvu Marketing plugin. 

Click Enable Auto-Updates next to the plugin. 

Once auto-updates are enabled, WordPress will automatically install the latest version of the Roomvu Marketing plugin whenever a new update is released, keeping your integration running smoothly at all times. 

​ 

Still having issues after updating? 

If your WordPress integration is still not working after updating the plugin and enabling auto-updates, please reach out to our support team at info@roomvu.com with the following details: 

Your Roomvu account email 

Your WordPress website URL 

A description of the issue you are experiencing 

Our team will investigate and get your integration back on track as quickly as possible.

How to Customize the Services Shown on Your Roomvu Profile and Landing Pages 

Learn how to customize the services displayed on your Roomvu profile and landing pages. Check or uncheck services from your account settings to show only what you offer. 

Updated over a month ago 

Table of contents 

roomvu displays a set of services on your profile, landing pages, and website based on your business type. By default, all available services are enabled for your account. If there are services you do not offer or do not want shown, you can easily customize this list to reflect exactly what you do. 

​ 

Why does this matter? 

Showing only the services you actually offer helps you come across as more focused and relevant to potential clients. A cluttered or inaccurate services section can create confusion and undermine trust. Keeping it clean and accurate ensures visitors to your profile or landing page immediately understand what you specialize in. 

​ 

Default services by business type 

roomvu provides a tailored set of services depending on your business field. Here is what is available for each: 

Business Type 

Available Services 

Real Estate Agents 

Home Buying, Home Selling, Real Estate Investments, Property Management, Luxury & High-Value Homes, Pre Construction 

Commercial Real Estate 

Commercial Real Estate, Office Properties, Retail Spaces, Industrial & Warehouses

Retirement Planning, Investment Strategies, Wealth Management, Tax Planning, Estate Planning, Investing For Kids

Insurance Agents

How to customize your services

In the left menu, scroll down to the Content Customization section. 

Click Landing Pages / Services . 

Scroll down to find the Services section. 

Check or uncheck any services you want to show or hide. 

Click Save when you are done. 

Your changes will be applied immediately across your Roomvu profile, landing pages, and website. 

Things to keep in mind 

All services are enabled by default when you first set up your account. 

You can come back and update your services at any time as your business evolves. 

If you offer a service that is not listed, please reach out to our support team at info@roomvu.com and we will look into adding it for you.

## What Is the Difference Between roomvu's Organic Content and Smart Ads? | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/14407012-what-is-the-difference-between-roomvu-s-organic-content-and-smart-ads

What Is the Difference Between roomvu's Organic Content and Smart Ads? | Roomvu Help Center

What Is the Difference Between roomvu's Organic Content and Smart Ads? 

What Is the Difference Between roomvu's Organic Content and Smart Ads? 

Many users refer to organic posts as "ads," which are actually automated branded content published to their social profiles. Smart Ads are a separate paid service targeting new audiences on Facebook and Instagram. 

Updated over a week ago 

Table of contents 

If you have ever referred to the posts roomvu shares on your social media as "ads," you are not alone. Many of our users use the word "ads" to describe any content that goes out on their behalf, which is completely understandable. However, there is an important difference between the two types of content roomvu offers, and knowing the difference helps us resolve your questions faster and more accurately. 

Organic Social Media Content 

When you sign up with roomvu, we automatically create and publish content on your social media accounts on a regular basis. This includes market update videos, real estate tips, community content, and other branded posts that go out on your Facebook, Instagram, and other connected platforms. 

This content is organic, meaning it is not paid advertising. It appears on your social media profile just like any post you would publish yourself. Your followers and connections can see it, engage with it, like it, comment on it, and share it. There is no ad budget involved and roomvu manages the entire content creation and publishing process for you. 

When most of our users say "my ads are not posting" or "can you change my ads," they are typically referring to this organic content. 

roomvu Smart Ads 

roomvu also offers a separate paid advertising service called Smart Ads. This is a completely different product. Smart Ads are actual paid advertisements that roomvu sets up and runs for you on Facebook and Instagram. These ads are targeted to a specific audience beyond your existing followers, use a dedicated ad budget, and are designed to generate new leads by reaching people who do not already know you. 

Smart Ads involve a separate setup process, a separate budget, and deliver a different type of result compared to organic content. 

Quick Reference 

Organic Content 

Smart Ads 

What it is 

Regular branded posts published to your social media profiles 

Paid advertisements run on Facebook and Instagram 

Who sees it 

Your existing followers and connections 

Targeted audiences beyond your followers 

Cost 

Included in your roomvu subscription 

Requires a separate ad budget 

Purpose 

Build brand awareness and stay top of mind 

Generate new leads and reach new audiences 

Setup 

Fully managed and automated by roomvu 

Set up separately through roomvu's Smart Ads service 

Why this matters when you contact support 

When you reach out about an issue with your "ads," our support team and AI assistant will consider both possibilities. To help us get you the right answer faster, it helps to provide a little extra context, for example: 

"The posts roomvu is publishing on my Facebook page are not going out" refers to organic content . 

"The paid ad campaign I am running on Facebook is not generating leads" refers to Smart Ads . 

The more context you provide, the faster and more accurately we can help you.

## Not Receiving the Constant Contact Verification Email? | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/14431472-not-receiving-the-constant-contact-verification-email

Not Receiving the Constant Contact Verification Email? | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Video Guides 

Not Receiving the Constant Contact Verification Email? 

Not Receiving the Constant Contact Verification Email? 

Guide for roomvu Platinum users who have not received the Constant Contact verification email. Covers common reasons the email may be missing and step-by-step instructions for resending the verification email from within Constant Contact settings. 

Updated over a week ago 

Table of contents 

When activating your email marketing integration with roomvu, you will receive a verification email from Constant Contact to the email address associated with your roomvu account. In most cases this email arrives within a few minutes, but occasionally users report not seeing it in their inbox. 

​ 

Before requesting a new verification email, here are the two most common reasons this happens: 

The verification email has landed in your spam or junk folder . Check there first before taking any further steps. 

You may be checking the wrong email inbox . Make sure you are looking in the inbox associated with the email address you used to sign up for roomvu. 

If you have checked both and still cannot find the verification email, here is how to request a new one. 

​ 

Important: This feature requires a Platinum plan 

The Constant Contact email marketing integration is only available to users on the roomvu Platinum plan. Make sure your account is on the correct plan before proceeding. 

How to resend the Constant Contact verification email 

In your roomvu account, go to the Email Newsletters section. 

Click Login to access your Constant Contact account. 

​ 

Once inside Constant Contact, click your username in the top right corner. 

Click Settings from the dropdown menu. 

In the Settings window, click the Account Emails tab. 

Under the Email Addresses section, find your email address. It is usually listed in the second row. 

Click the three dots next to your email address. 

Click Resend Verification Email . 

The verification email will be sent to your email address again. Check your inbox and spam folder, and click Verify in the email to complete the activation.

Outro Slides on roomvu 

Outro Slides on roomvu 

The outro slide appears in the last 3 seconds of all videos and can be customized with additional phone numbers, credentials, a website, and a slogan. AI Portraits are separate static images and are not currently included on the outro slide. 

Updated over a week ago 

Table of contents 

roomvu allows you to add a personalized intro and outro to your video content, giving every video a professional and branded finish. These are separate from your AI Portrait, which is a static image used on content like slideshows, video covers, and other branding materials. 

​ 

What are intro and outro slides? 

Outro slide: A closing slide that appears during the last 3 seconds of every video. It displays your contact information and branding, giving viewers a clear way to reach you after watching. 

​ 

Your AI Portrait is not currently included on the outro slide. The outro is a separate element with its own design and editable fields. 

​ 

What information appears on the outro slide? 

The outro slide pulls your basic profile information automatically, but you can also customize it with additional details. Here is what you can edit: 

Field 

Description 

Additional Phone Number / Titles 

Add a secondary phone number or additional professional titles 

Additional License Number / Credentials 

Add extra license numbers or professional credentials beyond your primary ones 

Website 

Your personal or business website URL 

Slogan 

A short tagline or personal motto that represents your brand 

How to set up or edit your outro slide 

Log in to your roomvu account and click the gear icon in the top right corner to open Settings. 

Navigate to the Video Intro & Outro section on the left menu. 

Fill in or update any of the fields you would like to appear on your outro. 

Click " Save Changes" when you are done. 

Your outro will automatically appear during the last 3 seconds of all your roomvu videos. 

​ 

A note on AI Portraits and outro slides 

We understand that many users would love to see their AI Portrait featured on their outro slide. While this is not currently available, we are always working on expanding our customization options. If this is something you would like to see added, we encourage you to share your feedback with our team.

## How to Add Your Social Media Links to Google My Business and Facebook | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/14471088-how-to-add-your-social-media-links-to-google-my-business-and-facebook

How to Add Your Social Media Links to Google My Business and Facebook | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English

English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections

How to Add Your Social Media Links to Google My Business and Facebook 

How to Add Your Social Media Links to Google My Business and Facebook 

Step by step guide on how to add social media profile links to Google My Business and Facebook. Helps you strengthen your online presence and make it easier for clients to connect across platforms. 

Updated over 3 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Adding your social media links to your Google My Business (GMB) profile and Facebook page makes it easier for potential clients to find and connect with you across all your platforms. It also strengthens your online presence and adds credibility to your profile. Here is how to do it on each platform. 

Adding Social Media Links to Google My Business 

Go to business.google.com and log in to your Google account. 

Select the business profile you want to edit. 

Click Edit Profile . 

Scroll down to find the Social Profiles section. 

Click the Add or Edit button next to the social platform you want to add. 

Select the platform from the dropdown list, for example Facebook, Instagram, LinkedIn, or X (Twitter). 

Paste your social media profile URL into the field provided. 

Click Save . 

Repeat this process for each social media platform you want to link. Your social media links will appear on your Google Business Profile and can be visible to anyone who finds you on Google Search or Google Maps. 

​ 

Adding Social Media Links to Your Facebook Page 

Go to your Facebook Page and make sure you are logged in as the page administrator. 

Click Edit Profile on your page. 

Scroll down to the More Info or Contact Info section. 

Look for the Social Media field. 

Select the social media platforms from the drop-down menu and add your username. 

Click Save Changes . 

Alternatively, you can add links directly to your Facebook Page bio or About section to make them more visible to visitors. 

​ 

Tips for getting the most out of your social media links 

Make sure all your profile URLs are correct and up to date before adding them. A broken link leaves a poor first impression. 

Use your roomvu VuCard link as one of your listed links. It serves as a central hub for your contact information and branding and works well as a landing page for anyone discovering you for the first time. 

Keep your social media profiles consistent across all platforms. Use the same profile photo, name, and branding so clients recognize you no matter where they find you. 

Check your links periodically to make sure they are still active, especially if you have changed your username or profile URL on any platform.

## How to Create a Lead-Capturing Landing Page with roomvu AI Page Builder | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/14484816-how-to-create-a-lead-capturing-landing-page-with-roomvu-ai-page-builder

How to Create a Lead-Capturing Landing Page with roomvu AI Page Builder | Roomvu Help Center

How to Create a Lead-Capturing Landing Page with roomvu AI Page Builder 

How to Create a Lead-Capturing Landing Page with roomvu AI Page Builder 

Updated over a week ago 

Table of contents 

Getting a professional landing page used to require hiring a designer, waiting days for revisions, and spending money you did not have to. With roomvu's AI Page Builder, you can launch a fully personalized, lead-capturing landing page in minutes, no design experience required. 

​ 

What is AI Page Builder? 

AI Page Builder is a roomvu tool that uses artificial intelligence to create professional landing pages tailored to your business goals, style, and branding. Whether you want to attract buyers, showcase listings, establish yourself as a market expert, or position yourself in the luxury space, the AI Page Builder creates a complete page built around your specific goal and audience. 

​ 

Why does this matter for your business? 

Your social media posts and videos do a great job of building awareness, but when a potential client wants to take the next step, they need somewhere to land. A well-designed landing page gives them that destination. It tells your story, showcases your expertise, and most importantly, captures their contact information so you can follow up. 

​ 

Without a dedicated landing page, potential leads often lose interest or move on before reaching out. With AI Page Builder, every campaign, listing, or piece of content you share can point to a page that is designed from the ground up to convert visitors into leads. It works around the clock, capturing inquiries even when you are with clients or away from your phone. 

​ 

For real estate agents, mortgage brokers, insurance agents, and financial advisors, a strong landing page is one of the highest-return marketing assets you can have. AI Page Builder makes creating one as simple as answering a few questions. 

​ 

How to access AI Page Builder 

Log in to your roomvu dashboard, scroll down to the More Tools section, and click AI Page Builder . 

Step 1: Choose your main goal 

The AI builds your entire page around the goal you select. Choose the one that best matches what you want to achieve: 

Goal 

Best For 

🏠 Get buyer leads 

Attracting buyers actively searching in your market 

🏷️ Move my listings 

Showcasing properties and driving seller inquiries 

📊 Be the market expert 

Establishing authority with stats, trends, and insights 

🤝 Build my brand 

Telling your story, specialties, and why clients choose you 

🔑 First-time buyers 

Guiding new buyers through the process and capturing leads 

💎 Luxury market 

Premium positioning for high-end properties and clients 

Step 2: Choose your style 

This sets the overall look and feel of your page. Pick the one that best reflects your personality and the clients you want to attract: 

Style 

Description 

🌊 Cool & Professional 

Clean, corporate, and trustworthy. Perfect for luxury and established agents 

☀️ Warm & Approachable 

Friendly, inviting, and human. Great for relationship-focused agents 

🖤 Bold & Luxury 

Dramatic, premium, and exclusive. Ideal for luxury market positioning 

🌿 Fresh & Modern 

Contemporary, clean, and optimistic. Appeals to modern buyers and sellers 

🎨 Use my own brand colors 

Build the page using your personal brand colors 

Step 3: Add the finishing touches 

These final options make your page feel personal and relevant to your audience: 

Include my photo: Uses your roomvu profile photo in the hero section of the page, putting a face to your name right away. 

Show my specialties: Displays your areas of expertise as credential badges, for example First Time Home Buying, Negotiation, or Condos. 

Add content topics: Creates dedicated sections on your page pulled from your roomvu content tags, such as Market Trends Reports, Forecast Videos, or Home Buyer Tips. 

Anything specific you want on this page: Add any custom requests or additional details you want the AI to incorporate. 

Once you are happy with your selections, click Build My Page and wait a few minutes for the AI to generate your page. 

​ 

After your page is created 

Once your page is ready you can review it and request changes if anything needs to be adjusted. When you are satisfied with the result you have two options: 

Save the page directly within roomvu to use as a live landing page. You will get a live link after saving. 

Copy the HTML code to host the page on your own website or platform. 

How to get the most out of your landing page 

Share the link to your landing page in your social media bio, email signature, and VuCard. 

Use it as the destination URL when running roomvu Smart Ads to maximize lead capture from your paid campaigns. 

Point your video content and social media posts to your landing page to give engaged viewers a clear next step. 

Update your page periodically to reflect your current goals, listings, or market focus.

## Why Didn't My Updated Profile Photo, Logo, or Contact Info Appear on My Content? | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/14679589-why-didn-t-my-updated-profile-photo-logo-or-contact-info-appear-on-my-content

Why Didn't My Updated Profile Photo, Logo, or Contact Info Appear on My Content? | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Tutorials 

Why Didn't My Updated Profile Photo, Logo, or Contact Info Appear on My Content? 

Why Didn't My Updated Profile Photo, Logo, or Contact Info Appear on My Content? 

Explains why profile photo, logo, or contact info updates may not appear on roomvu content. Platinum and Diamond users must submit a design update request. Basic, Pro, and Omni-Presence users are updated automatically. 

Updated over a week ago 

Table of contents 

If you have recently updated your profile photo, brokerage logo, phone number, or any other profile information on roomvu but your social media content is still showing the old details, the reason depends on which type of branding your account uses. 

​ 

Find out which branding type you have 

Your branding type is determined by your roomvu plan: 

Platinum or Diamond plan: You are using Platinum Design 

Basic, Pro, or Omni-Presence plan: You are using Premium Branding 

If you are on the Platinum or Diamond plan (Platinum Design) 

Platinum Design themes are custom-built by roomvu's in-house design team. Because of this, profile changes you make on roomvu, such as a new photo, updated logo, or new phone number, do not automatically carry over to your content. Your social media posts will continue using the previous version of your design until you submit an update request to our design team. 

​ 

To apply your changes to your content: 

Go to your roomvu dashboard and click Brand Theme in the left menu. 

Click Update Design . 

You will be taken to extra.roomvu.com/platinum-designs where you can submit your update request. 

Our design team will process your request and apply the updated information to your content. 

Update My Platinum Design 

For a full walkthrough of the request process, visit this guide. 

​ 

If you are on the Basic, Pro, or Omni-Presence plan (Premium Branding) 

Premium Branding templates pull your information directly from your roomvu profile. If your content is not reflecting your updated details, try the following: 

Make sure your changes have been saved correctly on your profile. 

Allow a short period of time for the update to propagate across your content. 

Refresh your dashboard and check your content again. 

If the information is still not updated after following these steps, book a support session and our team will look into it for you. 

Summary 

Plan 

Branding Type 

Do profile updates apply automatically? 

Platinum, Diamond 

Platinum Design 

No, submit an update request via Brand Theme 

Basic, Pro, Omni-Presence 

Premium Branding 

Yes, updates apply automatically

## How to Block Specific News Sources from Your Content Calendar | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/14690499-how-to-block-specific-news-sources-from-your-content-calendar

How to Block Specific News Sources from Your Content Calendar | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Video Guides 

How to Block Specific News Sources from Your Content Calendar 

How to Block Specific News Sources from Your Content Calendar 

Learn how to block specific news sources from appearing in your roomvu content calendar. Found in Content Calendar settings under the Advanced tab, the Customize News Source feature lets you exclude any website from your scheduled content. 

Updated over a week ago 

Table of contents 

roomvu curates and schedules content from a wide range of trusted sources to keep your feed active with valuable, relevant articles for your audience. Occasionally, you may come across a piece of content that references or promotes another company, brokerage, or brand that you would prefer not to be associated with. This is completely understandable, and roomvu gives you full control to block specific sources from ever appearing in your content. 

​ 

Why does this happen? 

roomvu selects content based on its value and relevance to your audience, not on which company produced it. An article may contain genuinely useful information for your clients while also being published by or mentioning another business in your industry. This does not mean roomvu endorses that source or that it appears as a competitor recommendation, but we understand that some agents and brokers prefer to avoid this entirely. 

​ 

How to block a news source 

From your roomvu dashboard, click Content Calendar in the left menu. 

Click Settings . 

Go to the Advanced tab. 

Find the Customize News Source section. 

Click Edit . 

Add the URL of the source you would like to block. 

Save your changes. 

Once a source is blocked, content from that website will no longer be scheduled or shared on your behalf. 

​ 

Can I block multiple sources? 

Yes. You can add as many sources as you like to your blocked list. Simply repeat the steps above and add each URL you want to exclude. 

​ 

What if I find a source I want to block in already-scheduled content? 

If you notice content from an unwanted source that is already scheduled in your calendar, you can manually remove it from your upcoming posts and then block the source to prevent it from appearing again in the future. If you need help with this, book a support session and our team will assist you.

## My AI Voice Clone Is Mispronouncing a Word. What Can I Do? | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/14705603-my-ai-voice-clone-is-mispronouncing-a-word-what-can-i-do

My AI Voice Clone Is Mispronouncing a Word. What Can I Do? | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Tutorials 

My AI Voice Clone Is Mispronouncing a Word. What Can I Do? 

My AI Voice Clone Is Mispronouncing a Word. What Can I Do? 

Learn what to do if your roomvu AI voice clone mispronounces a word. Submit a custom pronunciation request by emailing info@roomvu.com with the word and its correct pronunciation written in plain English. 

Updated over a week ago 

Table of contents 

AI voice cloning technology is remarkably accurate, but there are cases where certain words, especially place names, uncommon spellings, or abbreviated terms, can be mispronounced. This is a known limitation of text-to-speech engines, which rely on patterns to determine how words should sound and can occasionally get it wrong. 

If your AI voice clone is mispronouncing a word in your videos, we can fix it for you by submitting a custom pronunciation request to our team. 

​ 

Common examples of words that may need a custom pronunciation 

City or place names: Names like "Port St. Lucie" can be tricky. Our system may read "St" as "street" instead of "saint." Regional place names with unique local pronunciations are especially prone to this. 

Abbreviated words: Abbreviations like "St", "Dr", "Ave", or "Blvd" may be read literally rather than as their full intended words. 

Uncommon first or last names: Names that do not follow standard English pronunciation rules may be read incorrectly. 

Brokerage or company names: Unique business names or brand names that do not follow standard pronunciation patterns. 

Local neighbourhood or area names: Names with French, Spanish, Indigenous, or other non-English origins that have locally accepted pronunciations. 

How to submit a custom pronunciation request 

Since our AI voice engine does not use a standardized form or phonetic notation system, the easiest way to tell us the correct pronunciation is simply using plain English letters to describe how the word should sound. 

Send an email to info@roomvu.com with the following information: 

The word that is being mispronounced as it appears in your content. 

The correct pronunciation written out using plain English letters so we understand exactly how it should sound. For example: "St should be pronounced saint, not street" or "Thibodaux should be pronounced tib-uh-doe." 

Our team will submit the correction to the pronunciation engine and follow up with you once it has been applied. 

​ 

Note: Because pronunciation corrections are handled manually and applied to the AI engine, there may be a short processing time before the fix takes effect in your videos. In some cases, closely related words or names may also need to be adjusted separately, as a correction to one variation does not always carry over to another. 

Related Articles 

How to Activate and Use Roomvu AI Voice Clone

## Who Is the Person in My Avatar Video? That Is Not Me! | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/14708125-who-is-the-person-in-my-avatar-video-that-is-not-me

Who Is the Person in My Avatar Video? That Is Not Me! | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Tutorials 

Who Is the Person in My Avatar Video? That Is Not Me! 

Who Is the Person in My Avatar Video? That Is Not Me! 

If a generic or wrong-gender avatar appears in your videos, it means a personal AI Avatar has not been created yet. Create your avatar using your AI Portrait or a selfie and enable it in settings. 

Updated over a week ago 

Table of contents 

If you have noticed an unfamiliar face appearing in your avatar videos, do not worry. You have not been assigned someone else's profile by mistake. What you are seeing is a generic placeholder avatar that our system uses when no personal avatar has been created for your account yet. 

​ 

Why does this happen? 

When you add a Talking Avatar to your content without first creating a personalized avatar, roomvu automatically fills in with a generic default avatar. This placeholder is not linked to your appearance, gender, or identity in any way, which is why some users, particularly men, may see a female avatar appearing in their videos, and vice versa. 

​ 

This is one of the most common avatar-related questions we receive, and the fix is straightforward: you simply need to create your own personal avatar. 

​ 

How to fix it 

To replace the generic avatar with one that actually looks like you, you need to create your personal AI Avatar. You can do this using your existing AI Portrait or by taking a selfie directly within the platform. 

​ 

Once your avatar is created, you will need to enable it by going to your account settings at roomvu.com/dashboard/settings?tab=ai-avatar. 

​ 

For a full step by step guide on how to create and add your AI Avatar to your videos, visit this article. 

​ 

How to Setup Your Avatar 

The difference between AI Portraits and AI Avatars 

AI Portrait: A static image of you used on slideshows, video covers, and other branded content. It does not move or speak. 

AI Avatar (Talking Avatar): An animated version of you, synchronized with your cloned voice, used in editable videos and immersive listing tours. 

Your Talking Avatar needs to be created separately before it can appear in your content. Until it is set up, the system will fall back to a generic placeholder.

Can't Find a Support Session Soon Enough? Try Our Daily Group Support Sessions 

Can't Find a Support Session Soon Enough? Try Our Daily Group Support Sessions 

roomvu's daily Group Support Sessions offer a faster alternative to one-on-one bookings. Join a Zoom session, pick a topic-based breakout room, and get help the same or next day. Great for support and learning. 

Updated over a week ago 

Table of contents 

If the earliest available one-on-one support session is days away and you need help sooner, we have a faster alternative that is available every single day. 

​ 

What is a Group Support Session? 

Group Support Sessions are daily live sessions hosted on Zoom where multiple users join at the same time and get their issues addressed by our support team. Unlike individual sessions, these are available much sooner, often as early as the next day. 

When you join, the session is divided into separate breakout rooms on Zoom, each focused on a specific topic. You simply choose the breakout room that matches your issue and join. Each room typically has between one and six users at a time. 

​ 

How does it work? 

Our support team works through each user's issue one by one within the breakout room. Because of the group nature of these sessions, please come prepared and be patient while others are being helped before you. 

​ 

The unexpected bonus: you will learn more than you came for 

One of the things our users love most about Group Support Sessions is that while you are waiting for your turn, you get to listen in as other users get their issues resolved. Most of the time these issues come down to features that users were not fully aware of, which means every session doubles as an educational experience. Many users leave having learned things about the platform they never knew existed, even if it had nothing to do with the reason they originally joined. 

​ 

How to book a Group Support Session 

From your roomvu dashboard, click Get (VIP) Help in the top right corner. 

Click Group Support Session . 

Pick a date and time. Sessions are typically available as early as the next day. 

That is it. No long wait, no days of downtime. Come with your question and our team will take care of you.

How to Add an Open House Banner to Your Listing Video or Image 

How to Add an Open House Banner to Your Listing Video or Image 

Learn how to add an Open House banner with date and time to your listing video or image in roomvu. Done through Listing Studio in MLS Listings, then shareable across social media in a few clicks. 

Updated yesterday 

Table of contents 

Promoting an open house is one of the most effective ways to drive attendance and generate interest in a listing. With roomvu, you can add a branded Open House banner complete with the date and time directly to your listing video or image, and then share it across your social media channels in just a few steps. 

How to add an Open House banner to your listing 

From your roomvu dashboard, click MLS Listings in the left menu. 

Find the listing you want to promote and click the Options Menu Button. 

Click " Open House " 

A popup window will appear asking you to enter the date and time of the open house. 

Enter the details and click Save . 

Your listing video or image will now display the Open House banner with the date and time you have set. You can apply this to both your listing video and listing image depending on what you want to share. 

Option 2: Listing Studio 

Find the listing you want to promote and click Listing Studio . 

Inside Listing Studio, click Template . 

In the Label section, click the dropdown menu and select Open House . 

A popup window will appear asking you to enter the date and time of the open house. 

Enter the details and click Save . 

Sharing your Open House listing 

Once your Open House banner is set up, you can promote your listing directly to your connected social media channels from within roomvu. This gives your open house maximum visibility with your audience with minimal effort. 

Tips for getting the most out of your Open House promotion 

Post your Open House listing video or image at least a few days before the event to give your audience enough time to plan ahead. 

Share it across multiple platforms to reach as many potential buyers as possible. 

Consider posting a reminder the day before or the morning of the open house to keep it top of mind.

## How Roomvu Posts on Your Behalf | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/8688792-how-roomvu-posts-on-your-behalf

How Roomvu Posts on Your Behalf | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard

English

All Collections 

Content Calendar 

How Roomvu Posts on Your Behalf 

How Roomvu Posts on Your Behalf 

Understanding How Roomvu Effectively Manages Social Media Posts for Real Estate Professionals 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

If you're a real estate agent or mortgage broker, you may have wondered how Roomvu consistently posts tailored, hyper-local content on your social media accounts. It's a question we hear often, and understandably so. Entrusting your social media strategy to an external service is a big step, and you'd naturally want to know how the gears turn behind the scenes. That's why we've created this guide to shed light on the precise process Roomvu follows to post content on your behalf, keeping your online presence as engaging and relevant as possible. 

Now, let's dive into the nitty-gritty of how it all works. 

​ 

The Mechanism: API and Authorization 

One of the most critical aspects to understand is how securely Roomvu interacts with your social media accounts. You might be concerned about linking your social platforms to an external service, but rest assured, this is an entirely safe process. 

​ 

How It's Secure 

Authorization : The initial step involves linking your social media accounts to Roomvu. During this stage, OAuth (Open Authorization) protocols come into play. These protocols permit Roomvu to interact with your social media accounts without revealing your login credentials. 

Access Tokens : Once you've granted permission, Roomvu receives what is known as an "access token" from the social media platform. This token is a secure key that lets Roomvu post on your behalf without accessing your account directly. 

API-Enabled : The connection is established through official APIs provided by the social media platforms. These APIs are designed with security in mind, ensuring a safe bridge between Roomvu and your social media accounts. 

Revocable Access : It's worth noting that these access tokens are entirely within your control. You can revoke these permissions at any time, giving you full authority over what happens to your account. 

Using OAuth protocols and access tokens means that Roomvu never has access to your social media credentials. Instead, we interact with your accounts via a secure pathway established by the APIs, ensuring the utmost safety and security. 

​ 

The Content: Personalized and Relevant 

One of the standout features of Roomvu is the personalization of content. Unlike generic social media posts, Roomvu crafts each video or post focusing on hyper-local and relevant topics. You can always review your content calendar to see the content specifically picked and scheduled for you and your audience. 

​ 

Approve or Delete 

When reviewing the content on your calendar, you have two options 

Approve : No action is needed if the content aligns with your marketing goals. The post will automatically go live at the scheduled time. 

Delete : You can cancel the post if you feel the content is unsuitable. Over time, our system learns from your preferences to better curate future content. 

Two Weeks in Advance 

Roomvu also offers the convenience of reviewing your scheduled content for the next two weeks. This foresight allows you to plan other aspects of your marketing campaign more efficiently. 

​ 

Conclusion 

In summary, Roomvu's approach offers a hassle-free, secure, and personalized way to manage social media accounts. By leveraging technology similar to platforms like Hootsuite and coupling it with highly specialized content, Roomvu helps real estate agents and mortgage brokers become market leaders in the digital age. 

​ 

By staying consistently visible on social media with high-quality, relevant posts, you reach potential clients and build a strong brand. With Roomvu by your side, rest assured your online presence is in good hands. 

​ 

For more tips on social media marketing for real estate agents and mortgage brokers, stay tuned to Roomvu Academy.

## How to Post on Facebook Groups for Real Estate | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/8733195-how-to-post-on-facebook-groups-for-real-estate

How to Post on Facebook Groups for Real Estate | Roomvu Help Center

All Collections 

Social media 

How to Post on Facebook Groups for Real Estate 

How to Post on Facebook Groups for Real Estate 

This guide covers strategies for creating, sharing, and optimizing posts to engage potential clients and establish your brand. 

December 21, 2023 

Table of contents 

Facebook groups are online communities where people with common interests can interact, share, and learn from each other. For real estate agents, Facebook groups can be a powerful tool to generate leads, build relationships, and showcase their expertise. In this article, we will explain why you should post on Facebook groups for real estate, what to post on Facebook groups for real estate, and how to post on Facebook groups for real estate. 

Share a post from your Facebook Page to a Facebook group 

To share a post from your Page to your group: 

Log into Facebook, then click your profile photo in the top right. 

Click See all profiles, then select the Page you want to switch to. 

Beneath the post you want to share, click Share and select Share to a group. 

Click the group you want to share with, add optional text, and click Post. 

Why Post on Facebook Groups for Real Estate? 

Posting on Facebook groups for real estate can help you: 

Reach a large and targeted audience 

According to Statista , Facebook had 2.89 billion monthly active users as of the second quarter of 2021, making it the world's most popular social media platform. Moreover, thousands of Facebook groups for real estate cover various topics, niches, and locations. You can join the groups relevant to your market and audience and reach potential clients interested in buying, selling, renting, or investing in real estate. 

Establish your authority and credibility 

By posting valuable and informative content on Facebook groups for real estate, you can demonstrate your industry knowledge, skills, and experience. You can also answer questions, provide feedback, advise other group members, and position yourself as a helpful and trustworthy expert. This can help you build your reputation and brand awareness and attract more referrals and recommendations. 

Engage and connect with your audience 

Posting on Facebook groups for real estate can also help you create and maintain relationships with your audience. You can use Facebook groups to communicate with your existing and potential clients and keep them updated on your listings, services, and market trends. You can also use Facebook groups to interact with other real estate professionals and learn from their best practices, insights, and experiences. 

What to Post on Facebook Groups for Real Estate? 

The type of content you post on Facebook groups for real estate depends on each group's purpose, theme, and rules. However, some general guidelines are: 

Post relevant and valuable content 

Your posts should be related to the topic and audience of the group and provide value to the group members. For example, you can post market reports, industry news, tips and tricks, case studies, testimonials, or educational videos. Avoid posting spammy, promotional, or irrelevant content that may annoy or offend the group members or admins. 

Post engaging and interactive content 

Your posts should also be designed to capture the attention and interest of the group members and encourage them to engage with you and your content. For example, you can post polls, surveys, quizzes, contests, giveaways, or live Q&A sessions. You can also use emojis, GIFs, images, or videos to make your posts more appealing and expressive. 

Post original and authentic content 

Your posts should reflect your personality, voice, and style and showcase your unique value proposition. For example, you can post stories, anecdotes, or behind-the-scenes content that reveal your personal and professional journey, challenges, and achievements. You can also post content highlighting your values, mission, and vision and how you differentiate yourself from your competitors. 

How to Post on Facebook Groups for Real Estate? 

To post on Facebook groups for real estate, you need to follow these steps: 

Find and join the right groups 

You can use the search function on Facebook to find groups related to your niche, location, or interest. You can also browse the categories, recommendations, or suggestions on the Facebook groups page. Before joining a group, read the group description, rules, and reviews, and check the group activity, size, and engagement level. You can also create your group to have more control and influence over your audience and content. 

Follow the group rules and etiquette 

Once you join a group, you must respect the group rules and etiquette and abide by the group norms and expectations. For example, you should introduce yourself to the group and explain who you are, what you do, and why you joined the group. You should also avoid posting too frequently, aggressively, or self-promotionally and refrain from spamming, trolling, or flaming the group. You should also acknowledge and respond to the comments, questions, and feedback you receive on your posts and thank the group members for their engagement and support. 

Optimize your posts for maximum reach and impact 

To ensure your posts get seen and appreciated by the group members, you need to optimize your posts for maximum reach and impact. For example, you should use catchy headlines, clear and concise language, and compelling calls to action to entice the group members to click, read, and act on your posts. Using relevant keywords, hashtags, and tags would make your posts more searchable and discoverable. You should also post at the optimal times and frequencies and monitor and measure the performance and results of your posts. 

Conclusion 

Posting on Facebook groups for real estate can be a great way to grow your business, brand, and network. Following the tips and strategies in this article, you can create and share content that will attract, engage, and convert your audience and establish yourself as a leading real estate agent. Happy posting!

## How to Integrate MoxiWorks with roomvu CRM: A Step-by-Step Guide | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/8733322-how-to-integrate-moxiworks-with-roomvu-crm-a-step-by-step-guide

How to Integrate MoxiWorks with roomvu CRM: A Step-by-Step Guide | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Integration 

How to Integrate MoxiWorks with roomvu CRM: A Step-by-Step Guide 

How to Integrate MoxiWorks with roomvu CRM: A Step-by-Step Guide 

Integrate MoxiWorks with roomvu CRM using your UUID for streamlined real estate lead management and enhanced business efficiency. 

December 21, 2023 

Table of contents 

In the ever-evolving real estate landscape, professionals always look for tools that simplify and optimize their workflow. With roomvu’s pioneering video marketing capabilities, agents can generate hyper-local and relevant leads through ads and landing pages. Meanwhile, MoxiWorks offers a robust CRM system that makes managing these leads a breeze. But what if you could combine these two powerhouse platforms? The good news is, you can. Integrating MoxiWorks with roomvu CRM is not only possible but also incredibly straightforward. All you need is your MoxiWorks UUID, and you're well on your way to a streamlined process for managing leads and customer relationships. Here's how to do it step-by-step. 

Step 1: Locate Your MoxiWorks UUID 

What is a UUID? 

A UUID (Universally Unique Identifier) is a unique string of characters that identifies your profile within the MoxiWorks platform. 

Finding Your UUID 

Log into your MoxiWorks account : Use your credentials to log into your MoxiWorks profile. 

Navigate to Your Profile Page : Once logged in, go to your profile page on MoxiWorks. 

Find the UUID in the URL : Your UUID can be found as part of the URL on your profile page. Copy what comes after "profile/" and before "/show" 

Alternatively, you can ask your brokerage manager to provide your UUID. 

Step 2: Log Into Your roomvu Account 

Go to roomvu’s Login Page : Open your browser and go to roomvu’s login page. 

Enter Credentials : Use your roomvu username and password to log in. 

Step 3: Access "Leads Management" 

Once you are logged in to your roomvu account: 

Navigate to the Left Side Menu : Look for the menu options on the left side of the dashboard. 

Click on 'Leads Management' : Find and click on this option to move to the next step. 

Step 4: Initiate MoxiWorks Integration 

Click on 'Get Leads on Your CRM' : Once inside the ‘Leads Management’ section, locate and click on the 'Get Leads on Your CRM' button. 

Select MoxiWorks : A pop-up window will appear. From the available options, choose ‘MoxiWorks’. 

Step 5: Enter Your MoxiWorks UUID 

After you have selected MoxiWorks from the pop-up: 

Locate the UUID Field : You will see a field to enter your UUID. 

Paste Your UUID : Paste the UUID you had copied from your MoxiWorks URL into this field. 

Confirm : After pasting, confirm the information to complete the integration process. 

And there you have it! You’ve successfully integrated your MoxiWorks account with roomvu CRM. You can now enjoy the enhanced capabilities of these two powerful platforms, giving you a superior edge in managing your real estate business effectively.

## roomvu Leads Journey Builder: Tutorial | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/8733332-roomvu-leads-journey-builder-tutorial

roomvu Leads Journey Builder: Tutorial | Roomvu Help Center

Lead Management 

roomvu Leads Journey Builder: Tutorial 

roomvu Leads Journey Builder: Tutorial 

Use roomvu Leads Journey Builder for tailored lead nurturing with customized follow-ups and personalized interactions. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

In the digital age, the art of lead nurturing has been transformed. With roomvu Leads Journey Builder, crafting unique journeys for your leads based on your desired follow-up steps is now easier than ever. This tutorial aims to guide you through the intricacies of this innovative tool, ensuring your leads never feel neglected. 

Get Started with Default Journeys 

roomvu has thoughtfully prepared default journeys for your convenience. These can serve as a starting point. You can just modify these pre-made journeys or craft a new one tailored to your needs if you prefer a fresh start. 

​ 

To get started, Click " Leads Management " on the main page of your dashboard from the left sidebar. Then click " Journey Builder " from the new page. 

Crafting a New Journey 

Here, you can create your unique journeys. If unsure, you can always use ready journeys created by roomvu for different purposes. However, if you wish to build your unique journey: 

Click on the “ Add Journey ” option. 

Give your journey a unique name, then click next. 

Pick the " Lead's Source " for this journey. Then click " Save ." 

If you pick " General ," you can narrow the source even further. 

Designing Your Follow-Up Steps 

By default, A series of actions will be automatically used for your journey. 

You can add steps from the bottom in SMS or Email for each journey. 

You can also delete journeys to create new ones or edit the existing default steps. 

After adding a new phase, you can change different entries like the time, form, etc. 

Specify the time, which determines the duration since the lead filled out the form. 

Choose your desired action for the period you set above. 

You can opt for roomvu's pre-designed templates or tweak them to reflect your personal touch. This flexibility ensures your follow-up resonates with the lead, enhancing the chances of conversion. Preview the email content as you make changes. 

Tailoring Your Messages 

roomvu adds a dash of personalization by selecting videos relevant to the lead’s information. These videos are then shared in your follow-up emails, giving a unique edge to your messages. 

To further boost this personal touch: 

Use parameters in your messages to include details like the lead’s “first name” or “full name,” the “video name,” your specific “location, etc.” 

You can add more steps to build your own customized Journey. You can test the action for each step by sending yourself a test email/SMS. 

Notifications and Tracking 

Stay in the loop! 

Whenever a lead responds to your follow-ups, you'll be promptly notified. 

Want a holistic view? Navigate to the leads page to access comprehensive information about the leads and all the follow-up details. 

roomvu Leads Journey Builder: Conclusion 

roomvu's Leads Journey Builder isn’t just a tool; it’s a revolution in lead management. As you embrace this functionality, you automate a crucial aspect of your business and ensure that every lead is treated as valued, nudging them closer to a fruitful collaboration. So, dive in and embark on this journey of effective lead nurturing. 

roomvustore.com
