Roomvu Agent Websites: Elevating Your Online Presence 

Enhance your real estate presence with roomvu Agent Websites: Personal branding, dynamic content, and Platinum Package benefits. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

In the current dynamic digital era, a powerful online presence isn't just beneficial—it's crucial. This sentiment is particularly resonant for trust-driven fields like real estate and mortgage brokering. Despite hefty investments in sophisticated websites, many professionals find them underperforming. With clients and potential homebuyers leaning toward major platforms or referrals, roomvu Agent Websites emerges as a solution. Why pour funds into a high-cost site when roomvu provides an affordable, tailored platform with equivalent or superior benefits? 

How to Set Up and Customize Your Roomvu Website 

This guide walks you through setting up your personal domain, selecting a website template, updating your profile information, and configuring landing pages. 

​ 

To access the settings on your Dashboard Click the Gear icon on the top right corner to enter settings. 

​ 

​ 

Now on the right side menu scroll down to find " Website " 

​ 

​ 

1. Setup Your Personal Domain 

This section allows you to connect your own domain to your roomvu profile. 

1. Enter Your Domain 

• Type your preferred domain (e.g., www.yourname.com ) in the provided field. 

2. Check Your Current Profile Page 

• The link below shows your default Roomvu profile page (e.g., https://www.roomvu.com/agent/real-estate-trends ). 

• You can use this link as your temporary profile page before your custom domain is connected. 

2. DNS Server Setting 

To connect your domain, you need to update your DNS settings with your domain provider. 

1. Update IP Address 

• Change your domain’s A record to 138.197.154.187. 

• Click Copy IP to easily copy it. 

2. Need Help? 

• Click “How to update IPs?” for step-by-step instructions. 

• Book a session with roomvu’s support team if you need assistance. 

3. Website Template 

This section allows you to choose a layout for your website. 

1. Select one of the available templates: 

• Template 1 – A structured design with content sections. 

• Template 2 – A visually focused layout with a large image area. 

• Template 3 – A simple, clean design. 

2. Preview the templates 

• Click Sample Preview under each template to see how your site will look. 

3. Select the template you prefer and save your changes. 

4. Your Information 

This section lets you personalize your website with branding and business details. 

1. Slogan 

• Enter a tagline that represents your real estate services (e.g., “Real Estate Marketing Upgraded” ). 

2. Website Link 

• This field shows your Roomvu website URL. 

3. Landing Cover Image 

• Click “Change your cover image” to upload a new banner image. 

• Recommended dimensions: 1920 x 540 pixels. 

4. About You Section 

• Enter a short description about yourself and your real estate business. 

• Example: “All that is happening in the world of Real Estate.” 

5. All Agent Profile Settings 

• Click this link to adjust additional profile settings like contact details and social media links. 

5. Landing Pages 

Landing pages help capture leads by providing useful real estate insights. 

• Ask Me Anything! – Allow potential clients to ask real estate-related questions. 

• Want to know which homes you could buy with your current rent? – Helps renters explore homeownership options. 

• Find out if it’s time to sell your home. (Selected in screenshot) – Assists homeowners in evaluating if selling is a good option. 

• Best Homes Under $1M – Highlights homes priced under $1 million. 

​ 

​ 

6. Other Sections 

Enhance your website by adding useful property-related tools. 

• Quick Property Search – Allows visitors to search for available properties. 

• Agent Listings – Displays your personal listings. 

• Brokerage Listings – Showcases listings from your brokerage. 

7. Footer & Legal Information 

The footer section includes important disclaimers and compliance details. 

• MLS® & REALTOR® Trademarks 

States that the MLS® and REALTOR® trademarks are owned by CREA and used by authorized real estate professionals. 

• Disclaimer 

Clarifies that the information on the website is for general use and that accuracy is not guaranteed. 

• Equal Housing Opportunity Logo 

Ensures compliance with fair housing laws (checked in the screenshot). 

8. Saving and Publishing Your Website 

Once you’ve made all your changes: 

1. Review your settings. 

2. Click “Save Changes” to apply updates. 

3. Test your website link to ensure everything looks good. 

4. Share your personalized website with potential clients. 

Your roomvu website is now fully set up and ready to generate leads! 🚀

## How to Create a LinkedIn Account for Real Estate | Roomvu Help Center

How to Create a LinkedIn Account for Real Estate 

How to Create a LinkedIn Account for Real Estate 

Building a Professional Network: A Step-by-Step Guide for Real Estate Agents to Thrive on LinkedIn 

January 3, 2024 

Table of contents 

LinkedIn, often regarded as the premier platform for professionals, offers a tremendous opportunity for real estate professionals. Whether you’re a seasoned realtor, a property developer, or just starting, establishing a LinkedIn presence can boost your credibility, expand your network, and enhance business opportunities. Here’s a step-by-step guide on how to create a LinkedIn account tailored for real estate: 

Step 1: Sign Up for LinkedIn 

Visit the LinkedIn homepage at www.linkedin.com . 

Click on the ‘Join now’ button. 

Enter your email address, create a password, and click ‘Agree & Join .’ 

Now, enter your name and last name. 

Now, enter your location info, including your country, postal code, etc. 

Next, enter info about your most recent job and employment. 

A code will be sent to your email address. Enter it to validate your email address. 

Answer the following questions about your job preferences. 

Next, you will be shown a few people to connect to. Connect or skip. 

Profile Picture: Use a high-quality, professional photo. A headshot is ideal. 

Now you can connect to more companies, people, etc. When done click on Finish. 

Congratulations! You have now created your account. 

Step 2: Optimize Your Profile 

Now click on your name to open your profile. 

Click on the camera icon to edit your cover photo. 

Here are some tips: 

High-Quality Image : Ensure the image is of high resolution and doesn’t appear pixelated or stretched. LinkedIn recommends an image size of 1584 x 396 pixels. 

Stay Relevant : Use an image that’s relevant to the real estate industry. This could be a skyline of your primary city of operation, a stunning property you’ve listed/sold, or even a happy family outside their new home. 

Branding : Incorporate elements of your brand into the cover photo. If you have a personal or company logo, consider integrating it subtly without overwhelming the image. 

Avoid Clutter : While you might be tempted to showcase various properties, avoid making the cover photo too busy. A simple, clear image is more effective. 

Update Regularly : If you’ve recently sold a high-profile property or have a new branding campaign, update your cover photo to keep things fresh and relevant. 

Add a Call-to-Action (CTA) : While LinkedIn doesn’t allow clickable links on the cover photo, you can add a short CTA like “Contact me for your dream home!” or “Exploring the market? Let’s chat.” 

Consistency : Ensure the color scheme and style align with your brand, profile picture, and overall LinkedIn profile. Consistency helps in brand recall and portrays professionalism. 

Mobile Optimization : A significant number of users access LinkedIn via mobile. Make sure the essential elements of your cover photo are visible on mobile devices. Test how it looks across various devices. 

Local Landmarks : If you specialize in properties in a specific area, consider incorporating recognizable landmarks from that location. This establishes you as a local expert. 

Testimonials or Achievements : If you’ve received significant accolades or have a particularly glowing client testimonial, you can consider incorporating a short quote. However, be sure it doesn’t clutter the image. 

Engage a Designer : If you’re not confident in your design skills, consider hiring a graphic designer to craft a cover photo that aligns with your brand and professional image. 

Then click on the edit icon to optimize your profile 

Headline: Clearly define your role, e.g., “Realtor at XYZ Realty” or “Property Developer & Investor.” 

Summary: Briefly describe your expertise, achievements, and services in real estate. Mention any specialties or areas of focus. 

Step 3: Position and Education 

Click on the ‘Add Position’ button. 

Fill out details of your past and present roles related to real estate. This includes the company name, your role, tenure, and a brief description of responsibilities or achievements. 

Similarly, under ‘Education,’ add institutions you attended, courses undertaken, and any certifications received. 

Step 4: Customize Your Public Profile URL 

Go to ‘Edit public profile & URL’ on the right side of your profile page. 

on ‘Edit your custom URL.’ 

Opt for a professional URL that preferably includes your name and reference to real estate, e.g., “john-doe-realtor.” 

Read More: How to Convert Your LinkedIn Audience to Leads: A REALTORS® Definitive Guide to Getting Real Estate Leads on LinkedIn 

Step 5: Seek Recommendations and Endorsements 

Reach out to past clients, colleagues, or employers and request them to write a recommendation for your services on LinkedIn. 

List skills relevant to real estate, such as “Property Management” or “Real Estate Marketing.” Colleagues can then endorse you for these skills. 

Step 6: Create or Join Real Estate Groups 

You can use the search bar on LinkedIn to find natural estate-focused groups. 

Join groups that align with your niche or interest. 

Consider creating your own group if you have a unique real estate focus or wish to establish a community. 

Step 7: Establish a Company Page (If Applicable) 

Hover over the ‘Work’ icon on your LinkedIn homepage. 

Click on ‘Create a Company Page.’ 

Fill out details about your real estate company, including logo, description, and location. 

Step 8: Engage & Network 

Share industry insights, property listings, and success stories regularly. 

Engage with posts from your network by liking, sharing, or commenting. 

Connect with industry professionals, potential clients, and other stakeholders in the real estate sector. 

Step 9: LinkedIn Premium (Optional) 

Consider upgrading to LinkedIn Premium, especially if you’re keen on using advanced networking features, viewing more detailed insights, and accessing specialized courses on LinkedIn Learning. 

Final Thoughts 

With its professional ethos, LinkedIn serves as a valuable platform for real estate professionals. By establishing a solid profile, actively engaging, and leveraging its networking opportunities, you can elevate your brand and foster meaningful business relationships.

Engaging the Next Generation: A Guide for Real Estate Professionals on Establishing a Dynamic TikTok Presence

Table of contents 

The power of social media in today's digital age cannot be underestimated. Platforms like TikTok have emerged as influential tools for businesses, including the real estate sector. TikTok's short, engaging video format can be a game-changer for realtors looking to showcase properties and engage potential clients. Here's a step-by-step guide on how to create a TikTok account for real estate. 

Step 1: Download and Install the App 

Go to the App Store (iOS) 

or Google Play Store (Android). 

Download and install the app on your smartphone. 

Step 2: Sign Up 

Open the TikTok app. 

Tap on the 'Profile' icon, usually at the bottom right. 

Choose 'Sign Up.' 

Sign up using your phone number, email, or another social media account. For a business, using an email associated with the business is recommended. 

Read More: How to Use TikTok for Real Estate Marketing and Connect with Millennials 

https://www.roomvu.com/academy/how-to-use-tiktok-for-real-estate-marketing-and-connect-with-millennials/

Instagram & YouTube Integration: Link other social media profiles to drive platform traffic.

https://www.roomvu.com/academy/how-to-use-tiktok-to-generate-leads-for-real-estate-and-go-viral/ 

Step 4: Switch to a Pro Account 

In your profile, tap the three lines (or settings). 

Choose "Settings and Privacy.' 

Tap on Account 

Tap 'Switch to Business Account.' 

Choose the category 'Business' and further classify it as 'Real Estate.' 

Note: Pro Accounts provide insights about your followers and the performance of your posts.

How to Create a Facebook Business Page for Real Estate

Table of contents 

For real estate professionals seeking a digital edge, understanding how to create a Facebook business page for real estate is essential. With its expansive user base, Facebook is an invaluable platform for agents and agencies to amplify their reach, engage with potential clients, and showcase their properties. This article will guide you through creating a Facebook business page tailored to real estate. 

Start with Your Personal Facebook Account 

While your Business Page will be separate from your personal profile , you'll need a personal account to act as the admin. 

Select Your Page Type 

On the left side menu, find "pages" and click on it. 

Click on "Create a New Page." 

Enter Page Details 

For the name, use your business's name or your own if you're branding as a personal realtor. Type in 'Real Estate' for the category and select the most appropriate option. Fill in the bio describing your business, the area you cover, and any other services that separate you from the competition.

Connect Your WhatsApp 

Once you connect your WhatsApp account, you can add buttons for your Page audience to message you on WhatsApp. 

Read More: Adding Facebook Friends to Business Page: A Quick Guide

Set Up Automated Messaging 

Automated responses can be set up under the 'Inbox' section, ensuring you get all the client inquiries. You can use settings in your inbox and chat plugins to set up automated messages. 

Link with Instagram 

If you also operate a real estate-focused Instagram business account, link it for streamlined content sharing. 

How to Create a Facebook Business Page for Real Estate

Integrating Constant Contact CRM into roomvu: A Step-By-Step Guide 

Integrating Constant Contact CRM into roomvu: A Step-By-Step Guide 

A Comprehensive Guide to Using Constant Contact CRM on roomvu 

Updated over a week ago 

Table of contents 

As a real estate professional, it's essential to maintain strong relationships with your clients and prospects. With the power of Constant Contact CRM integrated into roomvu, you can effortlessly manage your contacts, craft personalized email campaigns, and track their performance to drive growth and foster lasting relationships. In this guide, we'll walk you through each step of using Constant Contact CRM on roomvu with detailed explanations and accompanying screenshots. Our tutorial will help you unlock the full potential of this powerful platform. 

What is Constant Contact 

Constant Contact is a customer relationship management (CRM) platform primarily focused on email marketing, although it has expanded to offer additional marketing tools and features over the years. It allows businesses to build and manage their email lists, create and send targeted email campaigns, track campaign performance, and automate email marketing tasks. The platform is designed to help small businesses, nonprofits, and individuals engage with their audience, maintain relationships, and drive growth. 

While Constant Contact is not a full-fledged CRM solution like Salesforce or HubSpot, it does include some basic CRM functionalities, such as contact management and segmentation. Users can import, store, and manage their contacts and segment them based on various criteria like engagement, demographic information, or custom tags. This enables more targeted and personalized email campaigns that can help improve overall marketing effectiveness. 

Video Guide 

We've got you covered for those who prefer a more visual learning experience. Alongside this written tutorial, we have also created a comprehensive video tutorial covering all the real-time steps. You can choose to follow along with either format or use them to maximize your learning experience. 

How to Integrate Constant Contact CRM into roomvu 

Here are the steps you need to take to connect Constant Contact to roomvu: 

Log in to your roomvu account. On the left side menu, find " Leads & Follow Up " and click on it. 

Now click on "Get Leads on Your CRM." 

Select "Constant Contact" from the list. 

A pop-up window will open, where you need to log in to your "Constant Contact" account. Enter your credentials and click on "Sign in". 

Alternatively, you can use "Google" to sign to Constant Contact, if you do not have an account already. 

Once you sign in, the status on roomvu for Constant Contact" will change as below: 

We hope this comprehensive step-by-step guide has given you the knowledge and confidence to effectively harness Constant Contact's power on roomvu. By leveraging this robust platform, you can enhance your real estate marketing strategy, build lasting relationships with your clients, and ultimately grow your business. Remember that practice makes perfect, so don't hesitate to experiment with different features and techniques to find the perfect formula that works for you. With the right approach and consistent effort, you'll soon see the positive impact of Constant Contact on your real estate endeavors. Happy emailing!

## Integrating roomvu and Chime CRM with Zapier: A Step-By-Step Guide to Automation | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/8769660-integrating-roomvu-and-chime-crm-with-zapier-a-step-by-step-guide-to-automation

Integrating roomvu and Chime CRM with Zapier: A Step-By-Step Guide to Automation | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Integration 

Integrating roomvu and Chime CRM with Zapier: A Step-By-Step Guide to Automation 

Integrating roomvu and Chime CRM with Zapier: A Step-By-Step Guide to Automation 

Streamline Your Real Estate Leads Management by Seamlessly Connecting Roomvu and Chime CRM with Zapier 

January 3, 2024 

Table of contents 

This tutorial will guide you through integrating Roomvu with Chime CRM with Zapier, a popular automation platform that simplifies the connection between various applications. By integrating these two systems, you can streamline your marketing efforts, improve lead management, and increase efficiency in your real estate business. 

Requirements 

A Roomvu account ( https://www.roomvu.com ) 

A Chime CRM account ( https://chime.me ) 

A Zapier account ( https://zapier.com ) 

Integrating roomvu and Chime CRM with Zapier 

Step 1: Sign in to Zapier 

Go to https://zapier.com and sign in with your Zapier account. Sign up for a free trial if you don't have an account. 

Once you're signed in, go to the "Make a Zap" button at the top of the dashboard. 

Step 2: Set up the roomvu and Chime Trigger 

In the "Choose App & Event" section, search for "roomvu" in the search bar. 

Select the "roomvu" app from the search results. 

Now, on the right side of the "Choose App & Event" section, search for "Chime" in the search bar. 

Select the "Chime CRM" app from the search results. 

Now, for the roomvu (Left Side) choose a trigger event from the available options (e.g., "New Lead"). 

Now for the Chime Action (Right Side), choose an action event from the available options (e.g., "Create Lead" or "Update Lead"). 

Click on "Continue" to proceed. 

Step 3: Connect your roomvu account 

In the next step, click on "Exclamation Mark." 

Then click on "Sign in" to authorize Zapier to access your roomvu account. 

You will see this pop-up window: 

Leave it open go to your roomvu account and click "Settings." 

Click on the "Account and Security tab. 

Scroll down to find " Integration ," find " Zapier, " and then click on " Copy Your API Key. " 

Now, head back to the popup window on Zapier. Then, Paste the code you just copied in the first field (API Key). Then, enter the email address that you use on your Roomvu account. Finally click on "Yes, Continue to roomvu. 

The status on your Zap for roomvu will turn Green for roomvu. 

You can test the trigger in the test section by clicking on the "Exclamation Mark" 

When you are done, click on "Continue." 

Step 4: Connect your Chime CRM account 

Click on "Sign in to Chime CRM" and enter your Chime CRM credentials to authorize Zapier to access your account. 

This will open a popup window. 

You must grab your Chime API key to connect Chime to Zapier. This is the unique identifier for your Chime account and is a requirement when connecting Chime to Zapier. To find your API key, navigate to Settings > Integrations > API > Copy : 

Click "Continue" and then "Test Action" to ensure the connection works correctly. 

Once the test is successful, click "Continue." 

Step 5: Activate the Zap 

Please review your Zap's summary and ensure everything is set up correctly. 

Click "Turn on Zap" to activate it. 

Conclusion 

Congratulations! You've successfully integrated roomvu with Chime CRM using Zapier. Now, your leads from roomvu will be automatically synced with Chime CRM, allowing you to manage your leads more effectively and focus on closing deals.

## How To Connect to Your Facebook Personal Page on roomvu | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/8770067-how-to-connect-to-your-facebook-personal-page-on-roomvu

Skip to main content

Social media 

How To Connect to Your Facebook Personal Page on roomvu 

How To Connect to Your Facebook Personal Page on roomvu 

Learn how to connect your Facebook personal page to your roomvu account for content automation. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Facebook personal accounts may have a better reach and engagement performance than a Facebook Page. Facebook has reduced the organic reach on Business pages to encourage users to run ads. Therefore, a personal page on Facebook is a better choice for organic reach. Fortunately, roomvu offers social media automation on both Business and personal accounts. This article will explore how agents can connect to their accounts on their roomvu dashboard. 

How To Connect To Your Personal Facebook Account on roomvu 

Follow these steps to get it done quickly. 

On a computer, open your web browser ( Edge, Chrome ); 

If you are using a Mac , do not use Safari ; Mac's security may cause the connection to fail. 

Go to your Facebook Personal page. 

In the upper-right corner, click on your photo. 

Click on Settings and Privacy 

Then click settings : 

Now on the right menu scroll down to find " Audience and visibility" and then click "Posts" 

Then click " Who can see your future posts?" 

And then make sure it is set to "Public" 

​ 

​ 

Now click "Done" and from the left menu scroll up and then click on Accounts Center 

That will open your META account . 

Then click on your Facebook Account . 

And then on your USERNAME and copy it as you will need it later to login with. 

After you have your username, close the user info popup and the META panel by clicking the X in the upper right-hand corner. 

Log out of Facebook …Again in the upper-right corner, click on your photo and then on "Logout" 

Do not auto-log back in. 

Then type in your USERNAME and password and log in. 

Facebook may tell you your password needs to be corrected even if you know it is correct. This is Facebook making you update your password. If this happens, click the forgot password and go through the password reset process. 

Now, open a new tab go to roomvu.com, and log in. 

In the lower-left corner is “ connect more ." Click that. 

The connection engine will open. Click on Facebook Personal "Connect" 

Enter the same USERNAME and password to log in to Facebook, and the connection will start. 

A popup may open asking for a 6-digit key that will be texted to you. You can just enter it, and the connection will finish. 

What if I did not get the 6-digit code? 

The most likely cause is the user’s settings in the Meta Account Center . Meta has selected the authentication app as the default 2FA. Here is how to fix it. 

On a computer, open your web browser (Edge, Chrome). If you are using a Mac, do not use Safari; Mac's security may cause the connection to fail. 

Go to your Facebook page. 

In the upper-right corner, click on your photo. 

Click on Settings and Privacy 

Then click settings : 

Then click on Accounts Center 

That will open your META account . 

Then click on your Facebook Account . 

Select password and security , then choose two-factor authentication 

A new window will open, select Facebook, then TEXT MESSAGE(SMS) and follow the steps. 

Facebook may send the code immediately, or it can take up to an hour or more. you must not click the resend code more than once as this can trigger a lockout from Facebook.

## How to Integrate roomvu into Your WordPress Website | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/8770091-how-to-integrate-roomvu-into-your-wordpress-website

How to Integrate roomvu into Your WordPress Website | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard

English 

Your Dashboard

All Collections

How to Integrate roomvu into Your WordPress Website 

How to Integrate roomvu into Your WordPress Website 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

roomvu WordPress marketing plugin is a tool that allows roomvu agents to connect their content calendar in the “agent’s dashboard” to their own WordPress websites. In order to connect your calendar to your own WordPress website you need to do a few steps to get things ready. This article will explain the necessary steps needed to integrate roomvu into your WordPress website. To use roomvu's automation on your WordPress website, you need: 

An up-and-running WordPress website. 

An active premium or higher agent account in roomvu (to get your API key). 

Installing roomvu's marketing plugin. 

https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Kdn3CnuYvBM 

1. Copy your Wordpress API Key 

Click the "gear icon" on the top right corner to enter settings. Scroll down to find the " Integration " on the left menu. Here on the top section you can click the " Copy Your API Key" 

2. Install roomvu's WordPress plugin 

Open your WordPress dashboard. On the left sidebar, find "Plugins," then click " Add New". 

On the search field type in “ roomvu ” and then hit enter on your keyboard”. 

When you find the Roomvu marketing plugin, click on the “Install now” Button; it takes a while to install the plugin; when the installation is finished, the “Install now” button turns to “Activate.” Click the “ Activate ” Button to activate the plugin. 

When the plugin is activated, you can find a new menu inside the posts menu in the sidebar. (Posts » roomvu Marketing) 

Enter your “email” and “API Key” here then press the save button. The email must be the one you use to log in to your roomvu account. 

Your roomvu content calendar is now connected to your WordPress website and the content will be published on your website automatically. Please note that the content on your calendar on your roomvu account will be posted on your WordPress website.

How to Connect Your CRM and Other Tools to roomvu 

How to Connect Your CRM and Other Tools to roomvu 

Learn how to connect your CRM, email marketing platform, or partner tools to roomvu. Import your leads and nurture them with roomvu's marketing tools from one centralized platform. Supports a wide range of CRMs including Follow Up Boss, HubSpot, and more. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

roomvu integrates with a wide range of CRM platforms, email marketing tools, and partner services, allowing you to import your leads directly into roomvu and nurture them using our full suite of marketing tools. Instead of managing your contacts across multiple platforms, you can bring everything together in one place and let roomvu handle the marketing side automatically. 

​ 

Why integrate your CRM with roomvu? 

Your CRM is where your leads live. But having leads in a CRM does not mean they are being marketed to effectively. By connecting your CRM to roomvu, you can automatically import those leads and start nurturing them with personalized video content, email campaigns, and social media marketing, all branded to you. This keeps you top of mind with your contacts without any additional manual effort. 

​ 

How to find and connect your CRM 

Log in to your roomvu account and click the gear icon in the top right corner to open Settings. 

In the left menu, scroll down and click the Integration tab. 

In the middle of the page, find the CRM Integration section. 

Locate your CRM from the list and click Connect . 

Follow the instructions provided for your specific CRM. roomvu has added step by step connection instructions for many of the supported platforms, which you can access by clicking Connect next to your CRM.

## How to add your contacts on Instagram? | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/8770124-how-to-add-your-contacts-on-instagram

How to add your contacts on Instagram? 

How to add your contacts on Instagram? 

March 11, 2024 

Table of contents 

There are two ways to find people to follow on Instagram. You can connect your device’s contact list in the app and Instagram will recommend accounts to follow based on your contacts. This article will explore how you can find people you know on Instagram and add your contacts as "following". 

How to Add Your Contacts on Instagram 

Keep in mind that when you confirm your phone number or email on Instagram, your account may be recommended to users who have your contact information in their device’s contact list. Your phone number and email are stored on Instagram when you sign up for an account with this information or have added it to your Personal Information . This way, you can find your contacts who have added their phone number and email to their account. 

Note: Make sure you have added your contacts to your phonebook on your phone including email addresses. 

On the Instagram app for Android and iPhone, follow these steps: 

Tap 

or your profile picture in the bottom right to go to your profile. 

Tap 

in the top right, then tap 

Settings . 

Tap Account , 

Then tap Contacts Syncing . 

Tap the toggle next to Connect Contacts to turn on contact syncing. 

Now on your profile click on the + icon to discover people 

Then click "See all" to see all contacts. 

How to Find People on Instagram By Their Name 

You can also tap on 🔍 at the bottom of the screen to search for people you'd like to follow. 

Keep in mind that your contact list is periodically synced and your contacts will be re-uploaded the next time Instagram syncs your contacts. To stop this, go to your device settings and turn off contacts syncing on all devices logged into Instagram.

## How to Set up and Run An Automated Email Campaign on roomvu | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/8770140-how-to-set-up-and-run-an-automated-email-campaign-on-roomvu

How to Set up and Run An Automated Email Campaign on roomvu | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Email Marketing 

How to Set up and Run An Automated Email Campaign on roomvu 

How to Set up and Run An Automated Email Campaign on roomvu 

Learn how to upload your contacts on your roomvu dashboard and set up an email campaign and generate leads. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

One of the services roomvu provides Real Estate agents with is the automated email marketing system where agents can send emails to their audience. To do so they need to set up a campaign once and sit back. No need to do anything else. The email campaign will send the best content for your area to your audience on a certain day. This article will explain the steps you need to take once to make sure everything is working well. 

How to Set up and Run An Email Campaign on roomvu 

Here are the steps you need to take: 

Login and Find Email Campaigns Page 

First, log in to your account, and on the right sidebar, click on " Email Newsletters ". 

The first page will show if you are running any email campaigns at the moment or not. 

On the right side, you can see a preview of the emails that will be sent to your audience. 

On the left side you can adjust the time, contacts and the body of the email to be sent to your audience. 

Important: Do not change the text inside the brackets / remove the brackets. These are placeholders that will be used our system to automatically import and add your contacts info, etc. If you change these, your audience might receive words like Title, Name, etc on the email. 

Once done, you may click "Test Email" to send a copy of the email to yourself to see if everything is okay. If you do not receive the email, make sure you have checked your emails, junk, spam, etc. 

Finally click "Start Campaign" to run the campaign and send emails on the scheduled time/day. You can view the stats for the email campaign.

## What is the MLS, and how does Roomvu assist with MLS listings? | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/8770870-what-is-the-mls-and-how-does-roomvu-assist-with-mls-listings

What is the MLS, and how does Roomvu assist with MLS listings? | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Listings 

What is the MLS, and how does Roomvu assist with MLS listings? 

What is the MLS, and how does Roomvu assist with MLS listings? 

MLS (Multiple Listing Service) listing is a tool, representing a property that is available for sale and is listed on an MLS database. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

An MLS (Multiple Listing Service) listing is a crucial tool in real estate, representing a property that is available for sale and is listed on an MLS database. This database is a comprehensive collection of properties listed by various real estate agents and brokers in a specific area. It provides detailed information about each property, including its price, size, features, location, photographs, and the contact details of the seller’s agent. The purpose of an MLS listing is to facilitate buyers and sellers in finding and comparing properties that align with their needs and preferences. Additionally, it aids real estate agents and brokers in collaborating and sharing commission opportunities. 

At Roomvu, we offer services related to MLS listings , but it's important to note that these services are exclusively available to our subscribers on the Premium, Platinum, and Diamond plans. Our platform provides enhanced tools and features for these plan members to effectively utilize MLS listings for their real estate marketing and sales strategies.

## What is the duration of availability for IDX feeds on Roomvu? | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/8771043-what-is-the-duration-of-availability-for-idx-feeds-on-roomvu

What is the duration of availability for IDX feeds on Roomvu? | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Integration 

What is the duration of availability for IDX feeds on Roomvu? 

What is the duration of availability for IDX feeds on Roomvu? 

January 3, 2024 

IDX, or Internet Data Exchange, is a system that allows real estate professionals to display the most comprehensive and current property listings on their websites. At Roomvu, our IDX feed includes a wide array of listings, such as 'Just Listed' and 'Just Sold' properties. These listings, even after a sale, remain active and accessible in our feed for approximately 30 days. After this period, they are removed to maintain the timeliness and relevance of our database. This ensures that our clients always have access to the latest market data through our IDX integration.

What should I do if my MLS ID is not recognized in the Roomvu system? 

What should I do if my MLS ID is not recognized in the Roomvu system? 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

If you encounter a situation where your MLS ID is not recognized by our system, it's important to note that Roomvu's platform pulls in listings only when you are identified as the primary listing agent. If you are indeed the primary listing agent and still facing this issue, we encourage you to reach out to us directly. Please email us with your MLS ID, and our team will assist in manually populating your listing into our system. This process ensures that your listings are accurately and promptly reflected on our platform.

## What are the different ways I can utilize Listing videos through Roomvu? | Roomvu Help Center

What are the different ways I can utilize Listing videos through Roomvu? 

What are the different ways I can utilize Listing videos through Roomvu? 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Roomvu offers versatile options for utilizing listing videos, ensuring that you can maximize their impact across various platforms. Here are the three ways you can use them: 

Organic Social Media Posting: Utilize our system to post these videos organically on your social media (SM) platforms. This integrated feature simplifies the process of sharing your listings with your audience. 

Download and Share: You have the option to download these videos and share them through other social media channels, text messages, or email. This allows for personalized and targeted distribution of your listings. 

Paid Advertising: Use our system to create and run paid ads featuring your listing videos. This can significantly increase engagement and visibility for your listings, helping you to reach a broader audience and generate more interest in your properties. 

Each of these options is designed to provide flexibility and effectiveness in your real estate marketing strategies.

## How to connect Follow Up Boss + roomvu | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/8773916-how-to-connect-follow-up-boss-roomvu

How to connect Follow Up Boss + roomvu | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Integration 

How to connect Follow Up Boss + roomvu 

How to connect Follow Up Boss + roomvu 

January 4, 2024 

Table of contents 

In order to use your roomvu leads with Follow Up Boss you need to use another platform called Zapier. Zapier lets you send info between Follow Up Boss and roomvu automatically—no code required. This article will teach you how to use Zapier to send leads from roomvu to your Follow Up Boss account in simple steps, including images and screenshots to help you further. This platform makes Real Estate lead conversion and sales follow-up more efficient and automated. 

How to connect Follow Up Boss + roomvu 

The process is pretty simple. It can be portrayed in the diagram below: 

That means you have to use Zapier as the middle app between roomvu and Follow Up Boss. So first, you need to integrate Roomvu with Zapier as described in the article below. 

https://www.roomvu.com/academy/how-to-integrate-zapier-with-roomvu/ 

Then you need to create a Zap to connect roomvu to Follow Up Boss. You need to log in to your Zapier account to create a Zap. Select roomvu in the first field and choose a new lead. on the second drop-down menu select Follow Up Boss and pick one of the actions. 

In the action field you can choose various options already defined in Zapier. Pick one, and you are already done. If needed, you can create more Zaps as well. 

Now you have to log in to your Follow-Up Boss Account. Click on Sign in. 

Now enter your credentials for your Follow Up Boss Account 

After logging in, this will ask you for your Follow UP Boss API key. 

Click on the blue link in the screenshot above to be taken to the page to retrieve your API key. 

To find your API Key, you'll first want to log into your account and head to "Admin", followed by "API". 

Once you've entered your API Key and clicked continue, we'll test your account to make sure the connection works. If it does, you're all set!

How to integrate WiseAgent into your Roomvu acount? 

How to integrate WiseAgent into your Roomvu acount? 

Learn how to export your roomvu leads in your WiseAgent CRM in simple and visual steps. 

March 11, 2024 

Table of contents 

WiseAgent is a simple, smart, and affordable Real Estate CRM software many agents use. WiseAgent automates their marketing or transactions. It was built by agents for agents and is very simple to set up and easy to use. Wise Agent Lead Management System is customizable and you are able to set up different rules for different lead sources. As an agent who gets Real Estate leads in your roomvu using Ads, Landing Pages, etc. you might want to use WiseAgents to manage those leads. This article will explain how you can integrate WiseAgent into your roomvu account. 

What is WiseAgent 

Like most other agents, you want to provide a remarkable customer experience and create an extremely thriving Real Estate business. However, you can not run your business the old-fashioned way. You need to automate your marketing or transactions, and so you can work with the clients and make lots of money. Agents built wise Agent for agents. So you can automate your business, convert more leads, and actually live the lifestyle you came here for. 

How to Integrate WiseAgent in Your roomvu Account 

Follow up on your leads on roomvu using WiseAgent's real estate lead management system! Wise Agent's Lead Management System has been turning many heads and getting a lot of attention as more real estate agents and offices realize how powerful of a feature it has become. At the same time, it remains very simple to set up and easy to use. While many real estate lead management systems are set up to launch auto-replies and drip campaigns, most choices are limited. 

Wise Agent Lead Management software also includes several different lead reports that can be generated to show what sources lead are coming from, the status and rank of leads, and how many leads were assigned to team members. 

Integrating WiseAgent into your account is pretty simple. All you have to do is follow the below steps and you are good to go. Watch the video below, or if you do not feel like it, skip to the text tutorial. 

Step 1: Get Your WiseAgent API Key 

Log in to your WiseAgent account and click “ Integration” in the top middle section of the main page. Then select “Settings” . 

On the next window, Click on “API Keys and Lead Email” to open its drop-down menu. Now under “API Key” click on the copy icon to copy your key. 

Step 2: Integrate Your WiseAgent Key in roomvu 

Now head to your roomvu account and click “Leads Management” from the left sidebar. 

Now, on the top-right corner, click on “Get Leads on Your CRM”. 

Now paste the “ API Key ” you copied from your WiseAgent account in the next window below and click on Add. 

ENLARGE 

Now, you will get your leads from roomvu in WiseAgent CRM.

How to convert your personal Instagram account to a professional account? 

How to convert your personal Instagram account to a professional account? 

Learn How to Set Up a Business Account on Instagram 

March 11, 2024 

Table of contents 

On Instagram, you can always convert your personal account to a business and professional account to access more features that can help you grow your business even further. Please note that using a personal account for Real Estate is not recommended on Instagram. As a Real Estate agent, you need to use a business account to make the most out of all the features the platform offers to grow your business. This article will teach you how to convert your personal Instagram account to a professional account. 

Why Convert Your Personal Instagram Account 

An Instagram business account will enable you to access insights that will help you understand your audience better and find out who is engaging with your business on Instagram. Your Professional Dashboard will allow you to track your performance, access and discover professional tools, and explore educational information curated by Instagram. 

How to Convert Your Personal Instagram Account 

Please note that you may only have 5 Instagram accounts at a time. To convert your profile to a business account follow these steps: 

Go to your profile and tap 

in the upper right corner. 

Tap 

Settings. 

For some accounts, the Switch to Professional Account option will be listed directly under 

Settings. If not Tap Account . 

Tap Switch to Professional Account . 

Tap Continue. 

Select a Category for your business and tap Done. 

Tap Business . 

Add Contact details and tap Next. Or tap Don’t use my contact info to skip this step. 

If you'd like, you can follow the steps to connect your business account to a Facebook Page associated with your business. This step is optional and will make it easier to use all of the features available for businesses across the Meta family of apps. Currently, only one Facebook Page can be connected to your business account. 

You can also display or hide your business category and contact information on your profile. After the above steps, go to your profile and tap Edit Profile . 

Go to Profile Display under Public Business Information, 

Choose whether to hide or display your category label and contact info. Then, tap Done .

Connect Facebook Page to Instagram Business Account 

Connect Facebook Page to Instagram Business Account 

This article will teach you how to connect your Instagram Business account to a Facebook Page. 

January 4, 2024 

Table of contents 

Upon switching to a business account on Instagram, you'll be given the option to connect to a Facebook Page. This option is not mandatory; however, to get the most out of Instagram's business tools, you should link your Instagram business account to a Facebook Account. The Facebook page you connect to your Instagram account can be changed anytime. This article will teach you how to do so in a few easy-to-follow steps. 

Why Connect Your Instagram Business Account to a Facebook Page 

Connecting your Instagram Business account to a Facebook page has a few perks. For example, you can: 

Run Instagram and Facebook ads from your Page. 

Post efficiently on both platforms. 

Manage your messages across Messenger and Instagram from a single unified inbox. 

Gain access to cross-app tools such as appointment booking buttons, donation stickers, and camera effects. 

Sync business contact information 

Notes 

You need an Instagram business account to connect to a Facebook page. 

Your personal Facebook account must have an Admin role on the Page you’d like to connect to. 

If the Page you'd like to connect to is unavailable, it may be because you are not an admin of that Page. Make sure you are an admin on that page. 

How to: 

Go to your Instagram profile. 

Select Edit Profile . 

Under Public Business Information, Select Page . 

Tap Create Facebook Page or Connect an Existing Page. 

Choose a Page from your Pages that you'd like to connect to, or select Create a New Facebook Page . 

Tap Done after you've chosen a Page or created a new Page. 

Your Instagram business account is now connected to your Facebook Page, and you can benefit from the features Facebook offers.

## How to Add a Link to Your Instagram Stories | Roomvu Help Center

How to Add a Link to Your Instagram Stories 

How to Add a Link to Your Instagram Stories 

Learn how to add a link to your Instagram stories and guide your audience to the webpages you define. A step-by-step guide. 

January 4, 2024 

Table of contents 

Instagram stories are the new trend in social media, where users can easily share images and 15-second videos. Instagram stories are very popular since they allow users to post content for a short time. Stories disappear after 24 hours but are stored in the users' archive section and can be permanently added to your highlights. Another advantage to Instagram stories is the fact that users can put a link to their own desired destination. In this article, we will teach you how to add a link to your Instagram stories for real estate and take your followers to certain web pages. 

Links on Instagram Stories 

Instagram stories allow users to share links to specific web pages. A while ago, only pages with a minimum of 10K followers could add links to their stories. However, after recent updates to Instagram, all users can now use links in their stories. Real estate agents can now freely guide their audience to their specific web pages. They can be certain listings, landing pages, etc. 

How to Add a Link to Your Instagram Stories 

First, log in to your roomvu dashboard and click on " News and Landing Pages. " 

Step 2: Pick the news title you like to share 

Step 3: Hover on the story image and click " Download (Story). " The news story will be downloaded to your computer. 

Now, Click on the same news article again and click on the copy link icon. 

Now, let's see how you can add a link to your Instagram stories: 

Step 1: Open the Instagram app on your phone and tap on the + button to add a story: 

Step 2 : On the next screen, click on the "story" and then tap on your phone's gallery to select the image or the video you want to share: 

Step 3: Pick the image or the video and tap the stickers icon in the top right corner. 

Step 4 : Select the " LINK" option on the next screen. 

Step 5 : Paste the link address to the news story you copied earlier and click "done." 

Step 6: On the next screen, move the link icon on the screen to where you see fit and then click on " Your Story " to post the story. 

And now you are done. Your audience can click on the link you have shared on the story to visit the webpage you have picked.

## How to reauthorize your Facebook permissions for Roomvu dashboard? | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/8774443-how-to-reauthorize-your-facebook-permissions-for-roomvu-dashboard

How to reauthorize your Facebook permissions for Roomvu dashboard? | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content

All Collections 

Social media 

How to reauthorize your Facebook permissions for Roomvu dashboard? 

How to reauthorize your Facebook permissions for Roomvu dashboard? 

A step-by-step guide to reauthorize Facebook permissions for your roomvu dashboard and start posting great content again. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Now and then, you might encounter issues with your Facebook page on the roomvu dashboard that stop you from posting content to Facebook. In this case, you might need to reauthorize Facebook access and permissions for your roomvu dashboard. This procedure is simple and can be done quickly through the steps explained in this article. 

Why Do I Need to Re-authorize Permissions? 

If you are experiencing any of the following issues, you might need to reauthorize your roomvu permissions for Facebook: 

roomvu dashboard isn’t displaying your Facebook Page when connecting a Profile. 

roomvu dashboard isn't displaying your Instagram Profile when connecting a Profile. 

Your Facebook posts are not being published. 

Your Facebook Page keeps getting disconnected. 

Possible Causes 

You might have accidentally removed permission that roomvu requires. 

If you have recently added a new page to your Facebook profile, you need to reauthorize your account so that the new page includes the same roomvu permissions. 

Sometimes, permission tokens are invalidated by Facebook for security reasons. In this case you need to reconnect roomvu to get one. 

How to Reauthorize Your Facebook Permissions 

Go to Facebook and navigate to " Security & Privacy ". 

Click on " Settings " and then on " Business Integrations ". 

Find roomvu and then use the checkbox to select it and then click on the " Remove " button. 

Next, Facebook will ask you to confirm. There will be an option that asks you if you want to remove all the images, videos, etc., that roomvu has posted on your behalf. Be careful here and ensure this option is unchecked, or Facebook will delete all your previously published videos. Click "Remove" 

There will be another pop-up telling you that roomvu has been removed. Click " Done. " 

Now, you need to connect your roomvu dashboard to your Facebook account. 

Click "More" on the bottom left corner 

Find Facebook and click on " Connect ". 

A pop-up window from Facebook saying that roomvu will have access to your name, profile photo, and email address will appear. Click on " Continue " 

If you have not already signed in to Facebook on your browser, you might need to enter your Facebook account's username and password. 

Next, another window from Facebook will tell you that: 

"roomvu would like to manage your ads, access your Facebook ads and related stats, manage your business, access your Page and App insights, read content posted on the Page and create and manage content on your Page." 

Click on " Okay. " 

Now go back to your dashboard, pick the Facebook page you want to connect, and click on " Save. " 

Now, you have successfully connected roomvu dashboard to your Facebook business page. If you go to settings in " Content Calendar, " you will see this:

## How to Embed Your roomvu Videos to Your Website Using iFrame | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/8774451-how-to-embed-your-roomvu-videos-to-your-website-using-iframe

How to Embed Your roomvu Videos to Your Website Using iFrame | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Settings 

How to Embed Your roomvu Videos to Your Website Using iFrame 

How to Embed Your roomvu Videos to Your Website Using iFrame 

A step-by-step guide to embed your real estate videos to your website using iFrame and WordPress embed function. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Embedding videos is a great way to share videos without uploading them directly to your website's server. Since you might need to use many of them, embedding helps save space on your website's server, and it's easier than uploading a video. In this article, we will teach you how to embed your roomvu videos to your website in a few straightforward steps. 

What is Video Embedding? 

Video embedding is a process in which you can share a video on a website using a source located on a server other than your website's. Your website reads the data from the different servers and uses a frame on a specific page to share the video. Users can click on the video and watch it as if it were on your website. 

Why Embed Videos 

Let's see why you should embed videos rather than directly upload them: 

Videos Use a Lot of Space 

Videos are large files that take up space. Depending on the quality and length of the video, its size can be anywhere from megabytes to tens of megabytes. Apart from the fact that you do not have to upload them at all (because of the option of embedding) videos come in different formats and sizes, which have to be optimized before adding them to your website. This adds to an already complicated process. 

It is Easier to Embed Than to Upload 

Uploading to the server can be a complicated task, along with putting pressure on the server. When there are many free video-sharing websites like YouTube and Vimeo, it does not make sense to try and host the videos on your website. Many big names in the business use YouTube, etc., to share their videos online and embed them on their websites. 

Embed as Many Times as You Like 

Embedding allows you to upload the video once and share it as many times as you like on many websites. For example, when a video is uploaded on roomvu or YouTube servers, you just need an iFrame code to share the video on any website. 

WordPress users often come across iframes when trying to embed something from an external source into their WordPress site. The most common example of an iframe embed code is the YouTube video embed code, which looks like this: 

<iframe width="640" height="480" src=" https://www.roomvu.com/agent/embed/lilian-smith-2/treb-condo-signs-life " frameborder="0" allow="accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture" allowfullscreen></iframe> 

How to Embed Videos to Your Website 

In this example, we assume you use WordPress to manage your website and will explain the steps accordingly. Still, the process is similar regardless since iFrame is a universal HTML code applicable to all websites. 

How to get the iFrame Codes for Your roomvu Videos 

On your dashboard, in “ Videos and News ” find the video you would like to embed on your website. Select it, click on three dots, and click “Embed Video “ 

A new window will open, showing the iframe code you need. Click on “Copy Code.” This will copy the iFrame code to your clipboard. 

How to Insert iFrame Codes into Your Website 

Go to your website’s WordPress dashboard and open the post you want to use the video in or create a new post. 

If you are using “ Block Editor ” ( needs WordPress 5.0 or higher ) on WordPress, click on “ Add block ” and search for “ Custom HTML “. 

Now right-click on the text space that reads “ Write HTML ” and “ Paste ” the code you copied from YouTube into the field. 

The code will be pasted into the block. 

You can also click on “ Preview ” to see if the code works. 

Classic Editor 

The process is slightly different if you use “Classic Editor” in WordPress. You need to select “insert,” then “media,” and then the “ embed ” tab. Now you can right-click and paste the iFrame code for your roomvu video. 

How to Embed YouTube Videos 

Find your video on YouTube and click the “ Share ” button below the video. 

Then select “ Embed .” 

Now copy the code that is displayed. You can also click on the “ Start at ” option to set a time other than the beginning of the video to make the video start somewhere in the middle. 

Alternative Option: Direct Embeds 

If you use “ Block Editor ” on your WordPress dashboard, you can paste a link instead of an iFrame Code directly to a simple block. WordPress will automatically turn it into an Embedded video. 

On YouTube “ Copy ” the link to the video. 

Now, on your post, paste the link into a default paragraph block. 

Note: This method does not work for all the videos from all sources. You might run into this message that says the video cannot be embedded. In this case, try option one above. 

Embed Your roomvu Videos to Your Website: Final Words 

Embedding videos is more convenient than actually uploading them to your website. It takes little time, does not use as much space on your website’s server, and can be used on many websites with a single code. You need your video’s iFrame code so you can use it on your website’s editor. Use Custom HTML or paste the video URL instead of the iFrame code to embed the video. The whole process is straightforward and can be done in a few steps. If you have any questions, leave a comment below, and we will help you with how to embed your videos into your website.

How to Download Videos from Your roomvu Dashboard

## How to Import and Share Your Reviews and Testimonials on roomvu | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/8774514-how-to-import-and-share-your-reviews-and-testimonials-on-roomvu

How to Import and Share Your Reviews and Testimonials on roomvu | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Settings 

How to Import and Share Your Reviews and Testimonials on roomvu 

How to Import and Share Your Reviews and Testimonials on roomvu 

Learn how to import reviews from Google, Zillow, and Testimonial Tree into roomvu. Reviews are auto-shared with your branding across social media, VuCard, and your website on a weekly basis. 

Updated over a week ago 

Table of contents 

Your reviews and testimonials are some of your most powerful marketing assets. roomvu lets you import them from multiple sources and automatically share them across your social media, VuCard, and website with your branding applied. Once the setup is complete, the process runs on its own. 

​ 

How it works 

roomvu fetches the 5 most recent reviews from Google and 10 from Zillow during the initial import. 

Only reviews with a rating of 4 stars or higher are imported. 

New reviews are fetched and added automatically on a weekly basis, so your content stays fresh without any manual effort. 

Note: If you notice fewer reviews imported than expected, one common reason is that reviews without any written text are not imported, only those with a rating and no accompanying comment are skipped. If you have reviews that appear on Google or Zillow but are not showing up in roomvu, this is likely why. Please note this may not be the only reason in every case. 

​ 

How to import your reviews 

There are several ways to connect your review sources to roomvu. Click the "Gear" icon on the top right corner to enter settings. Then on the left menu find and click " Client Reviews (Testimonials) " to enter the interface . 

Google Business Profile (connected account) 

If you have already connected your Google Business Profile to roomvu for content sharing, roomvu can use that same connection to import your reviews. This is the simplest option if your Google account is already linked. 

​ 

If you want to import reviews from a different Google Business page than the one connected to roomvu, make sure you are logged in to that Google account in your browser before proceeding. 

​ 

Import via Google Maps Link 

If you prefer to import reviews using a direct Google Maps link, follow these steps: 

Go to google.com/maps . 

Search for your name or business name. 

Click Share on your Google Business listing. 

Click Copy Link to copy the URL. 

Paste the link into roomvu testimonials import engine . 

For a full visual walkthrough of this process, visit this guide . 

​ 

Import from Testimonial Tree 

To connect your Testimonial Tree account, you will need your API token. Here is how to find it: 

Log in to your Testimonial Tree account. 

Navigate to Management then API . 

Click Generate API Authentication Token . 

Copy the token that appears. On PC use Ctrl+C and on Mac use Command+C. 

Paste the token into the corresponding field in roomvu. 

Import from Zillow 

To import your Zillow reviews, enter the email address associated with your Zillow profile into the Zillow field in roomvu. The system will automatically locate and import your reviews. 

​ 

Import Manually 

This is the less convenient way but if the review you have is not on the above platforms, you can add it manually. 

Where do your reviews appear? 

Once imported, your reviews are automatically shared with your branding across: 

Your social media accounts 

Your roomvu VuCard 

Your connected website 

New reviews continue to be pulled in weekly so your audience always sees your most recent feedback without you having to do anything.

Profile photo and Cover Image

## How to Clean and Organize Your Contacts for Email Marketing in Roomvu | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/8774548-how-to-clean-and-organize-your-contacts-for-email-marketing-in-roomvu

How to Clean and Organize Your Contacts for Email Marketing in Roomvu | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard

English 

Your Dashboard

All Collections 

Video Guides 

How to Clean and Organize Your Contacts for Email Marketing in Roomvu 

How to Clean and Organize Your Contacts for Email Marketing in Roomvu 

This article explains how to upload and clean contact lists in Roomvu email marketing using Simple Upload or AI cleaning, how to confirm lawful contact consent, and how to finalize contact import. 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

roomvu includes a built-in feature that helps you clean, organize, and prepare your contact list before using it for email marketing campaigns. 

​ 

If your contact file includes duplicates, formatting issues, or unnecessary data, Roomvu can process and clean it for you during upload. 

​ 

This guide explains how to upload and clean your contacts inside your account. 

Why Clean Your Contact List? 

A clean contact list helps: 

Improve email deliverability 

Remove duplicates 

Avoid invalid email addresses 

Keep your campaigns organized 

Reduce bounce rates 

Roomvu provides two upload options to help you achieve this. 

How to Upload and Clean Your Contacts 

Step 1: Open Email Campaigns 

Log in to your Roomvu account and click Email Newsletters from the left menu. 

Step 2: Go to Contacts 

Find and click Contacts , then select All Contacts . 

Step 3: Upload Your CSV File 

Click Upload Contact CSV . 

A pop-up window will appear with two processing options. 

Choose Your Upload Method 

You will see two options: 

Option 1: Use AI 

We recommend that you try to upload your contacts using AI first. This option uses AI to further clean and organize your contacts. 

​ 

Option 2: Simple Upload (Recommended) 

If the first option does not work your can try the next option. With Simple Upload , Roomvu automatically processes your file and performs standard cleaning. 

We recommend starting with this option first. 

Upload Your File 

After choosing your preferred method: 

Click Choose Your Contacts File 

Select your CSV file 

Confirm that you have obtained these contacts in a lawful and compliant manner 

You must confirm that your contacts have opted in to receive marketing emails. Uploading purchased or non-consented contact lists is not allowed. 

Step 4: Confirm Import 

After reviewing the report, click Confirm Import to finalize the process. 

Your cleaned contacts will now be available in your Contact List. 

Important Reminder About Compliance 

You must only upload contacts who have: 

Opted in to receive marketing emails 

Given you permission to contact them 

Avoid uploading purchased contact lists or batch contacts to protect your account and maintain compliance with email marketing regulations.

## How to balance Roomvu content with personal posts? | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/8823874-how-to-balance-roomvu-content-with-personal-posts

How to balance Roomvu content with personal posts? | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Tutorials 

How to balance Roomvu content with personal posts? 

How to balance Roomvu content with personal posts? 

How to Complement Roomvu's Automated Services with Your Unique Brand Persona for a Compelling Social Media Presence 

March 7, 2025 

Table of contents 

At roomvu , we provide high-quality, automated social media content to keep your business visible and engaging. From real estate market updates to homebuyer tips and neighborhood insights, our content helps establish you as a trusted expert. However, social media is not just about sharing industry updates—it’s about connecting with your audience on a personal level. 

If our system detects that your Instagram account is primarily posting business content, we recommend adding more personal content to improve your reach, engagement, and overall brand presence. Here’s why it matters and how to do it effectively. 

Why Balancing Personal and Business Content Matters 

1. Social Media is About Connection, Not Just Information 

People follow and engage with people , not just businesses. If your profile looks like an industry news feed, your audience may feel disconnected. Sharing personal content helps humanize your brand and makes you more relatable. 

2. People Remember Faces, Not Just Facts 

Studies show that people remember faces better than logos or text . If your Instagram feed lacks photos or videos of you, followers may not recognize or recall you when they need a real estate professional. 

3. Personal Posts Increase Engagement 

Business posts are valuable, but personal posts—such as behind-the-scenes content, lifestyle updates, and real moments—often generate more likes, comments, and shares. This boosts your overall reach, making even your business content more visible. 

4. Build Trust and Credibility 

Real estate is a relationship-based business. Clients choose to work with agents they know, like, and trust . Personal content helps build this trust by showing your personality, values, and daily life. 

How to Add Personal Content to Your Instagram Strategy 

1. Use roomvu’s Video Introduction Feature 

• Record a short 5-second video introduction inviting viewers to watch your roomvu videos. 

• This makes your automated posts feel more personal and builds your brand identity. 

• Example script: 

“Hey, I’m [Your Name]! Here’s a quick update on the real estate market—stay tuned for valuable insights.” 

• Check out our guide on [how to add personal video intros to roomvu videos]. 

2. Show Behind-the-Scenes Content 

• Share what goes on in your day-to-day real estate business. 

• Ideas: 

• A sneak peek of an upcoming listing. 

• A casual video before meeting a client. 

• A photo of you working at a coffee shop. 

• This makes your brand more authentic and engaging. 

3. Post Lifestyle & Personal Updates 

• Show who you are beyond real estate —this makes you more relatable. 

• Ideas: 

• Share a hobby or weekend activity (hiking, cooking, fitness, etc.). 

• A candid family moment (if comfortable sharing). 

• Inspirational quotes or personal reflections. 

4. Use Instagram Stories for Real-Time Engagement 

• Instagram Stories disappear in 24 hours, making them perfect for quick personal updates . 

• Post daily moments , even if they’re casual. 

• Examples: 

• A video walking through a new listing. 

• A behind-the-scenes look at an open house. 

• A poll asking followers what type of content they want to see. 

5. Engage With Your Audience 

• Respond to comments and DMs—make conversations personal! 

• Like and comment on followers’ posts to show you’re active. 

• Host Q&A sessions in Instagram Stories to answer real estate-related questions. 

Finding the Right Balance 

How Much Personal vs. Business Content Should You Post? 

A good content ratio is: 

✅ 70% business-related posts (roomvu content, market updates, tips) 

✅ 30% personal content (behind-the-scenes, lifestyle, engaging stories) 

If you’re currently posting 100% automated business content , start introducing one personal post per week and adjust based on engagement. 

Final Thoughts: Make Your Instagram More Human 

roomvu helps you maintain a consistent, professional social media presence, but your personal touch is what truly makes your brand stand out . 

✔ Add a mix of personal and business content to keep your audience engaged. 

✔ Show your face —people connect with people, not just posts. 

✔ Use Stories, lifestyle posts, and engagement tactics to build relationships. 

🚀 Start adding more personal content today and watch your Instagram reach grow!

How Tiktok scheduling for real estate works in Roomvu?

Table of contents 

You can use Roomvu to post Real Estate content on TikTok automatically. When it's time to post, your video will be automatically published on your behalf. ​

## How Roomvu posts on your behalf: A guide for real estate agents and mortgage brokers | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/8823887-how-roomvu-posts-on-your-behalf-a-guide-for-real-estate-agents-and-mortgage-brokers

How Roomvu posts on your behalf: A guide for real estate agents and mortgage brokers | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Content Calendar 

How Roomvu posts on your behalf: A guide for real estate agents and mortgage brokers 

How Roomvu posts on your behalf: A guide for real estate agents and mortgage brokers 

Understanding How Roomvu Effectively Manages Social Media Posts for Real Estate Professionals 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

If you're a real estate agent or mortgage broker, you may have wondered how Roomvu consistently posts tailored, hyper-local content on your social media accounts. It's a question we hear often, and understandably so. Entrusting your social media strategy to an external service is a big step, and you'd naturally want to know how the gears turn behind the scenes. That's why we've created this guide to shed light on the precise process Roomvu follows to post content on your behalf, keeping your online presence as engaging and relevant as possible. 

Now, let's dive into the nitty-gritty of how it all works. 

​ 

The Mechanism: API and Authorization 

One of the most critical aspects to understand is how securely Roomvu interacts with your social media accounts. You might be concerned about linking your social platforms to an external service, but rest assured, this is an entirely safe process. 

How It's Secure 

Authorization : The initial step involves linking your social media accounts to Roomvu. During this stage, OAuth (Open Authorization) protocols come into play. These protocols permit Roomvu to interact with your social media accounts without revealing your login credentials. 

Access Tokens : Once you've granted permission, roomvu receives what is known as an "access token" from the social media platform. This token is a secure key that lets roomvu post on your behalf without accessing your account directly. 

API-Enabled : The connection is established through official APIs provided by the social media platforms. These APIs are designed with security in mind, ensuring a safe bridge between roomvu and your social media accounts. 

Revocable Access : It's worth noting that these access tokens are entirely within your control. You can revoke these permissions at any time, giving you full authority over what happens to your account. 

Using OAuth protocols and access tokens means that roomvu never has access to your social media credentials. Instead, we interact with your accounts via a secure pathway established by the APIs, ensuring the utmost safety and security. 

​ 

The Content: Personalized and Relevant 

One of the standout features of roomvu is the personalization of content. Unlike generic social media posts, roomvu crafts each video or post focusing on hyper-local and relevant topics. You can always review your content calendar to see the content specifically picked and scheduled for you and your audience. 

Approve or Delete 

When reviewing the content on your calendar , you have two options 

Approve : No action is needed if the content aligns with your marketing goals. The post will automatically go live at the scheduled time. 

Delete : You can cancel the post if you feel the content is unsuitable. Over time, our system learns from your preferences to better curate future content. 

Two Weeks in Advance 

roomvu also offers the convenience of reviewing your scheduled content for the next two weeks. This foresight allows you to plan other aspects of your marketing campaign more efficiently. 

​ 

Conclusion 

In summary, roomvu's approach offers a hassle-free, secure, and personalized way to manage social media accounts. By leveraging technology similar to platforms like Hootsuite and coupling it with highly specialized content, roomvu helps real estate agents and mortgage brokers become market leaders in the digital age. 

​ 

By staying consistently visible on social media with high-quality, relevant posts, you reach potential clients and build a strong brand. With roomvu by your side, rest assured your online presence is in good hands. 

​ 

For more tips on social media marketing for real estate agents and mortgage brokers, stay tuned to roomvu Academy. 

Related Articles

How can I ensure that the content Roomvu posts on my social media complies with the regulations of the Mortgage Brokers industry? 

How can I ensure that the content Roomvu posts on my social media complies with the regulations of the Mortgage Brokers industry? 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

We make every effort to adhere to industry regulations. However, for added assurance, you can complete a compliance form and designate a contact person along with their email address. We will then send the planned content to this email every two days for review. The compliance officer has the authority to halt the publication of any content deemed inappropriate. Additionally, they will receive emails containing the following week's content. It's optional for you to respond to our emails; in the absence of a reply, we will assume there are no issues and proceed with publishing the content on your behalf.
