Roomvu's content engine 

Roomvu's content engine 

Inside Roomvu's Content Engine: How We Source, Create, and Automate Social Media Posts for Real Estate Professionals 

March 11, 2024 

Table of contents 

Creating content on social media can be challenging due to the vast audience and the constant need for fresh and relevant material. One common question arises: how does roomvu produce a steady stream of local, trustworthy content? The answer lies in roomvu's content strategy, which incorporates an advanced AI engine and a meticulously curated library of media assets. 

AI-Powered Content Vetting 

roomvu's content strategy leverages an AI engine that processes over 130,000 daily articles. This robust system performs several vital functions: 

Content Validation : The AI ensures we source information from credible, reputable news providers. 

Geographical Relevance : It adjusts the focus of news stories to create content tailored to specific regions, aligning with roomvu's emphasis on localized information. 

Content Summarization : It aids in distilling large volumes of text into key informational nuggets, thus making it easier for our audience to consume. 

Real-Time Updates : Operating in real-time, the AI engine keeps us ahead of the curve regarding the latest news and trends. 

Our Extensive Media Library 

Our content strategy at Roomvu involves maintaining an extensive library of over 80,000 micro footage, music assets, and AI-generated content. These media assets are carefully selected and curated, and we have full ownership of all of them. We take pride in that some of these assets are exclusively created by our network of skilled photographers, ensuring that our content is unique and of high quality. 

Commitment to Transparency and Intellectual Property 

We understand the importance of ethical content production. When we create content based on news articles, our process includes: 

Proper Attribution : We ensure we cite the news providers clearly and correctly. 

Traffic Back to the Source : We include backlinks to the original articles, allowing our audience to delve deeper into the subjects. 

Summarization and Originality : Our content adds value by offering unique perspectives or presenting information in a digestible format, ensuring we're not merely echoing what's already out there. 

Our track record of zero copyright infringement claims over the past five years attests to our commitment to responsible content creation. 

Conclusion 

At Roomvu, our content strategy is designed to prioritize creating top-notch content that is both relevant and informative. We take great care to ensure that our content is original and respects the intellectual property rights of creators. Our approach involves a range of measures, such as thorough research, fact-checking, and plagiarism checks, to ensure that we maintain our reputation for authenticity and integrity in the digital world.

Table of contents 

Navigating the world of real estate marketing can be challenging, but with roomvu, agents are offered a seamless and efficient way to integrate video marketing into their strategy. A common question many agents have is about the turnaround time for video production once their MLS listing is live. 

Understanding the Process 

Once a listing goes live on the MLS database, there's a natural curiosity about how soon a video can be produced. The key lies in the updating of our data. It generally takes just a few hours for our system to sync with the latest MLS listings. The efficiency of this process ensures that your marketing materials are as current as possible. 

Immediate Access to Videos 

The moment our data is updated with your new listing, the video becomes available for use. This quick turnaround is part of roomvu's commitment to providing timely and relevant content for your marketing needs. 

Ensuring Smooth Integration 

To guarantee that this process works seamlessly, it’s crucial for agents to log in to their roomvu dashboard. Once there, ensure that your listing is correctly linked to your profile under the MLS section. This step is vital to ensure the automatic generation of your listing videos, including updates like open houses. 

Leveraging Roomvu for Effective Marketing 

Roomvu's platform is designed not just to provide quick video content but also to integrate these videos effectively into your marketing campaigns. By leveraging Roomvu, agents can significantly enhance their online presence, positioning themselves as market leaders in the ever-competitive real estate landscape. 

Conclusion 

In conclusion, with Roomvu, the time from MLS listing going live to having a professionally crafted video ready for your marketing purposes is impressively short, typically just a few hours. This rapid turnaround ensures that your marketing efforts are always fresh, relevant, and engaging, giving you a competitive edge in the real estate market. Remember, the key to making this process work smoothly is ensuring that your listings are correctly linked in your Roomvu dashboard. The key advantage of this integration is the automation feature. This doesn't mean losing control over your content; manual posting is still an option if you prefer a more hands-on approach. roomvu Content Calendar: A Comprehensive Guide 

A Step-by-Step Guide to Setting Up and Customizing Your roomvu Content Calendar 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Maintaining an edge in the competitive landscape of real estate requires innovative marketing strategies. That's precisely what Roomvu aims to provide with its content calendar tool, designed to streamline your marketing efforts and enhance your online visibility. Our latest tutorial, "Master Your Roomvu Content Calendar: A Complete Setup & Customization Tutorial," walks you through the entire process, ensuring you can efficiently manage and optimize your content strategy. 

Why Your Marketing Strategy Needs a Content Calendar 

In digital marketing, consistency and relevance are key to engaging your audience and building your brand. A content calendar acts as your marketing roadmap, helping you to plan out your content, align it with your marketing objectives, and keep your audience engaged across all platforms. 

Navigating the Roomvu Content Calendar 

Our detailed tutorial video guides you through every aspect of setting up and customizing your Roomvu content calendar, making it a powerful component of your marketing toolkit. Here are the steps covered: 

Step 1: Account Login and Calendar Access 

Start by logging into your Roomvu account and selecting the " Content Calendar " from the left sidebar to view your scheduled content and access calendar settings. 

Step 2: Connect Your Social Media Channels 

Enhance your content’s reach by connecting your social media accounts. Navigate to "Connect More Socials" to link platforms such as YouTube and WordPress, allowing for direct content sharing. 

Step 3: Customize Your Content Settings 

Dive into "Content Settings" to tailor your content's frequency and types. Set your primary and secondary cities under the "Location" tab to generate hyper-local content, ensuring your posts resonate with your target market. 

Step 4: Define Your Content Preferences 

Specify the quantity and types of content you wish to post, keeping in mind the optimal number of weekly posts. Adjust your settings to include listings, local and national event content, and even Spanish content for specific regions. 

​ 

​ 

​ 

Step 5: Fine-Tune Content Sources and Hashtags 

Customize which sources your content is pulled from by excluding any undesired URLs. Additionally, optimize your hashtag strategy in the "Hashtags" tab, adding or removing tags to match your marketing needs. 

Step 6: Add a Personal Touch to Your Posts 

Create a versatile video caption to accompany your posts, adding a personal touch that makes your content stand out. 

​ 

​ 

​ 

Step 7: Expand Your Content Selection 

Learn how to further enrich your calendar by adding Roomvu-generated videos, market news images, and lead-generating landing pages. Discover how to upload your own videos and images, and how to create posts from intriguing news stories.

## FAQ: SEO and roomvu's Services for Real Estate Marketing | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/9140371-faq-seo-and-roomvu-s-services-for-real-estate-marketing

FAQ: SEO and roomvu's Services for Real Estate Marketing | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Features 

FAQ: SEO and roomvu's Services for Real Estate Marketing 

FAQ: SEO and roomvu's Services for Real Estate Marketing 

Enhancing Your Online Presence: Leveraging Roomvu for Strategic SEO, Local Keywords, and Social Media Engagement in Real Estate 

April 1, 2024 

Table of contents 

What is SEO, and why is it important for real estate marketing? 

SEO, or Search Engine Optimization, involves optimizing your online content so it appears prominently in search engine results. It is essential for real estate agents and brokers to increase visibility and attract potential clients. Since most homebuyers start their search online, effective SEO ensures your listings and content are easily discoverable. 

How does roomvu help with SEO for real estate? 

roomvu specializes in creating SEO-optimized content tailored for real estate agents and brokers. This includes hyper-local videos, blog posts, and social media content designed to enhance your online visibility, attract more potential clients, and position you as a market leader in your area. 

Can roomvu optimize content for local markets? 

Yes, roomvu focuses on local SEO by integrating relevant local search terms and keywords into your content. This enhances your visibility in specific geographic areas you serve, making it easier for potential clients searching for properties or real estate services in your area to find you. 

How does roomvu ensure content quality for SEO? 

roomvu prioritizes high-quality, relevant content that caters to your target audience's interests and needs. From informative blog posts to engaging videos and virtual tours, all content is optimized with relevant keywords to improve readability, engagement, and search engine rankings. 

How does roomvu utilize social media for real estate SEO? 

roomvu leverages various social media platforms, including Facebook, Instagram, LinkedIn, Twitter, TikTok, and YouTube, to maximize your SEO benefits. By creating platform-specific content, roomvu helps engage your audience, drive traffic to your website, and improve your online visibility and lead-generation efforts. 

How do social signals impact real estate SEO with roomvu? 

roomvu recognizes the importance of social signals like likes, shares, and comments in enhancing your content's SEO value. High engagement on social media platforms can increase visibility, backlinks, and mentions, drawing more potential clients to your listings or content. 

Would roomvu be able to help with local SEO strategies? 

Absolutely, roomvu emphasizes local SEO by optimizing your Google My Business listing, securing local backlinks, and using location-based keywords. This connects your services with local searchers, which is crucial for real estate agents and brokers focusing on specific geographic areas. 

How Can I Use Keywords in Hashtags and Captions for SEO Improvement 

Identify Effective Keywords 

You can start by identifying high-volume, relevant keywords that potential clients might use when searching for your area's properties or real estate services. Tools like Google Keyword Planner can help you discover keywords such as “homes for sale in [Location]” or “[Location] real estate agent.” These keywords are crucial for optimizing your content and hashtags to match user search queries. 

Incorporating Local Keywords in Hashtags 

Use local keywords as hashtags in your posts for social media platforms, especially Instagram and Twitter. For example, #CaliforniaHomes or #TorontoRealEstate. These localized hashtags help your content appear in searches related to specific locations, making it easier for potential clients in those areas to find your services. 

Strategic Placement of Keywords in Captions 

When crafting captions for your social media posts, integrate relevant keywords naturally into the text. This helps with SEO and ensures that your content is engaging and informative. For instance, a caption could read, “Discover your dream home in the heart of California. #CaliforniaHomes for sale that offer both luxury and comfort.” 

Keywords in Video Content Descriptions 

For platforms like YouTube and TikTok, where video content is predominant, include keywords in your video titles, descriptions, and tags. This practice enhances your content's discoverability, driving more traffic to your videos and, subsequently, to your website. 

Hashtags for Community and Niche Engagement 

Utilize hashtags to connect with specific real estate communities or niches, such as #LuxuryHomes, #FirstTimeHomeBuyer, or #EcoFriendlyHomes. These targeted hashtags can attract viewers with specific interests, increasing engagement and potential leads. 

Monitoring and Adapting Your Keyword Strategy 

Please review the performance of your keywords and hashtags to see which ones drive the most engagement and traffic. Social media platforms and Google Analytics offer insights that can help you adjust your strategy for better results. 

Best Practices for SEO-Enhancing Hashtags and Captions 

Consistency is Key 

Regularly posting content with well-researched hashtags and captions can build momentum and improve your visibility over time. 

Engagement Boosts SEO 

You can just engage with comments and shares to boost your posts' visibility. You can encourage interactions by asking questions or asking about your content. 

Use a Mix of Broad and Niche Hashtags 

While broad hashtags increase visibility, niche hashtags can attract a more targeted audience. A mix of both can enhance your content's reach and relevance. 

Avoid Overstuffing 

While using keywords and hashtags is important, avoid overstuffing your captions and descriptions. Ensure your content remains engaging and reader-friendly. 

By integrating these strategies into your roomvu content creation process, you can significantly improve the SEO of your real estate marketing efforts, attract more potential clients, and enhance your online visibility in the competitive real estate market.

## Mortgage Broker Content Compliance: A roomvu Advantage | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/9331409-mortgage-broker-content-compliance-a-roomvu-advantage

Mortgage Broker Content Compliance: A roomvu Advantage | Roomvu Help Center

English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Features 

Mortgage Broker Content Compliance: A roomvu Advantage 

Mortgage Broker Content Compliance: A roomvu Advantage 

Ensuring Every Marketing Piece is Approved: How Roomvu's Compliance Feature Protects Mortgage Brokers' Content 

May 15, 2024 

Table of contents 

In the financial sector, maintaining Mortgage Broker Content Compliance is crucial, especially for those dealing with sensitive financial matters. Understanding this need, roomvu offers a robust compliance feature tailored specifically for mortgage brokers to ensure all content adheres to regulatory standards and company policies. 

What is Mortgage Broker Content Compliance in roomvu? 

When mortgage brokers log in to roomvu, they benefit from a systematic compliance process designed to safeguard their content. Every two weeks, all scheduled content is sent to the broker's management team for approval. This proactive measure ensures that all marketing materials are thoroughly reviewed and compliant with industry regulations before being published. 

The Compliance Process 

Content Submission : Every two weeks, roomvu compiles all the content scheduled for the mortgage broker. 

Management Review : The compiled content is sent to the broker’s management team for a detailed review. 

Approval or Flagging : The management team either approves the content or flags it for issues related to its copy or advertisement. 

Issue Resolution : If any content is flagged, it will not be scheduled for posting unless the manager or head office provides approval after necessary modifications. 

Why Compliance Matters 

Mortgage brokers handle highly sensitive financial information. Ensuring the accuracy and appropriateness of the content they share is paramount to maintaining trust and credibility with their clients. Here are a few reasons why compliance is vital: 

Regulatory Adherence : Compliance ensures that all content adheres to industry regulations, avoiding potential legal issues. 

Brand Integrity : Approved content maintains the integrity and professionalism of the broker’s brand. 

Client Trust : Ensuring that all information shared is accurate and compliant fosters trust among clients, which is essential in the financial industry. 

https://www.roomvu.com/academy/how-roomvu-works/ 

The roomvu Advantage 

roomvu's compliance feature is designed to streamline the approval process, saving mortgage brokers time and effort. By automating the content review and approval process, roomvu allows brokers to focus on their core business activities while ensuring that their marketing materials are always compliant. 

Mortgage Broker Content Compliance: Conclusion 

Compliance is a critical aspect of content marketing for mortgage brokers, and roomvu's compliance feature provides a reliable solution. By involving management in the content approval process, roomvu ensures that all marketing materials meet regulatory standards and uphold the broker's professional reputation. This meticulous approach not only protects the brokers but also reinforces client trust and confidence in their services. 

Embrace roomvu's compliance feature and ensure that your marketing content is always up to the mark.

Setup roomvu to Manage Campaigns and Contacts for Constant Contact 

Setup roomvu to Manage Campaigns and Contacts for Constant Contact 

How to enable Constant Contact email marketing for your roomvu account 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

We’re thrilled to announce our new integration with Constant Contact , a leader and pioneer in email marketing. This partnership is designed to take your email marketing to the next level, ensuring better deliverability, more engagement, and a seamless experience. 

How to Enable the Integration 

Getting started with Constant Contact is easy! Follow these steps: 

STEP 1: 

Navigate to the Email Newsletters page in your roomvu account . 

STEP 2: 

Click the "Connect" button to activate the integration. 

STEP 3: 

You need to upload your contacts first. 

STEP 4: 

Check your email inbox for a confirmation email from Constant Contact. Click the confirmation button to verify your email address. 

Once completed, you’re ready to leverage the power of Constant Contact for your email campaigns. 

Managing Your Constant Contact Campaign from Your Settings 

To view your Constant Contact email marketing status or make changes to your campaign settings: 

Step 1: Access Your Settings 

From your roomvu dashboard, click the gear icon in the top right corner. 

Step 2: Select Email Campaign (ConstantContact): 

Click “ Email Campaign (ConstantContact )” in the left-hand menu to open the Constant Contact email marketing settings. 

Here, you can: 

Status of your constant contact connection 

Log In to Your Assigned Constant Contact Account: Quickly switch to your Constant Contact dashboard for more in-depth configuration. 

View Campaign Stats: Track the metrics for each campaign, including: 

Scheduled At – The date and time your newsletter is set to send. 

Sent – How many emails have been delivered. 

Opened – The number of recipients who opened the email. 

Clicked – The count of recipients who clicked on a link within the email. 

Exclusive for Platinum and Diamond Users 

This powerful integration is available exclusively for our Platinum and Diamond users. Normally priced at $80 per month, this feature is already included in your current plan —no additional costs, just added value for your marketing efforts. 

How It Works 

With this integration, roomvu simplifies your email marketing: 

• We create your newsletters using Roomvu’s engaging and professional content. 

• These newsletters are sent directly through your Constant Contact account, ensuring your communications are polished, effective, and professional. 

Accessing Your Constant Contact Account 

If you ever need to access your Constant Contact account, simply go to your roomvu Settings page and click on the Login option. This provides direct access to manage your account or explore additional tools. 

Important Account & Contact Management Information 

To ensure a seamless experience with Constant Contact , there are a few critical things to keep in mind regarding contact management and account access: 

🔹 Your Dashboard is the Single Source of Truth 

All contacts are managed directly within your Roomvu dashboard . If a contact is removed from your dashboard, it will also be removed from your Constant Contact account automatically. Be sure to maintain an up-to-date contact list within Roomvu to avoid accidental deletions. 

🔹 What Happens If You Lose Access to Your Platinum or Diamond Account? 

Constant Contact is exclusively available to Platinum and Diamond users. If your subscription expires, is downgraded, or payment fails , your Constant Contact account will automatically be reassigned to another user , and you will no longer have access to it. 

To avoid disruptions in your email marketing, ensure your subscription remains active and that your payment information is up to date. 

This integration is designed to make email marketing effortless and effective , so keeping your account in good standing ensures you continue benefiting from professional, high-converting email campaigns. 

Why Constant Contact? 

Constant Contact has long been recognized as an industry leader in email marketing. Their robust platform enhances email deliverability, ensuring your newsletters reach your audience effectively. With this integration, your marketing campaigns will look professional and have a higher chance of being seen.

## How to Integrate Agent Locator with roomvu to Export Your Leads | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/9615698-how-to-integrate-agent-locator-with-roomvu-to-export-your-leads

How to Integrate Agent Locator with roomvu to Export Your Leads | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Settings 

How to Integrate Agent Locator with roomvu to Export Your Leads 

How to Integrate Agent Locator with roomvu to Export Your Leads 

Seamlessly Connect Your roomvu Leads to Agent Locator in Just a Few Easy Steps 

July 16, 2024 

Table of contents 

Integrating Agent Locator with roomvu allows real estate agents to seamlessly export leads generated by roomvu directly to their Agent Locator CRM. Follow these simple steps to ensure your leads are efficiently transferred between the two platforms. 

Step 1: Log in to Your Agent Locator Account 

Log in to your Agent Locator account. 

Click on your profile icon in the screen's top right corner. 

Select "User Preferences" from the dropdown menu. 

Step 2: Copy the Feed Leads by Email Address 

In the User Preferences window, scroll down to find the section labeled "Feed Leads by Email." 

Copy the email address provided in this section. You will need this email address to set up the integration for roomvu. 

Step 3: Log in to your roomvu Account 

Log in to your roomvu account. 

On the main window, navigate to the left sidebar and click "Leads Management." 

Step 4: Set Up Lead Export to Agent Locator 

In the Leads Management window, click on "Get Leads on Your CRM." 

From the pop-up window, select "Agent Locator" from the list of CRMs. 

Paste the email address you copied from the Agent Locator into the designated field. 

Click "Add" to finalize the integration. 

You're Done! 

Congratulations! Your roomvu account is now integrated with Agent Locator. All leads generated by roomvu will be automatically exported to your Agent Locator CRM, ensuring a seamless workflow and efficient lead management.

## How to Automatically Import Google Reviews into Your roomvu Account | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/9773521-how-to-automatically-import-google-reviews-into-your-roomvu-account

How to Automatically Import Google Reviews into Your roomvu Account | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Settings 

How to Automatically Import Google Reviews into Your roomvu Account 

How to Automatically Import Google Reviews into Your roomvu Account 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

Sharing client reviews on social media is an effective way to build trust and showcase your expertise. With Roomvu, you can easily import your Google Reviews and create posts to share them across your social platforms. Follow these simple steps to set up your roomvu account for automatic Google Reviews import: 

​ 

Step 1: Find Your Google Business Page 

Search Your Name on Google : Search your business name on Google to locate your Google Business page. 

Click on Reviews 

Click Share : Once you’ve found your business page, click on the “Share” button. 

Click "Copy Link" : In the share options, click on “Click to Copy Link” to copy the URL of your Google Business page. 

Step 2: Set Up Review Import in Roomvu 

Open Your Roomvu Dashboard : Log in to your Roomvu account and navigate to your dashboard. 

Click Settings : On the dashboard, find and click the “Settings” option. 

Click " Client Reviews (Testimonials) " : In the settings menu, select “Client Reviews (Testimonials)” to access the review import options. 

Click "Import Reviews" : Next, click on “Import Reviews” to start the process. 

Select "Google Business" : From the options provided, choose “Google Business” as the source of your reviews. 

Paste the Link and Submit : Paste the link you copied earlier from your Google Business page into the field provided and click “Submit.” 

Step 3: Review Import and Posting 

Wait for Import Confirmation : After submitting, a message will pop up saying "Success! Wait 5 minutes." Allow a few minutes for the reviews to be imported. 

Share on Social Media : Once the reviews are imported, you can start creating posts to share them on your social media platforms. 

By following these steps, you can ensure that your positive client feedback is regularly featured on your social media, helping to build your brand and attract new clients.

All Collections 

Features 

roomvu Listing Studio: The Fastest Way to Create Stunning Real Estate Listing Videos 

roomvu Listing Studio: The Fastest Way to Create Stunning Real Estate Listing Videos 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

In the world of real estate, time is of the essence. You need tools that make your listings stand out and save you time and effort. That’s where roomvu's Listing Studio comes in—our most user-friendly feature designed to help you create and share stunning listing videos in just a few clicks. 

Ready-Made Videos in Minutes 

With Listing Studio, you don’t need to be a tech expert or spend hours creating videos. We do the heavy lifting for you. Simply import your listing, and within minutes, you’ll have a professional-quality video ready to go. It’s as easy as uploading your property details and letting our system handle the rest. 

roomvu Automatically Imports Your Listings 

roomvu integrates with 50+ real estate boards , automatically importing listings for many regions. 

How to Import Your Listings 

If you don’t see your listing, here are three ways to import your property: 

1. Import Listings 

Getting started with Listing Studio is as simple as adding your property listings. All you need to do is enter the MLS ID of your listing in the designated section of your dashboard. 

Step 1 

Visit your dashboard and click " MLS Listings " from the left menu. 

​ 

Step 2 

On the top right corner click "Import Listings" 

Step 3 

Enter your listing's ID and click "Add," Listing Studio will automatically pull in all the relevant details and media associated with your property. This quick step ensures your listing is ready to be customized and transformed into a professional video. 

Step 4: Pick Your Preferred Layout 

Start by selecting the layout that best showcases your property. Whether you prefer a modern, clean look or something more traditional, Listing Studio offers a variety of layouts tailored to different styles. 

Step 5: Pick the Color Set for the Layout 

Customize the colors to match your branding. Choose from our predefined color sets that complement your selected layout, ensuring your video aligns perfectly with your brand identity. 

Step 6: Enhance the Photo with AI 

Take your listing visuals to the next level with our AI-enhanced photo editing. Our system will automatically redecorate your listing photos, offering a virtual staging experience in just one click. You can choose between different AI-generated options designed to make your property look its best. 

Step 7: Finalize and Share Your Video 

Once you’re happy with your layout, colors, and photos, your video is ready. Download it with one click and share it on your social media channels or send it directly to potential buyers. It’s that simple! 

2. Import Manually 

If you wish to manually enter the information for your listings: 

​ 

Step 1 

Visit your dashboard and click " MLS Listings " from the left menu. 

​ 

Step 2 

On the top right corner click "Import Listings" 

Step 3 

click "Add Manually" 

Step 4 

Add the listing details manually. 

Step 5 

Upload property images to complete the listing. The first one is the cover photo so make sure you choose a photo that best presents the home. 

3. Connect Roomvu to Your Brokerage 

We can work with your brokerage to import listings automatically . Once a contract is signed and data feeds are accessed, your listings will sync seamlessly. 

Auto Post Content: Set It and Forget It 

Once your video is ready, Listing Studio automatically posts it. Whether it’s an open house, a newly listed property, or a recently sold home, your content is posted across your social media channels with minimal effort on your part. Set it up once, and let us handle the rest. 

Why Choose Listing Studio? 

Super Easy to Use: Create and customize videos in just a few clicks. 

Save Time: Import listings, customize, and share in minutes. 

MLS Integration: Effortlessly import data with no manual entry. 

AI-Powered Enhancement: Elevate your photos with one-click virtual staging. 

Auto Post Content: Automatically share your videos across social media. 

Listing Studio is the ultimate tool for agents who want to maximize efficiency without sacrificing quality. It allows you to save time, boost your listings, and easily engage more buyers and sellers. Experience the simplicity and speed of Listing Studio today.

## Increase Post Engagement by 10x with Personalized Intro Videos | Roomvu Help Center

Increase Post Engagement by 10x with Personalized Intro Videos 

Increase Post Engagement by 10x with Personalized Intro Videos 

Learn about the key benefits, including the power of human connection, enhanced credibility, and delivering more valuable messaging. 

September 3, 2024 

Table of contents 

Increase Your Video Engagement by 10x with Personalized Intro Videos 

Capturing and holding your audience’s attention is crucial. Our latest feature, personalized intro videos, has proven to increase video engagement by up to 10x, according to our data. This significant boost comes from the powerful combination of human connection, credibility, and perceived value. When you start a video with a personal introduction, viewers are not only more likely to watch but also to engage with the content. The face behind the brand builds trust, and the tailored message sets the expectation for valuable content, all of which contribute to dramatically improved viewer retention and interaction. 

Why Intro Videos Get 10x Engagement 

Our data shows that users who utilize personalized intro videos experience a 10x increase in engagement compared to those who don’t. This dramatic boost can be attributed to several key factors. 

Post Engagement Snapshot for Videos with Intros - Data from a roomvu User Dashboard 

1. The Power of Human Connection 

At the heart of social media is the human connection. People are naturally drawn to faces and are more likely to engage with content that feels personal. When viewers see a face at the start of a video, it captures their attention and creates an immediate connection. They’re not just watching a video—they’re engaging with a person. This simple yet powerful dynamic can significantly increase viewer retention and overall engagement. 

2. Building Credibility and Trust 

In an age where authenticity is key, showing your face in your videos adds a layer of credibility that’s hard to achieve through text or imagery alone. When you introduce yourself and your content, it sends a message to your audience that there’s a real person behind the brand—someone they can trust. This personal approach not only makes your content more relatable but also strengthens your brand’s authenticity, encouraging viewers to invest their time in what you have to say. 

3. Delivering More Valuable Messaging 

A personalized introduction sets the stage for what’s to come. It signals to your audience that the content they are about to watch is tailored and valuable. Viewers are more likely to perceive the video as informative and worthwhile when they see a real person speaking directly to them. This expectation of value encourages them to watch the video in its entirety, leading to higher engagement rates and better overall performance on social media platforms. 

4. Effortless Yet Impactful 

While the idea of adding an intro video might sound time-consuming, we’ve designed this feature to be as user-friendly as possible. With minimal effort, you can create a significant impact on how your content is perceived. The ease of recording and attaching an intro video means you can consistently enhance your content without taking up much of your valuable time. This balance of effort and impact makes it an essential tool for any real estate agent looking to elevate their online presence. 

Why You Should Embrace This Feature 

Personalized intro videos are more than just a tool—they’re a strategic advantage. By incorporating your face and voice into your videos, you’re not only boosting engagement but also establishing a stronger connection with your audience. This feature empowers you to present your brand in a way that’s both professional and personable, setting you apart in a crowded digital marketplace. 

Impact of Intro Videos: Engagement Metrics from roomvu Users 

Investing a few extra seconds to introduce your videos could be the key to transforming your social media strategy. Don’t miss out on the opportunity to connect with your audience on a deeper level, build trust, and significantly enhance your engagement metrics. Start using personalized intro videos today, and watch as your content resonates more powerfully with your audience.

## How to Warm Up Your Email Address Before Cold Outreach | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/9827428-how-to-warm-up-your-email-address-before-cold-outreach

How to Warm Up Your Email Address Before Cold Outreach | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Your Dashboard 
English 
English 

Search for articles... 

All Collections 

Email Marketing 

How to Warm Up Your Email Address Before Cold Outreach 

How to Warm Up Your Email Address Before Cold Outreach 

Guide on warming up a new email to avoid spam filters by gradually increasing volume and optimizing sender details. 

September 5, 2024 

Table of contents 

We at roomvu always recommend agents use a separate email address for their business. However, it is very common for emails to end up in spam folders with a new SMTP server, IP, or domain. In fact, before sending email marketing campaigns, you need to warm up your email address to avoid ending up in the spam folder. This article will review a few steps you need to take to prevent that. 

Why Warmup Your Email Address 

A new account on social media takes time to be trusted by various platforms. New accounts on social media face different limitations in terms of exposure, reach, comments, etc. New email addresses with new IPs face the same limitation. When you use a new email address and a new IP address for your SMTP, your email address and IP will have no reputation on the internet, and the fact that it is new will put them under scrutiny by mail services. Internet service providers do not know this IP address. 

Therefore, you need to warm it before you can use it for email campaigns, or your emails will end up in the spam folders. This is essential when you are planning to run a massive cold email outreach with a new account to ensure emails land in the inbox. 

What is Warming up The Email Address 

When an IP finds emails from a new IP address and a new server, it will evaluate the traffic from that source. Email volume is one of the critical factors in determining spam mail. Email server warmup builds your mail server reputation on the internet with ISPs by gradually increasing the volume of mail sent with your IP address. Therefore, you must start low with the mail volume and gradually increase it to your desired scale. 

Email warm-up is how you build a good sender reputation and prepare a new email account for sending emails at scale. You do so by gradually increasing the emails you send from that account. 

woodpecker 

In this case, you will allow the ISPs to gradually analyze the traffic from your mail servers and adjust to it. This way, the ISPs will monitor how your recipients engage with your emails. Failing to do so will overwhelm the ISPs, and your emails will get flagged as spam. 

Warming up The Email Address 

Please note that the guidelines here are suggestions only, and the best practice for each sender should be different. Use the tips here to get an idea of what you actually should do. 

The idea behind warming up mail servers is to reach your maximum mail volume in 10 days to two weeks. For example, if you want to send 1000 emails daily, you should start from a low number of around 20 and increase the volume daily until you reach 1000 emails on the last day. 

Source 

If you want to send 10K emails, you start with the same low number but extend the time period up to 2 weeks. 

To reach more significant numbers like 50K, you should break it down into more steps, like 20K, 30K, 40K, and then 50 K. Never make big jumps, as this will trigger spam filters in ISPs. Take it easy, and you will be fine. 

Ideally, it takes 8-12 weeks to accomplish maximum deliverability. 

saleshandy 

Monitoring the Progress 

Although the guidelines in this article will help you, you should constantly monitor your progress. If you notice a jump in spam rate, etc., taking it a bit easy and letting it cool will lower volumes. 

The From Line and Signature 

To lower your chances of being flagged as spam, you need to work on your "from line" and signature to sound like an actual person, not a bot sending the emails. You have to make it right. If you take it for granted, you will risk your chances of a great reach. Do not use random names and fake identities. Use profile images, etc., to further boost your credibility. 

Related Articles 

How to Clean and Optimize Your CSV Contacts for Email Marketing Using ChatGPT

## How to Cancel or Manage Your Roomvu Subscription | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/9841338-how-to-cancel-or-manage-your-roomvu-subscription

How to Cancel or Manage Your Roomvu Subscription | Roomvu Help Center 

Skip to main content 

Your Dashboard

How to Cancel or Manage Your Roomvu Subscription 

How to Cancel or Manage Your Roomvu Subscription 

This article explains how to cancel or manage your Roomvu subscription by accessing Payment & Billing settings and using Stripe to cancel your plan or update payment details. 

March 30, 2026 

Table of contents 

If you need to cancel your Roomvu subscription or update your billing details, you can now do this directly from your account settings. The process is simple and handled securely through Stripe. 

This guide walks you through where to find the option and what happens next. 

How to Cancel Your Roomvu Subscription 

Step 1: Log in to your Roomvu account 

Sign in and stay on your main dashboard. 

Step 2: Open Settings 

Click the gear icon on the top right corner of the dashboard to enter Settings . 

Step 3: Go to Payment & Billing 

In the left menu, scroll down and click Payment & Billing . 

Step 4: Click Cancel / Manage Subscription 

Select Cancel / Manage Subscription . 

You will be redirected to Stripe , our secure payment provider. 

Step 5: Manage your subscription in Stripe 

Inside Stripe, you can: 

Cancel your subscription 

Update your payment method 

Review your billing details 

All changes are handled securely by Stripe. 

After You Cancel 

Once your subscription is cancelled: 

You will retain access until the end of your current billing period 

No further charges will be made after that period ends 

Need Help? 

If you have trouble accessing Stripe or have questions about your billing, our support team is always here to help guide you through the process.

## roomvu's Second Language Feature for Real Estate Videos | Roomvu Help Center

URL: https://help.roomvu.com/en/articles/9911297-roomvu-s-second-language-feature-for-real-estate-videos

Your Dashboard

All Collections 

Features 

roomvu's Second Language Feature for Real Estate Videos 

roomvu's Second Language Feature for Real Estate Videos 

Updated over 2 weeks ago 

Table of contents 

At roomvu, effective communication is the cornerstone of successful business. Many users come from diverse nationalities and speak multiple languages. On the other hand, many clients prefer to work with professionals who speak their native language. In fact, for many people, English isn't their primary means of communication—they rely on their own language to navigate important decisions. This is where roomvu's second language features comes into play. 

Recognizing the importance of effective communication, we’ve launched our Second Language feature for real estate videos. This innovative tool allows you to create and share content in over 20 languages, helping you connect with your audience in a way that truly resonates. Speaking your clients’ preferred language expands your reach and fosters stronger, more trusted relationships. 

Why Add a Second Language? 

Expand Your Reach : Tap into communities where English isn't the primary language. 

Build Stronger Connections : Clients are more likely to trust and engage with agents who speak their language. 

Stay Competitive : Differentiate yourself in the market by offering multilingual content. 

Stay tuned as we plan to extend this feature to story images, emails, and landing pages soon! 

How to Set Up Your Second Language 

Enhancing your content with a second language is simple. Just follow these steps: 

Click the "Gear" icon to enter settings. Then click " content calendar settings ". 

Find the "Second Language" option in the middle of the settings page. 

Choose your desired language from the drop-down menu. 

Save Your Changes 

Click on "Save Changes" to apply the new settings. 

After you set your second language, you'll have immediate access to the videos, but please note that it may take up to one hour for your calendar to update with the second language content. 

Finding and Sharing Your Second Language Videos 

With your second language set, a new section will be added to your real estate videos. Here's how to find them: 

Click on " Videos & News " from the main sidebar on the left side of your dashboard. 

Click the tab featuring your second language . 

Choose a video and start sharing it on your preferred platforms to engage with a broader audience. 

Tips for Maximizing the Second Language Feature 

Consistency is Key : Regularly share content in English and your second language to maintain engagement. 

Understand Your Audience : Tailor your content to address your multilingual clients' specific needs and interests. 

Leverage Social Media : Connect as many popular social media platforms as possible to share content within your target language community to amplify your reach.
